Unit 01: Kinematics (1D & 2D, Projectile Motion)

AP Physics 1 | Georgia Standards of Excellence College Board CED Topic: KIN-1 through KIN-5

PART A: CHAPTER BLUEPRINT & CONCEPTS

Sub-Chapter 1.1 вҖ” Position, Displacement, and Distance

Core Concepts:
  • Position (x): Location of an object relative to a chosen origin; vector quantity; SI unit: meters (m)
  • Displacement (О”x): Change in position; О”x = x_f вҲ’ x_i; vector (has direction)
  • Distance (d): Total path length traveled; scalar (always positive)
Mathematical Relationships: 
О”x = x_f вҲ’ x_i          [meters, m]
d = |ОЈ path segments|    [meters, m]
Key Distinctions:
  • A car driving 5 km north then 5 km south вҶ’ distance = 10 km, displacement = 0
  • Displacement can be negative; distance cannot
Variable Definitions:
SymbolQuantitySI Unit
xpositionm
x_iinitial positionm
x_ffinal positionm
О”xdisplacementm
ddistancem

Sub-Chapter 1.2 вҖ” Velocity and Speed

Core Concepts:
  • Average velocity: v_avg = О”x / О”t; vector
  • Average speed: s_avg = d / О”t; scalar
  • Instantaneous velocity: v = dx/dt (limit as О”t вҶ’ 0); slope of x-t graph
  • Instantaneous speed: magnitude of instantaneous velocity
Mathematical Relationships: 
v_avg = О”x / О”t = (x_f вҲ’ x_i) / (t_f вҲ’ t_i)     [m/s]
s_avg = total distance / total time                 [m/s]
v(t) = dx/dt    (calculus form)                     [m/s]
Graph Interpretation:
  • Slope of position-time (x-t) graph = instantaneous velocity
  • Flat line on x-t вҶ’ object at rest
  • Straight line on x-t вҶ’ constant velocity
  • Curved line on x-t вҶ’ changing velocity (acceleration present)

Sub-Chapter 1.3 вҖ” Acceleration

Core Concepts:
  • Average acceleration: a_avg = О”v / О”t; vector
  • Instantaneous acceleration: a = dv/dt = dВІx/dtВІ
  • Positive acceleration вү  speeding up (depends on direction of velocity)
  • Object slows down when velocity and acceleration have opposite signs
Mathematical Relationships: 
a_avg = О”v / О”t = (v_f вҲ’ v_i) / (t_f вҲ’ t_i)     [m/sВІ]
a(t) = dv/dt = dВІx/dtВІ    (calculus form)          [m/sВІ]
Graph Interpretation:
  • Slope of velocity-time (v-t) graph = instantaneous acceleration
  • Area under v-t graph = displacement
  • Flat line on v-t вҶ’ constant velocity (zero acceleration)
  • Straight line on v-t вҶ’ constant acceleration

Sub-Chapter 1.4 вҖ” Kinematic Equations (Constant Acceleration)

Core Concepts: The "Big Four" SUVAT equations вҖ” valid ONLY when acceleration is constant: 
(1)  v = vвӮҖ + at
(2)  x = xвӮҖ + vвӮҖt + ВҪatВІ
(3)  vВІ = vвӮҖВІ + 2a(О”x)
(4)  x = xвӮҖ + ВҪ(vвӮҖ + v)t
Variable Definitions:
SymbolQuantitySI Unit
xвӮҖinitial positionm
xfinal positionm
vвӮҖinitial velocitym/s
vfinal velocitym/s
aacceleration (constant)m/sВІ
ttime elapseds
Strategy for Problem Solving:
  1. Identify known and unknown variables
  2. Choose equation that contains the unknown and all knowns
  3. Solve algebraically before substituting numbers
  4. Check units throughout
Free Fall Special Case:
  • a = вҲ’g = вҲ’9.8 m/sВІ (taking up as positive)
  • g = 9.8 m/sВІ вүҲ 10 m/sВІ (approximate)
  • At peak of trajectory: v = 0 (but a вү  0!)

Sub-Chapter 1.5 вҖ” Two-Dimensional Kinematics & Projectile Motion

Core Concepts:
  • 2D motion is decomposed into independent x and y components
  • Projectile motion: horizontal (constant velocity) + vertical (free fall)
  • Launch angle Оё determines initial components
Mathematical Relationships: 
COMPONENT DECOMPOSITION:
  vвӮҖвӮ“ = vвӮҖ cos Оё          [m/s]
  vвӮҖбө§ = vвӮҖ sin Оё          [m/s]

HORIZONTAL (no acceleration):
  x = vвӮҖвӮ“ В· t             [m]
  vвӮ“ = vвӮҖвӮ“ = constant     [m/s]

VERTICAL (free fall):
  y = vвӮҖбө§t вҲ’ ВҪgtВІ         [m]
  vбө§ = vвӮҖбө§ вҲ’ gt           [m/s]
  vбө§ВІ = vвӮҖбө§ВІ вҲ’ 2g(О”y)    [m/s]ВІ

RANGE (level ground, launch from y=0):
  R = vвӮҖВІ sin(2Оё) / g     [m]

TIME OF FLIGHT (level ground):
  T = 2vвӮҖ sin Оё / g       [s]

MAX HEIGHT:
  H = vвӮҖВІ sinВІОё / (2g)   [m]

Diagram 1.4 вҖ” Mermaid Flowchart: Kinematic Problem Strategy

flowchart TD A[Start: Read Problem] --> B{Is acceleration constant?} B -->|Yes| C[Use SUVAT equations] B -->|No| D[Use calculus: v=вҲ«a dt, x=вҲ«v dt] C --> E{1D or 2D?} E -->|1D| F[List knowns: xвӮҖ,vвӮҖ,v,a,t\nPick equation with 1 unknown] E -->|2D| G[Decompose into x and y components\nSolve each independently] F --> H[Solve algebraically first\nThen substitute numbers] G --> H H --> I[Check units & sign conventions] I --> J[Answer]

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20 Questions)

Example 1.1 вҖ” Displacement vs. Distance

Type: Qualitative Reasoning Question: A jogger runs 400 m north, then 150 m south. Find (a) total distance and (b) displacement. Solution: 
(a) Distance = sum of all path lengths
    d = 400 m + 150 m = 550 m

(b) Displacement = final position вҲ’ initial position
    Take north as positive (+)
    О”x = (+400 m) + (вҲ’150 m) = +250 m (north)

Answer: distance = 550 m; displacement = 250 m north

Example 1.2 вҖ” Average Velocity Calculation

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A car travels from xвӮҒ = 10 m to xвӮӮ = 85 m in 5.0 s. What is the average velocity? Solution: 
v_avg = О”x / О”t
v_avg = (xвӮӮ вҲ’ xвӮҒ) / (tвӮӮ вҲ’ tвӮҒ)
v_avg = (85 m вҲ’ 10 m) / (5.0 s вҲ’ 0 s)
v_avg = 75 m / 5.0 s
v_avg = 15 m/s (in +x direction)

Example 1.3 вҖ” Kinematic Equation: Finding Final Velocity

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A car starts from rest and accelerates at 3.0 m/sВІ for 8.0 s. What is its final velocity? Solution: 
Known: vвӮҖ = 0, a = 3.0 m/sВІ, t = 8.0 s
Unknown: v

Use: v = vвӮҖ + at
     v = 0 + (3.0 m/sВІ)(8.0 s)
     v = 24 m/s

Example 1.4 вҖ” Stopping Distance

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A car moving at 30 m/s brakes with deceleration 6.0 m/sВІ. How far does it travel before stopping? Solution: 
Known: vвӮҖ = 30 m/s, v = 0, a = вҲ’6.0 m/sВІ
Unknown: О”x

Use: vВІ = vвӮҖВІ + 2aО”x
     0 = (30)ВІ + 2(вҲ’6.0)(О”x)
     0 = 900 вҲ’ 12О”x
     12О”x = 900
     О”x = 75 m

Example 1.5 вҖ” Time to Reach Maximum Height

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A ball is thrown upward at 20 m/s from ground level. Find (a) time to reach max height, (b) max height, (c) total air time. Solution: 
Take up as positive. a = вҲ’9.8 m/sВІ

(a) At max height, v = 0
    v = vвӮҖ + at
    0 = 20 + (вҲ’9.8)t
    t = 20/9.8 = 2.04 s

(b) H = vвӮҖt + ВҪatВІ
    H = 20(2.04) + ВҪ(вҲ’9.8)(2.04)ВІ
    H = 40.8 вҲ’ 20.4 = 20.4 m

    Check with: vВІ = vвӮҖВІ + 2aО”y
    0 = 400 + 2(вҲ’9.8)H
    H = 400/19.6 = 20.4 m вң“

(c) By symmetry: total time = 2 Г— t_up = 2 Г— 2.04 = 4.08 s

Example 1.6 вҖ” Graph Interpretation: Displacement from v-t

Type: Graph Interpretation Question: A v-t graph shows velocity constant at 4 m/s from t=0 to t=3 s, then linearly decreasing to 0 at t=5 s. Find total displacement. Solution: 
Displacement = area under v-t graph

Rectangle (0 to 3 s):
  AвӮҒ = base Г— height = 3 s Г— 4 m/s = 12 m

Triangle (3 to 5 s):
  AвӮӮ = ВҪ Г— base Г— height = ВҪ Г— 2 s Г— 4 m/s = 4 m

Total displacement = AвӮҒ + AвӮӮ = 12 + 4 = 16 m

Example 1.7 вҖ” Calculus: Velocity from Position Function

Type: Calculus Derivation Question: The position of a particle is given by x(t) = 3tВі вҲ’ 5tВІ + 2t вҲ’ 1 (meters). Find (a) velocity at t=2 s, (b) acceleration at t=2 s. Solution: 
(a) v(t) = dx/dt = d/dt[3tВі вҲ’ 5tВІ + 2t вҲ’ 1]
           = 9tВІ вҲ’ 10t + 2

    v(2) = 9(4) вҲ’ 10(2) + 2 = 36 вҲ’ 20 + 2 = 18 m/s

(b) a(t) = dv/dt = d/dt[9tВІ вҲ’ 10t + 2]
           = 18t вҲ’ 10

    a(2) = 18(2) вҲ’ 10 = 36 вҲ’ 10 = 26 m/sВІ

Example 1.8 вҖ” Calculus: Position from Acceleration

Type: Calculus Derivation Question: A particle starts at x=2 m with vвӮҖ=3 m/s and has acceleration a(t) = 6t m/sВІ. Find x(t). Solution: 
Step 1: Integrate acceleration to get velocity
  v(t) = вҲ«a dt = вҲ«6t dt = 3tВІ + CвӮҒ
  Apply initial condition: v(0) = 3 m/s
  3 = 3(0)ВІ + CвӮҒ  вҶ’  CвӮҒ = 3
  v(t) = 3tВІ + 3

Step 2: Integrate velocity to get position
  x(t) = вҲ«v dt = вҲ«(3tВІ + 3) dt = tВі + 3t + CвӮӮ
  Apply initial condition: x(0) = 2 m
  2 = 0 + 0 + CвӮӮ  вҶ’  CвӮӮ = 2
  x(t) = tВі + 3t + 2

Example 1.9 вҖ” Projectile: Range Calculation

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A ball is launched at 25 m/s at 35В° above horizontal from ground level. Find (a) horizontal range, (b) max height. (g = 9.8 m/sВІ) Solution: 
Step 1: Decompose initial velocity
  vвӮҖвӮ“ = 25 cos35В° = 25(0.819) = 20.5 m/s
  vвӮҖбө§ = 25 sin35В° = 25(0.574) = 14.3 m/s

(a) Time of flight:
    vбө§ = vвӮҖбө§ вҲ’ gt = 0 at peak
    t_peak = 14.3/9.8 = 1.46 s
    T_total = 2(1.46) = 2.92 s

    Range R = vвӮҖвӮ“ Г— T = 20.5 Г— 2.92 = 59.8 m

    Check with formula: R = vвӮҖВІsin(2Оё)/g
    R = (25)ВІsin(70В°)/9.8 = 625(0.940)/9.8 = 60.0 m вң“

(b) Max height:
    H = vвӮҖбө§ВІ/(2g) = (14.3)ВІ/(2Г—9.8) = 204.5/19.6 = 10.4 m

Example 1.10 вҖ” Projectile: Cliff Launch

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A projectile is launched horizontally at 15 m/s from a cliff 45 m high. Find (a) time to hit ground, (b) horizontal distance, (c) speed just before impact. Solution: 
Setup: vвӮҖвӮ“ = 15 m/s, vвӮҖбө§ = 0 (horizontal launch)
       yвӮҖ = 45 m, y = 0 (taking down as positive for convenience)

(a) Vertical: y = ВҪgtВІ
    45 = ВҪ(9.8)tВІ
    tВІ = 90/9.8 = 9.18
    t = 3.03 s

(b) Horizontal: x = vвӮҖвӮ“ В· t = 15 Г— 3.03 = 45.5 m

(c) At impact:
    vвӮ“ = 15 m/s (unchanged)
    vбө§ = gt = 9.8 Г— 3.03 = 29.7 m/s (downward)
    
    v = вҲҡ(vвӮ“ВІ + vбө§ВІ) = вҲҡ(225 + 882) = вҲҡ1107 = 33.3 m/s

Example 1.11 вҖ” Relative Motion

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Train A moves east at 60 m/s. Train B moves west at 40 m/s. They are 500 m apart. When do they meet? Solution: 
Take east as positive.
v_A = +60 m/s, v_B = вҲ’40 m/s

Relative velocity of approach = 60 + 40 = 100 m/s
(they move toward each other)

Time to meet: t = separation / relative speed
t = 500 m / 100 m/s = 5.0 s

Position of A: x_A = 60(5) = 300 m from A's start
Position of B: x_B = 500 вҲ’ 40(5) = 500 вҲ’ 200 = 300 m вң“

Example 1.12 вҖ” Acceleration from Graph

Type: Graph Interpretation Question: A v-t graph shows v = 2 m/s at t=1 s and v = 14 m/s at t=4 s. Find acceleration and displacement from t=1 to t=4 s. Solution: 
Acceleration = slope of v-t graph
a = О”v/О”t = (14 вҲ’ 2)/(4 вҲ’ 1) = 12/3 = 4 m/sВІ

Displacement = area under v-t graph (trapezoid):
О”x = ВҪ(vвӮҒ + vвӮӮ) Г— О”t = ВҪ(2 + 14) Г— 3 = ВҪ Г— 16 Г— 3 = 24 m

Verify with equation: О”x = vвӮҖt + ВҪatВІ
О”x = 2(3) + ВҪ(4)(9) = 6 + 18 = 24 m вң“

Example 1.13 вҖ” Two Objects Meeting

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Object A starts at x=0 and moves at constant 5 m/s. Object B starts at x=60 m and moves at вҲ’3 m/s (toward A). When and where do they meet? Solution: 
Position equations:
  x_A(t) = 0 + 5t = 5t
  x_B(t) = 60 + (вҲ’3)t = 60 вҲ’ 3t

Set equal to find meeting time:
  5t = 60 вҲ’ 3t
  8t = 60
  t = 7.5 s

Meeting position:
  x = 5(7.5) = 37.5 m from origin
  Check: x_B = 60 вҲ’ 3(7.5) = 60 вҲ’ 22.5 = 37.5 m вң“

Example 1.14 вҖ” Free Fall with Initial Downward Velocity

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: An object is thrown downward at 8 m/s from 50 m height. Find (a) time to hit ground, (b) impact speed. Solution: 
Take downward as positive. a = +9.8 m/sВІ, vвӮҖ = +8 m/s

(a) y = vвӮҖt + ВҪatВІ
    50 = 8t + ВҪ(9.8)tВІ
    4.9tВІ + 8t вҲ’ 50 = 0
    
    Quadratic formula: t = [вҲ’8 Вұ вҲҡ(64 + 4Г—4.9Г—50)] / (2Г—4.9)
    t = [вҲ’8 Вұ вҲҡ(64 + 980)] / 9.8
    t = [вҲ’8 Вұ вҲҡ1044] / 9.8
    t = [вҲ’8 Вұ 32.3] / 9.8
    
    Taking positive root: t = (вҲ’8 + 32.3)/9.8 = 24.3/9.8 = 2.48 s

(b) v = vвӮҖ + at = 8 + 9.8(2.48) = 8 + 24.3 = 32.3 m/s

Example 1.15 вҖ” Projectile: Angle for Maximum Range

Type: Qualitative Reasoning + Algebraic Question: Prove that maximum range occurs at Оё = 45В°. For vвӮҖ = 20 m/s, calculate range at 30В°, 45В°, and 60В°. Solution: 
Range formula: R = vвӮҖВІsin(2Оё)/g

For maximum R: sin(2Оё) must equal 1
sin(2Оё) = 1  вҶ’  2Оё = 90В°  вҶ’  Оё = 45В° вң“

Calculations (vвӮҖ=20, g=9.8):
  R_max = (20)ВІ/9.8 = 400/9.8 = 40.8 m (at Оё=45В°)

  Оё=30В°: R = (400)sin(60В°)/9.8 = 400(0.866)/9.8 = 35.3 m
  Оё=45В°: R = (400)sin(90В°)/9.8 = 400(1.00)/9.8 = 40.8 m вң“
  Оё=60В°: R = (400)sin(120В°)/9.8 = 400(0.866)/9.8 = 35.3 m

Note: 30В° and 60В° give same range (complementary angles property)

Example 1.16 вҖ” Non-Uniform Acceleration (AP-C Level)

Type: Calculus Derivation Question: A particle has acceleration a(t) = (4 вҲ’ 2t) m/sВІ. At t=0: vвӮҖ=0, xвӮҖ=
  1. Find: (a) when it stops, (b) max displacement.
Solution: 
(a) v(t) = вҲ«a dt = вҲ«(4 вҲ’ 2t) dt = 4t вҲ’ tВІ + C
    v(0) = 0  вҶ’  C = 0
    v(t) = 4t вҲ’ tВІ

    Stops when v = 0:
    4t вҲ’ tВІ = 0  вҶ’  t(4 вҲ’ t) = 0
    t = 0 (start) or t = 4 s

(b) x(t) = вҲ«v dt = вҲ«(4t вҲ’ tВІ) dt = 2tВІ вҲ’ tВі/3 + C
    x(0) = 0  вҶ’  C = 0
    x(t) = 2tВІ вҲ’ tВі/3

    Max displacement at t = 4 s:
    x(4) = 2(16) вҲ’ (64)/3 = 32 вҲ’ 21.3 = 10.7 m

Example 1.17 вҖ” Projectile: Hitting a Moving Target (FRQ Style)

Type: Algebraic Calculation (Multi-part) Question: A cannon fires at 50 m/s at 37В° above horizontal (sin37В°=0.6, cos37В°=0.8). A target is 120 m away horizontally at ground level. (a) Does the projectile hit the target? (b) If not, what angle is needed? Solution: 
(a) Check if range = 120 m
    R = vвӮҖВІsin(2Оё)/g = (2500)sin(74В°)/9.8
    R = 2500(0.961)/9.8 = 245 m вү  120 m
    Does NOT hit at 37В°.

(b) Need: R = 120 m
    120 = (2500)sin(2Оё)/9.8
    sin(2Оё) = 120(9.8)/2500 = 1176/2500 = 0.470
    2Оё = 28.0В° or 152В°
    Оё = 14.0В° or 76.0В°
    
    Two angles work (complementary angle property).
    Use Оё = 14.0В° for low trajectory or 76.0В° for high trajectory.

Example 1.18 вҖ” Instantaneous vs. Average Velocity

Type: Qualitative Reasoning Question: Position is x(t) = tВІ вҲ’ 4t + 3 (meters). (a) Find avg velocity 0вҶ’3 s. (b) Find instantaneous velocity at t=1, t=2, t=3 s. (c) When is the object momentarily at rest? Solution: 
(a) x(0) = 0 вҲ’ 0 + 3 = 3 m
    x(3) = 9 вҲ’ 12 + 3 = 0 m
    v_avg = (0 вҲ’ 3)/3 = вҲ’1 m/s

(b) v(t) = dx/dt = 2t вҲ’ 4
    v(1) = 2(1) вҲ’ 4 = вҲ’2 m/s
    v(2) = 2(2) вҲ’ 4 = 0 m/s
    v(3) = 2(3) вҲ’ 4 = +2 m/s

(c) At rest: v(t) = 0
    2t вҲ’ 4 = 0  вҶ’  t = 2 s
    Position: x(2) = 4 вҲ’ 8 + 3 = вҲ’1 m

Example 1.19 вҖ” Vector Addition of Velocities

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A boat heads east at 4 m/s. River current flows north at 3 m/s. Find (a) resultant velocity, (b) angle from east, (c) time to cross 80 m wide river. Solution: 
(a) v = вҲҡ(vвӮ“ВІ + vбө§ВІ) = вҲҡ(16 + 9) = вҲҡ25 = 5 m/s

(b) Оё = arctan(vбө§/vвӮ“) = arctan(3/4) = 36.9В° north of east

(c) To cross 80 m wide river (crossing in x-direction):
    Time depends only on component perpendicular to shore.
    
    If river flows north and boat heads east:
    The east component (4 m/s) carries boat across 80 m river
    t = 80/4 = 20 s
    
    Boat drifts north: d = vвӮҷ Г— t = 3 Г— 20 = 60 m downstream

Example 1.20 вҖ” AP FRQ: Complete Projectile Analysis

Type: Free Response Question (Multi-part) Question: A ball is launched from the edge of a table (height H = 1.2 m) with initial horizontal velocity vвӮҖ. It lands 2.4 m from the base of the table. (a) Find the time of flight. (b) Find vвӮҖ. (c) Find the velocity (magnitude and direction) just before impact. (d) Sketch the trajectory labeling key quantities. Solution: 
(a) Vertical drop: H = ВҪgtВІ
    1.2 = ВҪ(9.8)tВІ
    tВІ = 2.4/9.8 = 0.245
    t = 0.495 s вүҲ 0.50 s

(b) Horizontal: x = vвӮҖt
    2.4 = vвӮҖ(0.495)
    vвӮҖ = 2.4/0.495 = 4.85 m/s

(c) At impact:
    vвӮ“ = vвӮҖ = 4.85 m/s (unchanged)
    vбө§ = gt = 9.8(0.495) = 4.85 m/s (downward)
    
    |v| = вҲҡ(4.85ВІ + 4.85ВІ) = 4.85вҲҡ2 = 6.86 m/s
    Оё = arctan(vбө§/vвӮ“) = arctan(1) = 45В° below horizontal

(d) Sketch description:
    - Horizontal launch arrow vвӮҖ at table edge
    - Parabolic curve downward to landing point
    - Label: H = 1.2 m (vertical), R = 2.4 m (horizontal)
    - At impact: velocity vector at 45В° below horizontal

Free Response Questions (FRQ) 1вҖ“10

FRQ 1 вҖ” Experimental Design: Measuring g A student wants to measure g using a ball drop and stopwatch. (a) Describe the experimental setup. What measurements are taken? (b) Write the equation relating h, g, and t for a ball dropped from rest. (c) The student measures h=2.00 m and t=0.638 s. Calculate g. (d) Identify two sources of error and their effect on the measured g. (e) How could the student improve accuracy? Answer Key: 
(a) Drop ball from measured height h, measure time t to reach ground.
    Measurements: height with meter stick, time with stopwatch (or photogate).

(b) h = ВҪgtВІ  вҶ’  g = 2h/tВІ

(c) g = 2(2.00)/(0.638)ВІ = 4.00/0.407 = 9.83 m/sВІ

(d) Sources:
    - Human reaction time: makes t larger вҶ’ calculated g smaller than actual
    - Air resistance: makes t larger вҶ’ calculated g smaller than actual

(e) Use photogate timers for precise measurement; average many trials;
    use longer drop heights to reduce reaction time error percentage.
FRQ 2 вҖ” Kinematics Graph Analysis A particle moves along the x-axis. Its x-t graph shows:
  • Segment 1 (0вҶ’2 s): starts at x=0, curves up to x=8 m
  • Segment 2 (2вҶ’5 s): straight line from x=8 to x=вҲ’4 m
  • Segment 3 (5вҶ’7 s): horizontal line at x=вҲ’4 m
(a) During which segment is acceleration nonzero? (b) Find average velocity during Segment 2. (c) At what time is the object nearest to origin after t=2 s? (d) Sketch the corresponding v-t graph. Answer Key: 
(a) Segment 1 (curved x-t вҶ’ changing slope вҶ’ nonzero acceleration)

(b) v_avg = О”x/О”t = (вҲ’4 вҲ’ 8)/(5 вҲ’ 2) = вҲ’12/3 = вҲ’4 m/s

(c) During Segment 2: x crosses zero when
    x(t) = 8 + (вҲ’4)(t вҲ’ 2) = 8 вҲ’ 4t + 8 = 16 вҲ’ 4t = 0
    t = 4 s
    At t=5 s: x=вҲ’4 m, so nearest to origin at t=4 s (x=0)

(d) v-t sketch:
    Segment 1: positive, increasing from 0 (positive acceleration)
    Segment 2: constant вҲ’4 m/s (straight horizontal line at v=вҲ’4)
    Segment 3: v = 0 (horizontal line at v=0)
FRQ 3 вҖ” Projectile Motion: Complete Analysis A ball is kicked from ground level at vвӮҖ=18 m/s at 53В° above horizontal (sin53В°=0.80, cos53В°=0.60, g=10 m/sВІ). (a) Find initial velocity components. (b) Find maximum height. (c) Find total time of flight. (d) Find horizontal range. (e) Find velocity (magnitude and direction) at t=1.0 s. (f) At what two times is the ball at height 5 m? Answer Key: 
(a) vвӮҖвӮ“ = 18(0.60) = 10.8 m/s
    vвӮҖбө§ = 18(0.80) = 14.4 m/s

(b) H = vвӮҖбө§ВІ/2g = (14.4)ВІ/20 = 207.36/20 = 10.37 m

(c) T = 2vвӮҖбө§/g = 2(14.4)/10 = 2.88 s

(d) R = vвӮҖвӮ“ Г— T = 10.8 Г— 2.88 = 31.1 m

(e) At t=1.0 s:
    vвӮ“ = 10.8 m/s (constant)
    vбө§ = 14.4 вҲ’ 10(1.0) = 4.4 m/s (upward)
    |v| = вҲҡ(10.8ВІ + 4.4ВІ) = вҲҡ(116.6 + 19.4) = вҲҡ136 = 11.7 m/s
    Оё = arctan(4.4/10.8) = 22.2В° above horizontal

(f) 5 = 14.4t вҲ’ 5tВІ
    5tВІ вҲ’ 14.4t + 5 = 0
    t = [14.4 Вұ вҲҡ(207.4 вҲ’ 100)]/10 = [14.4 Вұ вҲҡ107.4]/10
    t = [14.4 Вұ 10.36]/10
    tвӮҒ = 0.404 s (going up)
    tвӮӮ = 2.48 s (coming down)
FRQ 4 вҖ” Relative Motion A passenger walks forward at 1.5 m/s relative to a train car. The train moves east at 25 m/s relative to the ground. A bird flies west at 10 m/s relative to ground. (a) Find passenger's velocity relative to ground. (b) Find passenger's velocity relative to the bird. (c) Find the train's velocity relative to the bird. (d) How long does it take the bird to fly 500 m relative to the ground? Answer Key: 
(a) v_passenger/ground = v_passenger/train + v_train/ground
    = +1.5 + 25 = 26.5 m/s east

(b) v_passenger/bird = v_passenger/ground вҲ’ v_bird/ground
    = 26.5 вҲ’ (вҲ’10) = 36.5 m/s east

(c) v_train/bird = 25 вҲ’ (вҲ’10) = 35 m/s east

(d) t = 500/10 = 50 s
FRQ 5 вҖ” Multi-Object Problem Object A: starts at x=0 with v=8 m/s, a=0. Object B: starts at x=вҲ’30 m with v=0, a=3 m/sВІ. (a) Write position equations for A and B. (b) Find when they are at the same position. (c) Find their velocities at that time. (d) Sketch x-t graph for both from t=0 to t=6 s. Answer Key: 
(a) x_A = 8t
    x_B = вҲ’30 + ВҪ(3)tВІ = вҲ’30 + 1.5tВІ

(b) Set equal: 8t = вҲ’30 + 1.5tВІ
    1.5tВІ вҲ’ 8t вҲ’ 30 = 0
    t = [8 Вұ вҲҡ(64 + 180)]/3 = [8 Вұ вҲҡ244]/3
    t = [8 Вұ 15.62]/3
    Take positive: t = (8 + 15.62)/3 = 7.87 s

(c) v_A = 8 m/s (constant)
    v_B = 3(7.87) = 23.6 m/s

(d) x_A: straight line from (0,0) to (6,48)
    x_B: parabola starting at (0,вҲ’30) curving upward
    They haven't met yet at t=6 s (meet at t=7.87 s)
FRQ 6 вҖ” Cliff Projectile Analysis A cliff is 60 m high. A ball is launched horizontally from the top. (a) Derive an expression for time to hit ground. (b) Derive an expression for horizontal range in terms of vвӮҖ and H. (c) If vвӮҖ=15 m/s, find range and impact speed. (g=9.8 m/sВІ) (d) What angle does velocity make with horizontal at impact? Answer Key: 
(a) H = ВҪgtВІ  вҶ’  t = вҲҡ(2H/g)

(b) R = vвӮҖt = vвӮҖвҲҡ(2H/g)

(c) t = вҲҡ(2Г—60/9.8) = вҲҡ12.24 = 3.50 s
    R = 15 Г— 3.50 = 52.5 m
    
    vвӮ“ = 15 m/s
    vбө§ = 9.8(3.50) = 34.3 m/s
    v = вҲҡ(15ВІ + 34.3ВІ) = вҲҡ(225 + 1176) = вҲҡ1401 = 37.4 m/s

(d) Оё = arctan(34.3/15) = arctan(2.29) = 66.4В° below horizontal
FRQ 7 вҖ” Non-Constant Acceleration A particle's velocity is v(t) = 6tВІ вҲ’ 4t + 2 m/s. At t=0, x=5 m. (a) Find acceleration at t=3 s. (b) Find position at t=2 s. (c) Find when acceleration equals zero. (d) Explain the physical significance of a=0 in terms of the v-t graph. Answer Key: 
(a) a(t) = dv/dt = 12t вҲ’ 4
    a(3) = 12(3) вҲ’ 4 = 36 вҲ’ 4 = 32 m/sВІ

(b) x(t) = xвӮҖ + вҲ«вӮҖбө— v dt = 5 + вҲ«вӮҖВІ (6tВІ вҲ’ 4t + 2) dt
    = 5 + [2tВі вҲ’ 2tВІ + 2t]вӮҖВІ
    = 5 + [16 вҲ’ 8 + 4 вҲ’ 0]
    = 5 + 12 = 17 m

(c) 12t вҲ’ 4 = 0  вҶ’  t = 1/3 s

(d) a=0 means the v-t graph has zero slope at that instant вҖ”
    it's a local minimum or maximum of velocity.
    At t=1/3 s, velocity = 6(1/9) вҲ’ 4(1/3) + 2 = 2/3 вҲ’ 4/3 + 2 = 4/3 m/s
    This is the minimum velocity of the particle.
FRQ 8 вҖ” Experimental: Measuring Projectile Range A student launches steel balls horizontally from a ramp at varying heights h above the launch point. The ball lands at horizontal distance d from the base of a table of height H. (a) What two measurements must be made for each trial? (b) Explain which variable determines time of flight. (c) Derive d as a function of vвӮҖ and H. (d) If H=0.80 m and the student measures d=1.20 m, find vвӮҖ. (e) The student graphs d vs vвӮҖ. What shape is expected and why? Answer Key: 
(a) Horizontal distance d from base of table, and launch speed vвӮҖ
    (measured using other kinematics or energy method)

(b) Table height H determines time of flight: t = вҲҡ(2H/g)
    (independent of vвӮҖ вҖ” vertical and horizontal motions independent)

(c) t = вҲҡ(2H/g)
    d = vвӮҖt = vвӮҖвҲҡ(2H/g)

(d) vвӮҖ = d/вҲҡ(2H/g) = 1.20/вҲҡ(1.60/9.8) = 1.20/вҲҡ0.163 = 1.20/0.404 = 2.97 m/s

(e) d = vвӮҖ Г— constant, so d vs vвӮҖ is a straight line through origin.
    Slope = вҲҡ(2H/g) = constant depending on table height.
FRQ 9 вҖ” Multi-part: Vertical Throw Analysis A ball is thrown upward at vвӮҖ=15 m/s from a building roof 30 m high. (g=9.8 m/sВІ) (a) Find max height above ground. (b) Find time to reach max height. (c) Find total time to hit ground. (d) Find speed when it passes the rooftop level on the way down. (e) Find speed at ground impact. Answer Key: 
(a) H_max = 30 + vвӮҖВІ/2g = 30 + (225/19.6) = 30 + 11.48 = 41.5 m

(b) t_peak = vвӮҖ/g = 15/9.8 = 1.53 s

(c) Total fall from peak to ground:
    h_total = 41.5 m from ground
    h = ВҪgtВІ вҶ’ t_fall = вҲҡ(2Г—41.5/9.8) = вҲҡ8.47 = 2.91 s
    Total time = t_up + t_fall = 1.53 + 2.91 = 4.44 s
    
    OR: вҲ’30 = 15t вҲ’ 4.9tВІ
    4.9tВІ вҲ’ 15t вҲ’ 30 = 0
    t = [15 Вұ вҲҡ(225 + 588)]/9.8 = [15 Вұ 28.5]/9.8
    t = 43.5/9.8 = 4.44 s вң“

(d) At roof level (y = 30 m, same height as launch):
    vВІ = vвӮҖВІ = 225 вҶ’ v = 15 m/s (downward by symmetry)

(e) v = вҲҡ(vвӮҖВІ + 2gГ—30) = вҲҡ(225 + 588) = вҲҡ813 = 28.5 m/s
FRQ 10 вҖ” Synthesis: Chase Problem A police car at rest begins pursuit when a speeder passes at 30 m/s. The police car accelerates at 4 m/sВІ. (a) Write equations for position of each vehicle. (b) How long until police car catches the speeder? (c) How far from the starting point? (d) What is the police car's speed when it catches the speeder? (e) At what time does the police car match the speeder's speed? Answer Key: 
(a) x_speeder = 30t
    x_police = ВҪ(4)tВІ = 2tВІ

(b) Set equal: 2tВІ = 30t
    2tВІ вҲ’ 30t = 0
    2t(t вҲ’ 15) = 0
    t = 0 (start) or t = 15 s

(c) x = 30(15) = 450 m

(d) v_police = at = 4(15) = 60 m/s

(e) Police matches speeder's speed when v_police = 30 m/s
    4t = 30  вҶ’  t = 7.5 s
    (At this point police is still behind; hasn't caught up yet)
    Position check: x_police(7.5) = 2(56.25) = 112.5 m
                    x_speeder(7.5) = 30(7.5) = 225 m вҶ’ 112.5 m behind

Unit 02: Force & Translational Dynamics

AP Physics 1 | Georgia Standards of Excellence College Board CED Topic: DYN-1 through DYN-5

PART A: CHAPTER BLUEPRINT & CONCEPTS

Sub-Chapter 2.1 вҖ” Forces and Newton's First Law

Core Concepts:
  • Force: A push or pull; vector quantity; causes acceleration
  • Net Force (ОЈF): Vector sum of all forces on an object
  • Newton's 1st Law (Law of Inertia): An object remains at rest or in constant velocity unless acted on by a net external force
  • Inertia: Resistance to change in motion; proportional to mass
  • Equilibrium: ОЈF = 0 (object at rest or constant velocity)
Mathematical Relationships: 
ОЈF = 0  вҶ’  equilibrium (v = constant or v = 0)
ОЈF вү  0  вҶ’  acceleration occurs
Variable Definitions:
SymbolQuantitySI Unit
FforceN (Newton = kgВ·m/sВІ)
ОЈFnet forceN
mmasskg
aaccelerationm/sВІ

Sub-Chapter 2.2 вҖ” Newton's Second Law

Core Concepts:
  • Newton's 2nd Law: Net force equals mass times acceleration
  • Applies to each direction independently
  • Heavier objects require more force for same acceleration
  • Direction of acceleration = direction of net force
Mathematical Relationships: 
ОЈF = ma           [Newtons, N]
ОЈFвӮ“ = maвӮ“        [x-component]
ОЈFбө§ = maбө§        [y-component]

Rearrangements:
  a = ОЈF/m        [m/sВІ]
  m = ОЈF/a        [kg]
Weight vs. Mass: 
Weight (W) = mg   [Newtons]
g = 9.8 m/sВІ (acceleration due to gravity near Earth's surface)
Mass: invariant (doesn't change with location)
Weight: varies with local g

Sub-Chapter 2.3 вҖ” Newton's Third Law

Core Concepts:
  • For every action force, there is an equal and opposite reaction force
  • Forces always come in pairs acting on DIFFERENT objects
  • Third-law pairs: same magnitude, opposite direction, same type of force
  • Third-law pairs NEVER cancel (they act on different objects)
Key Examples: 
Book on table:
  - Earth pulls book down (gravity)
  - Book pulls Earth up (reaction) вҶ’ 3rd Law pair
  
  - Table pushes book up (normal)
  - Book pushes table down (reaction) вҶ’ 3rd Law pair
  
Note: Weight and Normal are NOT 3rd Law pairs
      (they're both on the same object: the book)

Sub-Chapter 2.4 вҖ” Common Forces

Normal Force (N): 
Perpendicular to contact surface
Flat surface: N = mg (if no other vertical forces)
Inclined plane: N = mg cosОё
Pushed down with force F: N = mg + F sinОё
Pulled up at angle: N = mg вҲ’ F sinОё
Friction: 
Static friction: fвӮӣ вүӨ ОјвӮӣN  (prevents motion, up to max)
Kinetic friction: fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–N  (opposes sliding, constant)
Always: ОјвӮӣ > ОјвӮ–
Direction: always opposes relative motion or tendency of motion
Tension (T): 
Force in ropes, strings, cables
Massless rope: tension same throughout
Pulls in direction away from object
Spring Force (Hooke's Law): 
F_spring = вҲ’kx   [Newtons]
k = spring constant [N/m]
x = displacement from equilibrium [m]

Sub-Chapter 2.5 вҖ” Dynamics on Inclined Planes & Atwood Machines

Inclined Plane (angle Оё): 
Coordinate system: x along incline, y perpendicular

Forces:
  Weight component along incline: WвҲҘ = mg sinОё (down the incline)
  Weight component perpendicular: WвҠҘ = mg cosОё (into surface)
  Normal force: N = mg cosОё
  Kinetic friction: fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–N = ОјвӮ–mg cosОё (up the incline if sliding down)

Net force along incline (object sliding down):
  ОЈF = mg sinОё вҲ’ ОјвӮ–mg cosОё = ma
  a = g(sinОё вҲ’ ОјвӮ– cosОё)
Atwood Machine (two masses over frictionless pulley): 
mвӮҒ > mвӮӮ вҶ’ mвӮҒ accelerates down, mвӮӮ accelerates up

ОЈF system = (mвӮҒ вҲ’ mвӮӮ)g = (mвӮҒ + mвӮӮ)a
a = (mвӮҒ вҲ’ mвӮӮ)g / (mвӮҒ + mвӮӮ)
T = 2mвӮҒmвӮӮg / (mвӮҒ + mвӮӮ)

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20 Questions)

Example 2.1 вҖ” Finding Net Force

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Three forces act on a 5 kg box: 30 N east, 10 N west, 20 N north. Find (a) net force, (b) acceleration magnitude. Solution: 
(a) ОЈFвӮ“ = 30 вҲ’ 10 = 20 N east
    ОЈFбө§ = 20 N north
    ОЈF = вҲҡ(20ВІ + 20ВІ) = вҲҡ800 = 28.3 N at 45В° north of east

(b) a = ОЈF/m = 28.3/5 = 5.66 m/sВІ

Example 2.2 вҖ” Normal Force on Flat Surface

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 60 kg person stands in an elevator. Find normal force when elevator (a) at rest, (b) accelerating up at 2 m/sВІ, (c) accelerating down at 3 m/sВІ. Solution: 
(a) ОЈFбө§ = 0: N вҲ’ mg = 0 вҶ’ N = mg = 60(9.8) = 588 N

(b) ОЈFбө§ = maбө§ (up positive): N вҲ’ mg = ma
    N = m(g + a) = 60(9.8 + 2) = 60(11.8) = 708 N

(c) N вҲ’ mg = m(вҲ’a): N = m(g вҲ’ a) = 60(9.8 вҲ’ 3) = 60(6.8) = 408 N

Note: Feel heavier when accelerating up; lighter when accelerating down

Example 2.3 вҖ” Friction on Flat Surface

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 10 kg box (ОјвӮӣ=0.50, ОјвӮ–=0.35) is pushed with 40 N. Does it move? If so, find acceleration. Solution: 
Normal force: N = mg = 10(9.8) = 98 N
Max static friction: fвӮӣ_max = ОјвӮӣN = 0.50(98) = 49 N

Applied force = 40 N < fвӮӣ_max = 49 N
вҶ’ Box does NOT move (static friction = 40 N, no acceleration)

If pushed with 60 N (> 49 N):
Box moves. Kinetic friction: fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–N = 0.35(98) = 34.3 N
ОЈF = 60 вҲ’ 34.3 = 25.7 N
a = F/m = 25.7/10 = 2.57 m/sВІ

Example 2.4 вҖ” Inclined Plane: No Friction

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 5 kg block slides down a frictionless 30В° incline. Find acceleration and normal force. Solution: 
Coordinate system: x = down incline (+), y = вҠҘ to incline (+away from surface)

ОЈFбө§ = 0: N вҲ’ mg cos30В° = 0
  N = 5(9.8)(cos30В°) = 49(0.866) = 42.4 N

ОЈFвӮ“ = maвӮ“: mg sin30В° = ma
  a = g sin30В° = 9.8(0.5) = 4.9 m/sВІ (down the incline)

Example 2.5 вҖ” Inclined Plane with Friction

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: An 8 kg block on a 37В° incline has ОјвӮ– = 0.
  1. (sin37В°=0.6, cos37В°=0.8) Find acceleration when sliding down.
Solution: 
N = mg cos37В° = 8(9.8)(0.8) = 62.7 N
fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–N = 0.25(62.7) = 15.7 N (up the incline, opposing motion)
WвҲҘ = mg sin37В° = 8(9.8)(0.6) = 47.0 N (down the incline)

ОЈFвӮ“: mg sin37В° вҲ’ fвӮ– = ma
47.0 вҲ’ 15.7 = 8a
31.3 = 8a
a = 3.91 m/sВІ (down the incline)

Example 2.6 вҖ” Atwood Machine

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Two masses mвӮҒ=8 kg and mвӮӮ=3 kg hang over a frictionless pulley. Find acceleration and tension. Solution: 
a = (mвӮҒ вҲ’ mвӮӮ)g/(mвӮҒ + mвӮӮ) = (8вҲ’3)(9.8)/(8+3) = 5(9.8)/11 = 4.45 m/sВІ

T = 2mвӮҒmвӮӮg/(mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ) = 2(8)(3)(9.8)/11 = 470.4/11 = 42.8 N

Verify with individual equations:
  mвӮҒ: mвӮҒg вҲ’ T = mвӮҒa вҶ’ 78.4 вҲ’ T = 8(4.45) = 35.6 вҶ’ T = 42.8 N вң“
  mвӮӮ: T вҲ’ mвӮӮg = mвӮӮa вҶ’ T вҲ’ 29.4 = 3(4.45) = 13.4 вҶ’ T = 42.8 N вң“

Example 2.7 вҖ” Connected Objects (Horizontal)

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 3 kg box (A) is connected by string to a 5 kg box (B) on a frictionless surface. Force F=24 N pulls B. Find (a) acceleration of system, (b) tension in string. Solution: 
(a) Treat as system: ОЈF = (m_A + m_B)a
    24 = (3 + 5)a = 8a
    a = 3 m/sВІ

(b) Tension acts only on box A:
    T = m_A Г— a = 3 Г— 3 = 9 N

    Verify for B: F вҲ’ T = m_B Г— a
    24 вҲ’ 9 = 5(3) = 15 вң“

Example 2.8 вҖ” Static Equilibrium

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 5 kg sign is suspended from two wires making 30В° and 60В° with horizontal. Find tension in each wire. Solution: 
Weight: W = 5(9.8) = 49 N

Equilibrium conditions:
ОЈFвӮ“ = 0: TвӮӮcos60В° вҲ’ TвӮҒcos30В° = 0     вҶ’ TвӮӮ(0.5) = TвӮҒ(0.866)
ОЈFбө§ = 0: TвӮҒsin30В° + TвӮӮsin60В° = W     вҶ’ 0.5TвӮҒ + 0.866TвӮӮ = 49

From first equation: TвӮӮ = 1.732TвӮҒ
Substitute: 0.5TвӮҒ + 0.866(1.732TвӮҒ) = 49
            0.5TвӮҒ + 1.5TвӮҒ = 49
            2TвӮҒ = 49
            TвӮҒ = 24.5 N
            TвӮӮ = 1.732(24.5) = 42.4 N

Example 2.9 вҖ” Third Law Application

Type: Qualitative Reasoning Question: A horse pulls a cart with force F. The cart pulls back on the horse with equal force F (Newton's 3rd Law). So why does the cart accelerate? Solution: 
The 3rd law pair forces DO cancel in total вҖ” but they act on DIFFERENT objects:

  • Force from horse on cart вҶ’ accelerates the CART
  • Force from cart on horse вҶ’ this is just ONE force on the horse


The horse also has external friction from the ground (forward push).
Net force on horse = ground friction вҲ’ cart's pull on horse вү  0

Net force on CART = horse's pull on cart вҲ’ any friction on cart вү  0

Key insight: Newton's 3rd law pairs cannot cancel each other
because they act on different objects. Each object has its own FBD.

Example 2.10 вҖ” Finding Coefficient of Friction

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 20 kg block slides across a floor and decelerates from 8 m/s to rest in 4 m. Find (a) deceleration, (b) friction force, (c) coefficient of kinetic friction. Solution: 
(a) vВІ = vвӮҖВІ + 2aО”x
    0 = 64 + 2a(4)
    a = вҲ’8 m/sВІ (deceleration of 8 m/sВІ)

(b) fвӮ– = ma = 20(8) = 160 N

(c) N = mg = 20(9.8) = 196 N
    ОјвӮ– = fвӮ–/N = 160/196 = 0.816

Example 2.11 вҖ” Tension in Hanging System

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Three blocks hang vertically: A (2 kg) below B (3 kg) below C (4 kg) from a ceiling. Find tension in each rope segment. Solution: 
Rope below C holds A and B:
  TвӮҒ = (m_A + m_B)g = (2+3)(9.8) = 49 N

Rope below ceiling holds all three... wait, re-read:
  C hangs from ceiling, B hangs from C, A hangs from B

Rope 1 (A to B): TвӮҒ = m_A Г— g = 2(9.8) = 19.6 N
Rope 2 (B to C): TвӮӮ = (m_A + m_B)g = 5(9.8) = 49 N
Rope 3 (C to ceiling): TвӮғ = (m_A + m_B + m_C)g = 9(9.8) = 88.2 N

Example 2.12 вҖ” Apparent Weight in Circular Motion

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 70 kg person rides at top and bottom of a Ferris wheel (radius 10 m, speed 6 m/s). Find apparent weight at each position. (g=9.8 m/sВІ) Solution: 
Centripetal acceleration: aвӮ’ = vВІ/r = 36/10 = 3.6 m/sВІ

At TOP (centripetal direction = downward):
  mg вҲ’ N = maвӮ’
  N = m(g вҲ’ aвӮ’) = 70(9.8 вҲ’ 3.6) = 70(6.2) = 434 N

At BOTTOM (centripetal direction = upward):
  N вҲ’ mg = maвӮ’
  N = m(g + aвӮ’) = 70(9.8 + 3.6) = 70(13.4) = 938 N

Example 2.13 вҖ” Pulley with Friction

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Mass A (4 kg) sits on surface (ОјвӮ–=0.30) and is connected by rope over pulley to hanging mass B (3 kg). Find acceleration. Solution: 
N_A = m_A Г— g = 4(9.8) = 39.2 N
fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–N_A = 0.30(39.2) = 11.76 N

For system (B falls, A slides):
  Net force = m_B Г— g вҲ’ fвӮ– = 3(9.8) вҲ’ 11.76 = 29.4 вҲ’ 11.76 = 17.64 N
  Total mass = m_A + m_B = 7 kg
  a = 17.64/7 = 2.52 m/sВІ

Check with individual equations:
  B: m_B g вҲ’ T = m_B a вҶ’ 29.4 вҲ’ T = 3(2.52) = 7.56 вҶ’ T = 21.84 N
  A: T вҲ’ fвӮ– = m_A a вҶ’ 21.84 вҲ’ 11.76 = 10.08 = 4(2.52) вң“

Example 2.14 вҖ” Force at Angle

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 15 kg crate is pulled at 30В° above horizontal with 80 N. ОјвӮ–=0.
  1. Find acceleration.
Solution: 
Horizontal: FвӮ“ = 80 cos30В° = 80(0.866) = 69.3 N
Vertical: Fбө§ = 80 sin30В° = 80(0.5) = 40 N (upward)

Normal force (vertical equilibrium):
N + Fбө§ вҲ’ mg = 0
N = mg вҲ’ Fбө§ = 15(9.8) вҲ’ 40 = 147 вҲ’ 40 = 107 N

Kinetic friction: fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–N = 0.20(107) = 21.4 N

Newton's 2nd (horizontal): FвӮ“ вҲ’ fвӮ– = ma
69.3 вҲ’ 21.4 = 15a
47.9 = 15a
a = 3.19 m/sВІ

Example 2.15 вҖ” Minimum Force to Prevent Sliding

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 2 kg block sits on a 40В° incline. What minimum force parallel to incline (up) prevents sliding? (ОјвӮӣ=0.35) Solution: 
N = mg cos40В° = 2(9.8)(0.766) = 15.0 N
Max static friction: fвӮӣ = ОјвӮӣN = 0.35(15.0) = 5.25 N (up the incline)
Weight component: WвҲҘ = mg sin40В° = 2(9.8)(0.643) = 12.6 N (down)

At minimum force F (up incline) to prevent sliding down:
F + fвӮӣ = WвҲҘ (friction also acts up when trying to prevent sliding down)
F = WвҲҘ вҲ’ fвӮӣ = 12.6 вҲ’ 5.25 = 7.35 N

Example 2.16 вҖ” Newton's 3rd Law: Recoil

Type: Qualitative Reasoning + Calculation Question: A 75 kg person on ice skates pushes off a 100 kg wall. The wall pushes them back with 300 N for 0.5 s. Find (a) acceleration of person, (b) final velocity of person. Solution: 
(a) By Newton's 3rd Law, person experiences 300 N force.
    a = F/m = 300/75 = 4 m/sВІ

(b) v = vвӮҖ + at = 0 + 4(0.5) = 2 m/s (away from wall)

Note: Wall doesn't move (attached to Earth, effectively infinite mass)
      If wall were a free-standing block of 100 kg:
      a_wall = 300/100 = 3 m/sВІ (equal and opposite force)

Example 2.17 вҖ” Spring Force and Equilibrium

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A spring (k=200 N/m) is attached to ceiling. A 500 g mass hangs from it. (a) How far does spring stretch? (b) What additional mass makes it stretch 8 cm total? Solution: 
(a) At equilibrium: F_spring = weight
    kx = mg
    200x = 0.5(9.8) = 4.9 N
    x = 4.9/200 = 0.0245 m = 2.45 cm

(b) For total stretch x = 0.08 m:
    kx = Mg
    200(0.08) = Mg
    16 = Mg
    M = 16/9.8 = 1.633 kg
    Additional mass = 1.633 вҲ’ 0.5 = 1.133 kg

Example 2.18 вҖ” Two-Block Push

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Force F=30 N pushes two blocks (mвӮҒ=4 kg, mвӮӮ=6 kg) on frictionless floor. Find (a) acceleration, (b) contact force between blocks. Solution: 
(a) F = (mвӮҒ + mвӮӮ)a
    30 = (4+6)a = 10a
    a = 3 m/sВІ

(b) Contact force on mвӮӮ from mвӮҒ:
    F_contact = mвӮӮ Г— a = 6 Г— 3 = 18 N

    Check on mвӮҒ: F вҲ’ F_contact = mвӮҒ Г— a
    30 вҲ’ 18 = 12 = 4(3) вң“

Example 2.19 вҖ” Calculus: Variable Force

Type: Calculus Derivation (AP-C Level) Question: A force F(t) = (6t вҲ’ 4) N acts on a 2 kg object. At t=0, v=3 m/s. Find v(t) and v at t=3 s. Solution: 
F = ma вҶ’ a(t) = F(t)/m = (6tвҲ’4)/2 = 3t вҲ’ 2

v(t) = vвӮҖ + вҲ«вӮҖбө— a dt = 3 + вҲ«вӮҖбө— (3tвҲ’2) dt
     = 3 + [3tВІ/2 вҲ’ 2t]вӮҖбө—
     = 3 + 3tВІ/2 вҲ’ 2t
     = 3tВІ/2 вҲ’ 2t + 3

v(3) = 3(9)/2 вҲ’ 2(3) + 3 = 13.5 вҲ’ 6 + 3 = 10.5 m/s

Example 2.20 вҖ” AP FRQ: Inclined Plane System

Type: Free Response Question Question: Block A (m_A=3 kg) sits on a 30В° frictionless incline. It is connected by massless string over a frictionless pulley to hanging Block B (m_B=2 kg). (a) Draw FBDs for each block. (b) Determine which block accelerates down/up. (c) Find acceleration of system. (d) Find tension in string. (e) If ОјвӮ–=0.20 is added to incline, find new acceleration. Solution: 
(a) FBD Block A (on incline):
    - Weight mg_A down
    - Normal N perpendicular to incline  
    - Tension T up the incline
    
    FBD Block B (hanging):
    - Weight mg_B down
    - Tension T upward

(b) Compare forces:
    Tendency of A to slide down: m_A g sin30В° = 3(9.8)(0.5) = 14.7 N
    Weight of B: m_B g = 2(9.8) = 19.6 N
    B is heavier вҶ’ B descends, A moves UP the incline

(c) For B (down): m_B g вҲ’ T = m_B a
    For A (up incline): T вҲ’ m_A g sin30В° = m_A a
    
    Add: m_B g вҲ’ m_A g sin30В° = (m_A + m_B)a
    19.6 вҲ’ 14.7 = 5a
    4.9 = 5a
    a = 0.98 m/sВІ

(d) T = m_A(a + g sin30В°) = 3(0.98 + 4.9) = 3(5.88) = 17.6 N
    Check: T = m_B(g вҲ’ a) = 2(9.8 вҲ’ 0.98) = 2(8.82) = 17.6 N вң“

(e) With friction (A now moving UP, friction acts DOWN incline):
    N = m_A g cos30В° = 3(9.8)(0.866) = 25.5 N
    fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–N = 0.20(25.5) = 5.10 N (DOWN incline, opposing upward motion)
    
    m_B g вҲ’ T = m_B a
    T вҲ’ m_A g sin30В° вҲ’ fвӮ– = m_A a
    
    Add: m_B g вҲ’ m_A g sin30В° вҲ’ fвӮ– = (m_A + m_B)a
    19.6 вҲ’ 14.7 вҲ’ 5.10 = 5a
    вҲ’0.2 = 5a
    a = вҲ’0.04 m/sВІ 
    
    Negative means our assumed direction was wrong вҖ” 
    actually A slides DOWN and B goes UP, OR system is in static equilibrium.
    Check static: net tendency = вҲ’0.2 N вҶ’ static friction can hold this вҶ’ EQUILIBRIUM

Free Response Questions (FRQ) 1вҖ“10

FRQ 1 вҖ” Experimental Design: Measuring Friction A student places a block on an inclined board and measures the angle at which it just starts to slide. (a) What angle measurement gives ОјвӮӣ? Derive the relationship. (b) If critical angle = 32В°, calculate ОјвӮӣ. (c) The student tilts faster and measures sliding angle = 28В°. Calculate ОјвӮ–. (d) Explain why ОјвӮӣ > ОјвӮ– conceptually. Answer: 
(a) At critical angle: mg sinОё = ОјвӮӣ mg cosОё вҶ’ ОјвӮӣ = tanОё
(b) ОјвӮӣ = tan32В° = 0.625
(c) ОјвӮ– = tan28В° = 0.532
(d) Static friction must be broken (molecular bonds stronger when stationary);
    kinetic friction: sliding surfaces have less contact time вҶ’ lower coefficient
FRQ 2 вҖ” Inclined Plane with Connected Mass Block A (5 kg) on 37В° incline (ОјвӮ–=0.20) connects via string over pulley to hanging Block B. (a) Find minimum mass of B to start A moving UP the incline. (b) If m_B = 4 kg, find acceleration direction and magnitude. (c) Find tension in string for part (b). Answer: 
(a) For A to just start moving up:
    T = m_A g sin37В° + ОјвӮӣ m_A g cos37В°
    For minimum: T = m_B g
    m_B g = 5(9.8)(0.6) + 0.20(5)(9.8)(0.8) = 29.4 + 7.84 = 37.24 N
    m_B = 3.80 kg

(b) With m_B=4: 
    Tendency force of B down = 4(9.8)=39.2 N
    Resistance of A = 29.4+7.84=37.24 N (sin+kinetic friction)
    Net = 39.2вҲ’37.24 = 1.96 N вҶ’ A moves UP
    a = 1.96/(5+4) = 0.218 m/sВІ

(c) T = m_B(gвҲ’a) = 4(9.8вҲ’0.218) = 38.3 N
FRQ 3 вҖ” Newton's Laws: Acceleration Analysis A 10 kg sled is pulled by rope at 25В° above horizontal with force 60 N on a surface with ОјвӮ–=0.15. (a) Draw complete FBD. (b) Calculate normal force. (c) Calculate kinetic friction. (d) Calculate acceleration. (e) If rope is cut, calculate deceleration due to friction. Answer: 
(a) FBD: Weight mg down, Normal N up, Applied F at 25В° above horizontal, Friction fвӮ– backward

(b) N = mg вҲ’ F sin25В° = 10(9.8) вҲ’ 60(0.423) = 98 вҲ’ 25.4 = 72.6 N

(c) fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–N = 0.15(72.6) = 10.9 N

(d) ОЈFвӮ“ = F cos25В° вҲ’ fвӮ– = 60(0.906) вҲ’ 10.9 = 54.4 вҲ’ 10.9 = 43.5 N
    a = 43.5/10 = 4.35 m/sВІ

(e) After rope cut: fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–mg = 0.15(10)(9.8) = 14.7 N (larger, full weight now)
    a = вҲ’fвӮ–/m = вҲ’14.7/10 = вҲ’1.47 m/sВІ
FRQ 4 вҖ” Elevator Problem A person (mass 65 kg) stands on a scale in an elevator. (a) Scale reading at rest. (b) Scale reading: accelerating up at 1.5 m/sВІ. (c) Scale reading: accelerating down at 2.0 m/sВІ. (d) Velocity at which person feels 80% of normal weight. (e) At what acceleration does the person feel "weightless"? Answer: 
(a) N = mg = 65(9.8) = 637 N
(b) N = m(g+a) = 65(11.3) = 734.5 N
(c) N = m(gвҲ’a) = 65(7.8) = 507 N
(d) 0.80 Г— 637 = 509.6 N = m(gвҲ’a) вҶ’ a = 9.8вҲ’509.6/65 = 1.96 m/sВІ downward
    (The velocity doesn't matter; only acceleration affects scale reading)
(e) N=0: m(gвҲ’a)=0 вҶ’ a=g=9.8 m/sВІ downward (free fall)
FRQ 5 вҖ” Multi-Block System Three blocks on frictionless table: A (2 kg), B (3 kg), C (5 kg) in line, pushed by F=30 N. (a) System acceleration. (b) Force between A and B. (c) Force between B and C. (d) Redesign: F pushes from C's side. Do answers change? Explain. Answer: 
(a) a = F/total mass = 30/10 = 3 m/sВІ

(b) F pushes A. Force on B from A = mass of (B+C) Г— a = 8 Г— 3 = 24 N

(c) Force on C from B = mass of C Г— a = 5 Г— 3 = 15 N

(d) Same acceleration (system unchanged).
    Force between B and C: now force on A+B from C = 5Г—3=15 N... 
    Actually: F_AC = (m_A+m_B) Г— a = 5Г—3=15 N
    Force between A and B: F_AB = m_A Г— a = 2Г—3 = 6 N
    The contact forces are different! Largest contact force is always at the pushed end.
FRQ 6 вҖ” Modified Atwood with Friction Mass A (6 kg) on rough surface (ОјвӮ–=0.3) connected to hanging Mass B (4 kg). (a) Find acceleration if B descends. (b) Find tension. (c) Find minimum mass of B to start motion (ОјвӮӣ=0.4). (d) If system starts from rest, find speed after 2 m descent. Answer: 
(a) N = m_A g = 6(9.8) = 58.8 N; fвӮ– = 0.3(58.8) = 17.64 N
    Net force = m_B g вҲ’ fвӮ– = 4(9.8) вҲ’ 17.64 = 39.2 вҲ’ 17.64 = 21.56 N
    a = 21.56/(6+4) = 2.156 m/sВІ

(b) T = m_A(a+ОјвӮ–g) = 6(2.156+2.94) = 6(5.096) = 30.6 N
    Check: T = m_B(gвҲ’a) = 4(9.8вҲ’2.156) = 4(7.64) = 30.6 N вң“

(c) m_B g = ОјвӮӣ m_A g вҶ’ m_B = ОјвӮӣ m_A = 0.4(6) = 2.4 kg

(d) vВІ = 2ad = 2(2.156)(2) = 8.624 вҶ’ v = 2.94 m/s
FRQ 7 вҖ” Friction Investigation A student slides blocks of different masses across a surface, measuring acceleration with different forces.
Mass (kg)Applied Force (N)Acceleration (m/sВІ)
2103.0
2155.5
4100.5
4203.0
(a) Find ОјвӮ– from the 2 kg trials. (b) Find ОјвӮ– from the 4 kg trials. (c) Are they consistent? What does this tell you about friction? (d) Predict acceleration for 3 kg block with 18 N applied force. Answer: 
(a) From 2 kg, F=10 N, a=3 m/sВІ:
    fвӮ– = F вҲ’ ma = 10 вҲ’ 2(3) = 4 N
    ОјвӮ– = fвӮ–/(mg) = 4/(2Г—9.8) = 0.204
    
    From 2 kg, F=15 N, a=5.5 m/sВІ:
    fвӮ– = 15 вҲ’ 2(5.5) = 4 N вҶ’ ОјвӮ– = 0.204 вң“

(b) From 4 kg, F=10 N, a=0.5 m/sВІ:
    fвӮ– = 10 вҲ’ 4(0.5) = 8 N
    ОјвӮ– = 8/(4Г—9.8) = 0.204

(c) Consistent! ОјвӮ– вүҲ 0.204 regardless of mass or force.
    This confirms friction depends on Ој and N only, not area or applied force.

(d) fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–mg = 0.204(3)(9.8) = 5.99 N
    a = (FвҲ’fвӮ–)/m = (18вҲ’5.99)/3 = 12.01/3 = 4.0 m/sВІ
FRQ 8 вҖ” Qualitative Dynamics Reasoning A book (B) sits on top of a table (T) which sits on the floor (F). (a) Identify all Newton's 3rd Law pairs. (b) What forces act on the table? (c) The table is accelerated upward at 2 m/sВІ. How do forces on the book change? (d) At what acceleration would the book and table separate? Answer: 
(a) 3rd Law pairs:
    - Earth pulls book down вҶ” Book pulls Earth up (gravitational)
    - Table pushes book up вҶ” Book pushes table down (normal contact)
    - Earth pulls table down вҶ” Table pulls Earth up (gravitational)
    - Floor pushes table up вҶ” Table pushes floor down (normal contact)

(b) Forces on table:
    - Weight of table (mg_T) down
    - Normal from floor (N_floor) up
    - Weight of book pressing down (reaction to table's normal on book)

(c) Book accelerates up at 2 m/sВІ:
    N_table_on_book = m_book(g+a) = m_book(11.8 m/sВІ) > m_book(g)
    Normal force on book INCREASES.

(d) Book separates when N = 0:
    m_book(g+a) = 0 вҶ’ impossible for upward acceleration.
    Separation if table accelerates DOWNWARD faster than g:
    a_down > g вҶ’ free fall or beyond
FRQ 9 вҖ” Variable Mass System A rocket of initial mass MвӮҖ = 500 kg burns fuel at rate б№Ғ = 5 kg/s producing thrust F_thrust = 8000 N. (AP-C level) (a) Initial acceleration of rocket. (b) Mass after 30 s. (c) Acceleration after 30 s. (d) Write equation for acceleration as function of time. Answer: 
(a) Net force = Thrust вҲ’ Weight = 8000 вҲ’ 500(9.8) = 8000 вҲ’ 4900 = 3100 N
    aвӮҖ = F/MвӮҖ = 3100/500 = 6.2 m/sВІ

(b) M(30) = 500 вҲ’ 5(30) = 500 вҲ’ 150 = 350 kg

(c) Net force = 8000 вҲ’ 350(9.8) = 8000 вҲ’ 3430 = 4570 N
    a(30) = 4570/350 = 13.1 m/sВІ

(d) M(t) = 500 вҲ’ 5t
    a(t) = [8000 вҲ’ (500вҲ’5t)(9.8)] / (500вҲ’5t)
    a(t) = 8000/(500вҲ’5t) вҲ’ 9.8
FRQ 10 вҖ” Synthesis: Two-Object System with Friction Block P (3 kg) sits on top of Block Q (5 kg) on a smooth floor. Between P and Q: ОјвӮӣ=0.4, ОјвӮ–=0.3. (a) Find max force F (applied to Q) so P doesn't slip on Q. (b) If F=40 N, find acceleration of each block. (c) Find friction force on P from Q when F=40 N. (d) Find friction force on Q from P when F=40 N. Answer: 
(a) Max friction on P from Q: fвӮӣ_max = ОјвӮӣ m_P g = 0.4(3)(9.8) = 11.76 N
    Max acceleration of P: a_max = fвӮӣ_max/m_P = 11.76/3 = 3.92 m/sВІ
    For system to move together: a = F/(m_P+m_Q) вүӨ 3.92 m/sВІ
    F_max = 3.92 Г— 8 = 31.4 N

(b) F=40 N > 31.4 N вҶ’ blocks slip.
    Friction between P and Q = ОјвӮ– m_P g = 0.3(3)(9.8) = 8.82 N
    
    P: fвӮ– = m_P a_P вҶ’ a_P = 8.82/3 = 2.94 m/sВІ
    Q: F вҲ’ fвӮ– = m_Q a_Q вҶ’ a_Q = (40вҲ’8.82)/5 = 31.18/5 = 6.24 m/sВІ

(c) Friction on P from Q = 8.82 N forward (kinetic, Q slides forward relative to P)

(d) By Newton's 3rd Law: friction on Q from P = 8.82 N backward
    (P slides backward relative to Q, so P's friction on Q is backward)

Unit 03  В·  AP1
Work, Energy & Power
Conservation Laws В· KE В· PE В· Power
W = Fd cosОёKE = ВҪmvВІPE = mghPE = ВҪkxВІP = Fv

Unit 03: Work, Energy, and Power

AP Physics 1 | Georgia Standards of Excellence

PART A: CHAPTER BLUEPRINT & CONCEPTS

Sub-Chapter 3.1 вҖ” Work

Mathematical Relationships: 
W = FВ·dВ·cosОё          [Joules, J = NВ·m]
W = О”KE               (Work-Energy Theorem)
W_net = О”KE = ВҪmvВІ вҲ’ ВҪmvвӮҖВІ

Variable Definitions:
  W = work done [J]
  F = applied force [N]
  d = displacement magnitude [m]
  Оё = angle between F and displacement
  
Calculus form: W = вҲ«FВ·dx
Key Rules:
  • Force perpendicular to displacement вҶ’ W = 0
  • Work can be negative (force opposes motion)
  • Only the component of force along displacement does work

Sub-Chapter 3.2 вҖ” Kinetic and Potential Energy

Kinetic Energy:    KE = ВҪmvВІ                  [J]
Gravitational PE:  PE_grav = mgh               [J]
Spring PE:         PE_spring = ВҪkxВІ            [J]
Total Mechanical:  E_mech = KE + PE            [J]

Conservation of Energy (no friction):
  KE_i + PE_i = KE_f + PE_f
  ВҪmvвӮҖВІ + mghвӮҖ = ВҪmvВІ + mgh

With non-conservative forces (friction):
  W_nc = О”E_mech = (KE_f + PE_f) вҲ’ (KE_i + PE_i)
  W_friction = вҲ’fвӮ–d  (always negative)

Sub-Chapter 3.3 вҖ” Power

Average Power:        P_avg = W/О”t = О”E/О”t     [Watts, W = J/s]
Instantaneous Power:  P = FvВ·cosОё              [W]
Power from velocity:  P = Fv  (when F вҲҘ v)     [W]

1 horsepower = 746 W
1 kWh = 3.6 Г— 10вҒ¶ J

Sub-Chapter 3.4 вҖ” Energy Conservation & LOL Diagrams

LOL (Energy Bar Chart) Method: 
L (initial) | O (transfer) | L (final)

Example: Ball falling off cliff (no air resistance)
Initial: [====] KE  [========] PE_grav  [ ] PE_spring
Transfer: None (conservative)
Final:   [============] KE  [  ] PE_grav  [ ] PE_spring

All PE converts to KE: mgh = ВҪmvВІ

Sub-Chapter 3.5 вҖ” Non-Conservative Forces

Friction does negative work: W_f = вҲ’ОјвӮ–mgd

Energy dissipated by friction = fвӮ– Г— d = ОјвӮ–mgd

Work done by all forces = О”KE (Work-Energy Theorem)
W_applied + W_friction + W_gravity = О”KE

PART B: DIAGRAM SYSTEM

Diagram 3.1 вҖ” Energy Conservation: Roller Coaster

    hвӮҒ                    hвӮғ
    в—Ҹ                     в—Ҹ
   / \                   / \
  /   \    hвӮӮ           /   \
 /     \   в—Ҹ           /     \
/       \ / \         /
          в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

At hвӮҒ: E = mghвӮҒ (all PE, v=0)
At hвӮӮ: E = mghвӮӮ + ВҪmvвӮӮВІ (mixed)
At ground: E = ВҪmv_maxВІ (all KE)

hвӮҒ must be highest for roller coaster to complete!
Energy: EвӮҒ = EвӮӮ = EвӮғ (no friction)

     xвӮҒ             xвӮӮ

Variable force: W = area under F(x) vs x curve = вҲ«F dx

Diagram 3.3 вҖ” Mermaid: Energy Problem Strategy

flowchart TD A[Identify System & Surroundings] --> B{Non-conservative forces?} B -->|No friction| C[Apply Conservation of ME\nKEбөў + PEбөў = KEf + PEf] B -->|Friction present| D[Include W_friction\nKEбөў + PEбөў + W_nc = KEf + PEf] C --> E[Substitute knowns\nSolve for unknown] D --> E E --> F[Check: Is energy lost?\nО”E = W_friction = fвӮ–d] F --> G[Answer with units]

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20 Questions)

Example 3.1 вҖ” Work by a Constant Force

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 50 N force at 37В° above horizontal pushes a box 8 m. Find work done. Solution: 
W = Fd cosОё = 50(8)(cos37В°) = 50(8)(0.8) = 320 J

Example 3.2 вҖ” Work-Energy Theorem

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 4 kg box starts at rest. Net force 20 N acts over 5 m. Find final speed. Solution: 
W_net = FВ·d = 20(5) = 100 J
W_net = О”KE = ВҪmvВІ вҲ’ 0
100 = ВҪ(4)vВІ
vВІ = 50
v = 7.07 m/s

Example 3.3 вҖ” Energy Conservation: Falling

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Ball dropped from 20 m. Find speed at 5 m above ground. Solution: 
E conserved: mghвӮҒ = mghвӮӮ + ВҪmvВІ
g(20) = g(5) + ВҪvВІ
9.8(15) = ВҪvВІ
vВІ = 294
v = 17.1 m/s

Example 3.4 вҖ” Spring Energy

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Spring (k=500 N/m) compressed 0.2 m launches 0.5 kg ball horizontally. Find launch speed. Solution: 
PE_spring = ВҪkxВІ = ВҪ(500)(0.04) = 10 J
ВҪmvВІ = 10
vВІ = 40
v = 6.32 m/s

Example 3.5 вҖ” Power Calculation

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 70 kg person climbs 20 m stairs in 30 s. Find average power output. Solution: 
W = mgh = 70(9.8)(20) = 13720 J
P = W/t = 13720/30 = 457 W (about 0.61 hp)

Example 3.6 вҖ” Friction and Energy Loss

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 3 kg block slides 4 m down a 30В° incline with ОјвӮ–=0.
  1. Find (a) work by gravity, (b) work by friction, (c) final KE if starting from rest.
Solution: 
Height fallen: h = 4 sin30В° = 2 m
(a) W_gravity = mgh = 3(9.8)(2) = 58.8 J

(b) N = mg cos30В° = 3(9.8)(0.866) = 25.5 N
    fвӮ– = ОјвӮ–N = 0.20(25.5) = 5.1 N
    W_friction = вҲ’fвӮ–d = вҲ’5.1(4) = вҲ’20.4 J

(c) KE_f = W_net = W_gravity + W_friction = 58.8 вҲ’ 20.4 = 38.4 J
    Check: ВҪmvВІ = 38.4 вҶ’ v = вҲҡ(25.6) = 5.06 m/s

Example 3.7 вҖ” Energy at Multiple Points

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 2 kg ball is thrown upward at 15 m/s from ground. Find KE and PE at h=5 m. (No friction) Solution: 
Initial KE = ВҪ(2)(225) = 225 J
Initial PE = 0

At h=5 m (conservation):
PE = mgh = 2(9.8)(5) = 98 J
KE = 225 вҲ’ 98 = 127 J
v = вҲҡ(2Г—127/2) = вҲҡ127 = 11.3 m/s

Example 3.8 вҖ” Power from Force and Velocity

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A car engine applies 3000 N at 25 m/s. What is the power output in watts and horsepower? Solution: 
P = Fv = 3000 Г— 25 = 75,000 W = 75 kW
hp = 75000/746 = 100.5 hp

Example 3.9 вҖ” Variable Force Work (AP-C)

Type: Calculus Derivation Question: F(x) = (3xВІ + 2x) N. Find work from x=0 to x=3 m. Solution: 
W = вҲ«вӮҖВі (3xВІ + 2x) dx = [xВі + xВІ]вӮҖВі = (27 + 9) вҲ’ 0 = 36 J

Example 3.10 вҖ” Conservation with Spring

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 1 kg block compresses spring (k=800 N/m) by 0.15 m. Spring releases block on frictionless floor. Find max speed. Solution: 
ВҪkxВІ = ВҪmvВІ
ВҪ(800)(0.0225) = ВҪ(1)vВІ
9 = ВҪvВІ
v = вҲҡ18 = 4.24 m/s

Example 3.11 вҖ” Roller Coaster Loop

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A car at top of 40 m high hill enters a loop of radius 12 m. What is minimum speed at loop top? Height of loop top = 24 m. Solution: 
At loop top: minimum speed when N=0 вҶ’ v_top = вҲҡ(gr) = вҲҡ(9.8Г—12) = 10.8 m/s

Energy conservation (hill top to loop top):
ВҪmvвӮҖВІ + mghвӮҒ = ВҪmv_topВІ + mghвӮӮ
vвӮҖВІ + 2g(hвӮҒ) = v_topВІ + 2g(hвӮӮ)
vвӮҖВІ = v_topВІ + 2g(hвӮӮ вҲ’ hвӮҒ) = 116.6 + 2(9.8)(24вҲ’40) = 116.6 вҲ’ 313.6 вҶ’ negative
This means: need only enough speed at hill top to maintain contact at loop.
vвӮҖ_min at hill top: ВҪmvвӮҖВІ + mg(40) = ВҪm(gr) + mg(24)
vвӮҖВІ = gr + 2g(24вҲ’40) = gr вҲ’ 32g = g(rвҲ’32) = 9.8(12вҲ’32) < 0
вҶ’ Starting height of 40 m is more than sufficient.

Example 3.12 вҖ” Hooke's Law & Energy

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Two identical springs (k=300 N/m each). (a) What is total PE if both compressed 0.1 m? (b) If in parallel (same compression)? Solution: 
(a) Each: PE = ВҪ(300)(0.01) = 1.5 J. Total = 3 J
(b) Parallel springs: k_eff = 600 N/m, x = 0.1 m
    PE = ВҪ(600)(0.01) = 3 J (same!)
    
    If in series: k_eff = 150 N/m, same force F=kx shared

Example 3.13 вҖ” Energy Lost to Friction

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Block slides 6 m across floor and decelerates from 8 m/s to 3 m/s. Mass = 2 kg. Find ОјвӮ–. Solution: 
Energy lost = О”KE = ВҪm(vвӮҖВІ вҲ’ vВІ) = ВҪ(2)(64вҲ’9) = 55 J
W_friction = fвӮ– Г— d = ОјвӮ–mg Г— d = 55
ОјвӮ– = 55/(2 Г— 9.8 Г— 6) = 55/117.6 = 0.468

Example 3.14 вҖ” Efficiency

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A motor (1500 W) lifts a 200 kg load 10 m. It takes 20 s. Find efficiency. Solution: 
Useful work done = mgh = 200(9.8)(10) = 19600 J
Energy input = P Г— t = 1500 Г— 20 = 30000 J
Efficiency = (19600/30000) Г— 100% = 65.3%

Example 3.15 вҖ” Escape from Gravity (PE вҶ’ KE)

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Ball launched from ground at 15 m/s. What is its height when speed = 10 m/s? (No friction) Solution: 
ВҪmvвӮҖВІ = ВҪmvВІ + mgh
ВҪ(225) = ВҪ(100) + 9.8h
112.5 = 50 + 9.8h
h = 62.5/9.8 = 6.38 m

Example 3.16 вҖ” Power and Velocity of Car

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Car engine provides constant power 60 kW. Mass = 1200 kg. At what speed does the car reach maximum velocity (when driving force equals friction = 800 N)? Solution: 
P = Fv at constant speed
60000 = 800 Г— v
v = 75 m/s = 270 km/h

Example 3.17 вҖ” Pendulum Energy

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A 0.5 kg pendulum bob swings from 0.3 m above lowest point. Find (a) max speed, (b) speed at 0.1 m above lowest point. Solution: 
(a) All PE вҶ’ KE at bottom:
    mgh = ВҪmvВІ
    v = вҲҡ(2gh) = вҲҡ(2Г—9.8Г—0.3) = вҲҡ5.88 = 2.42 m/s

(b) At h=0.1 m:
    mghвӮҖ = mgh + ВҪmvВІ
    v = вҲҡ(2g(hвӮҖвҲ’h)) = вҲҡ(2Г—9.8Г—0.2) = вҲҡ3.92 = 1.98 m/s

Example 3.18 вҖ” Spring Launched Projectile

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Spring (k=400 N/m, compressed 0.25 m) launches 0.2 kg ball at 30В° above horizontal. Find range. (g=9.8 m/sВІ) Solution: 
PE_spring = ВҪ(400)(0.0625) = 12.5 J = ВҪmvВІ
vвӮҖ = вҲҡ(2Г—12.5/0.2) = вҲҡ125 = 11.18 m/s

vвӮҖвӮ“ = 11.18 cos30В° = 9.68 m/s
vвӮҖбө§ = 11.18 sin30В° = 5.59 m/s
T = 2vвӮҖбө§/g = 1.14 s
R = vвӮҖвӮ“ Г— T = 9.68 Г— 1.14 = 11.0 m

Example 3.19 вҖ” Energy Theorem with Calculus

Type: Calculus Derivation Question: F(x) = (10 вҲ’ 2x) N acts on 2 kg object at rest. Find speed at x=4 m. Solution: 
W = вҲ«вӮҖвҒҙ (10 вҲ’ 2x) dx = [10x вҲ’ xВІ]вӮҖвҒҙ = 40 вҲ’ 16 = 24 J
W = О”KE = ВҪmvВІ вҲ’ 0
24 = ВҪ(2)vВІ
v = вҲҡ24 = 4.90 m/s

Example 3.20 вҖ” AP FRQ: Complete Energy Analysis

Type: Free Response Question: A 5 kg block starts from rest at top of ramp (h=4 m, length=8 m, ОјвӮ–=0.15). (a) Find speed at bottom using energy methods. (b) Block then slides on flat floor and compresses a spring (k=600 N/m). How far is spring compressed? (c) Does block return to original height? Justify. (d) Sketch energy bar charts at each stage. Solution: 
(a) On ramp:
    W_friction = вҲ’ОјвӮ–mg cosОё Г— L = вҲ’0.15(5)(9.8)(cos30В°)(8)
    cos Оё = h/L вҶ’ sinОё = 4/8 = 0.5, Оё=30В°, cosОё=0.866
    W_friction = вҲ’0.15(5)(9.8)(0.866)(8) = вҲ’50.9 J
    
    E_initial = mgh = 5(9.8)(4) = 196 J
    KE_bottom = 196 вҲ’ 50.9 = 145.1 J
    v = вҲҡ(2Г—145.1/5) = вҲҡ58.04 = 7.62 m/s

(b) On flat floor with spring (assuming frictionless floor):
    ВҪmvВІ = ВҪkxВІ
    145.1 = ВҪ(600)xВІ
    xВІ = 290.2/600 = 0.484
    x = 0.695 m

(c) No. Energy was lost to friction on the ramp. Even if spring and floor are frictionless,
    block returns with only 145.1 J (not 196 J), which brings it only to h=145.1/(mg)=2.97 m
    (not original 4 m).

(d) Energy bars:
    Initial: [====large====] PE, [empty] KE, [empty] Spring PE
    Bottom of ramp: [=====] KE, [empty] PE, [empty] Spring PE (some lost to heat)
    Max spring: [empty] KE, [empty] PE, [=====] Spring PE

Power = Answer: 98 W [mgh/t] 39. At what height is KE = PE for ball thrown upward? Answer: h = vвӮҖВІ/4g 40. Spring launcher: PE=25 J launches 0.5 kg. Speed = Answer: 10 m/s [v=вҲҡ(2Г—25/0.5)] 41. Machine with 75% efficiency inputs 200 J. Useful output: Answer: 150 J 42. Two balls: same mass, one at h=10 m, one at h=5 m. KE ratio at ground: Answer: 2:1 43. Ball falls freely 10 m. Using g=10: speed = Answer: вҲҡ200 вүҲ 14.1 m/s 49. A compressed spring releases; all PE converts to KE on frictionless surface. FRQ 1 вҖ” Energy Conservation on Curved Track

(a) 2 kg block slides from rest at h=6 m down frictionless curved track. Find speed at bottom. (b) Track has ОјвӮ–=0.2 for bottom 4 m. Find final speed. (c) Draw LOL diagram for each scenario. Answer: 
(a) mgh = ВҪmvВІ вҶ’ v = вҲҡ(2gh) = вҲҡ(2Г—9.8Г—6) = вҲҡ117.6 = 10.8 m/s
(b) Energy lost = ОјвӮ–mgГ—d = 0.2(2)(9.8)(4) = 15.68 J
    KE_final = mgh вҲ’ 15.68 = 117.6 вҲ’ 15.68 = 101.9 J
    v = вҲҡ(2Г—101.9/2) = вҲҡ101.9 = 10.1 m/s

FRQ 2 вҖ” Spring-Block System

k=1000 N/m, block 2 kg, compressed 0.3 m, ОјвӮ–=0.25 on horizontal surface. (a) Initial PE. (b) Max speed. (c) Distance until block stops. Answer: 
(a) PE = ВҪ(1000)(0.09) = 45 J
(b) v = вҲҡ(2Г—45/2) = вҲҡ45 = 6.71 m/s
(c) Distance: fвӮ–Г—d = 45 J вҶ’ ОјвӮ–mgГ—d = 45 вҶ’ d = 45/(0.25Г—2Г—9.8) = 9.18 m

FRQ 3 вҖ” Power and Performance

A 1200 kg car's engine outputs 90 kW. Resistive force = 1500 N. (a) Max constant speed. (b) Acceleration at 20 m/s. (c) Power at 20 m/s maintaining constant speed. Answer: 
(a) P = Fv вҶ’ 90000 = 1500v вҶ’ v = 60 m/s
(b) Net force = P/v вҲ’ friction = 90000/20 вҲ’ 1500 = 4500 вҲ’ 1500 = 3000 N
    a = 3000/1200 = 2.5 m/sВІ
(c) P = FГ—v = 1500Г—20 = 30,000 W = 30 kW (only friction force at constant speed)

FRQ 4 вҖ” Gravitational PE and Projectiles

Ball launched at vвӮҖ=20 m/s, 53В° above horizontal from 15 m cliff. (a) PE at launch point. (b) KE at top of trajectory. (c) Speed at ground. (d) At what height is KE=PE? Answer: 
(a) PE = mgh = m(9.8)(15) [need mass вҖ” use m=1 kg as reference]
(b) At peak: v = vвӮҖcosОё = 20(0.6)=12 m/s; KE=ВҪ(1)(144)=72 J
(c) E_total at launch = KE+PE = ВҪ(1)(400) + (1)(9.8)(15) = 200+147=347 J
    At ground: ВҪvВІ=347 вҶ’ v=вҲҡ694=26.3 m/s
(d) KE=PE: E_total/2=PE=mgh вҶ’ h=173.5/(9.8)=17.7 m above ground
    Since cliff is 15 m, height above ground = 17.7 m (ball is 2.7 m above cliff top)

FRQ 5 вҖ” Variable Force Work (AP-C)

F(x) = (8x вҲ’ 2xВІ) N for 0 вүӨ x вүӨ 4 m. Object starts from rest, mass 4 kg. (a) Work from x=0 to x=
  1. (b) Speed at x=4. (c) Where is force maximum?
Answer: 
(a) W = вҲ«вӮҖвҒҙ(8xвҲ’2xВІ)dx = [4xВІвҲ’(2/3)xВі]вӮҖвҒҙ = 64вҲ’(2/3)(64) = 64вҲ’42.7 = 21.3 J
(b) v = вҲҡ(2W/m) = вҲҡ(2Г—21.3/4) = вҲҡ10.67 = 3.27 m/s
(c) dF/dx = 8 вҲ’ 4x = 0 вҶ’ x = 2 m; F(2) = 16вҲ’8 = 8 N

FRQs 6вҖ“10 Answer Keys:

FRQ 6: Efficiency problem вҖ” useful output/input Г— 100%; actual values depend on given data
FRQ 7: Pendulum max height/speed вҶ’ h=L(1-cosОё), v=вҲҡ(2gL(1-cosОё))
FRQ 8: Energy dissipated = mgh вҲ’ ВҪmv_impactВІ (for fall with air resistance)
FRQ 9: Spring series vs parallel вҖ” k_series=k/2, k_parallel=2k
FRQ 10: Roller coaster minimum speed at loop top v=вҲҡ(gr); energy conservation for starting height

Unit 04  В·  AP1
Linear Momentum
Impulse В· Collisions В· Center of Mass

Unit 04: Linear Momentum, Impulse & Collisions

AP Physics 1 | Georgia Standards of Excellence

PART A: CONCEPTS

4.1 Momentum & Impulse

Linear Momentum:   p = mv              [kgВ·m/s]
Impulse:           J = FО”t = О”p        [NВ·s]
Impulse-Momentum:  J = mv_f вҲ’ mv_i
F_avg = О”p/О”t

Impulse = Area under F-t graph

4.2 Conservation of Momentum

Isolated system (no external forces): ОЈp = constant
mвӮҒvвӮҒбөў + mвӮӮvвӮӮбөў = mвӮҒvвӮҒf + mвӮӮvвӮӮf

System momentum conserved when:
  - No external net force
  - During ALL collisions (elastic and inelastic)
  - During explosions

4.3 Types of Collisions

ELASTIC:
  - Both KE and momentum conserved
  - Objects bounce; no deformation
  - vвӮҒf = ((mвӮҒвҲ’mвӮӮ)vвӮҒбөў)/(mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ) + 2mвӮӮvвӮӮбөў/(mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ)
  - vвӮӮf = 2mвӮҒvвӮҒбөў/(mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ) + ((mвӮӮвҲ’mвӮҒ)vвӮӮбөў)/(mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ)

PERFECTLY INELASTIC:
  - Objects stick together; maximum KE loss
  - v_f = (mвӮҒvвӮҒбөў + mвӮӮvвӮӮбөў)/(mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ)

INELASTIC:
  - Momentum conserved, some KE lost
  - Objects deform but separate

4.4 Center of Mass

x_cm = (mвӮҒxвӮҒ + mвӮӮxвӮӮ + ...)/M_total
v_cm = (mвӮҒvвӮҒ + mвӮӮvвӮӮ)/M_total  = p_total/M
a_cm = F_ext/M_total

Center of mass moves as if all external forces act at it.
Internal forces don't affect motion of CM.

4.5 2D Momentum Conservation

x: mвӮҒvвӮҒвӮ“бөў + mвӮӮvвӮӮвӮ“бөў = mвӮҒvвӮҒвӮ“f + mвӮӮvвӮӮвӮ“f
y: mвӮҒvвӮҒбө§бөў + mвӮӮvвӮӮбө§бөў = mвӮҒvвӮҒбө§f + mвӮӮvвӮӮбө§f

Apply independently in each direction.

PART B: DIAGRAMS

Area under F-t curve = Impulse = О”p

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20)

Ex 4.1 вҖ” Momentum Calculation

Q: 5 kg object at 8 m/s east. Momentum? 
p = mv = 5(8) = 40 kgВ·m/s east

Ex 4.2 вҖ” Impulse

Q: 100 N force acts on 3 kg for 0.5 s from rest. Find impulse and final speed. 
J = FО”t = 100(0.5) = 50 NВ·s
О”p = 50: mv_f = 50 вҶ’ v_f = 50/3 = 16.7 m/s

Ex 4.3 вҖ” Conservation: Perfectly Inelastic

Q: 4 kg at 6 m/s hits 2 kg at rest. They stick. Find v_f. 
mвӮҒvвӮҒ = (mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ)v_f
4(6) = 6Г—v_f вҶ’ v_f = 4 m/s
KE_lost = ВҪ(4)(36) вҲ’ ВҪ(6)(16) = 72 вҲ’ 48 = 24 J

Ex 4.4 вҖ” Conservation: Elastic (Equal Masses)

Q: 3 kg at 5 m/s hits 3 kg at rest. Elastic. Final velocities? 
Equal mass elastic: vвӮҒf = 0, vвӮӮf = 5 m/s (velocity exchange)
Check p: 3(5) = 3(0) + 3(5) = 15 вң“
Check KE: ВҪ(3)(25) = ВҪ(3)(25) вң“

Ex 4.5 вҖ” Impulse from Graph

Q: F-t graph: triangle from t=0 to t=4 s, peak F=20 N at t=2 s. Impulse? 
J = ВҪ Г— base Г— height = ВҪ(4)(20) = 40 NВ·s

Ex 4.6 вҖ” Explosion

Q: 5 kg bomb at rest explodes. 2 kg fragment goes left at 10 m/s. Find velocity of 3 kg fragment. 
Initial p = 0
0 = 2(вҲ’10) + 3v вҶ’ v = 20/3 = 6.67 m/s right

Ex 4.7 вҖ” Force from Momentum Change

Q: Ball (0.1 kg) at 20 m/s hits wall, bounces at 15 m/s. Contact time = 0.01 s. Avg force? 
О”p = m(v_f вҲ’ v_i) = 0.1(вҲ’15вҲ’20) = вҲ’3.5 NВ·s
F_avg = О”p/О”t = вҲ’3.5/0.01 = вҲ’350 N (from wall on ball)
Magnitude = 350 N

Ex 4.8 вҖ” 2D Collision

Q: 2 kg at 4 m/s east + 3 kg at 3 m/s north. They stick. Find v_f. 
pвӮ“ = 2(4) = 8 kgВ·m/s
pбө§ = 3(3) = 9 kgВ·m/s
Total mass = 5 kg
vвӮ“ = 8/5 = 1.6 m/s, vбө§ = 9/5 = 1.8 m/s
|v| = вҲҡ(1.6ВІ + 1.8ВІ) = вҲҡ(2.56+3.24) = вҲҡ5.80 = 2.41 m/s
Оё = arctan(1.8/1.6) = 48.4В° north of east

Ex 4.9 вҖ” Center of Mass

Q: 3 kg at x=1 m, 5 kg at x=5 m, 2 kg at x=9 m. Find x_cm. 
x_cm = (3Г—1 + 5Г—5 + 2Г—9)/(3+5+2) = (3+25+18)/10 = 46/10 = 4.6 m

Ex 4.10 вҖ” Elastic: Unequal Masses

Q: 6 kg at 4 m/s hits stationary 2 kg. Elastic. Find vвӮҒf and vвӮӮf. 
vвӮҒf = (mвӮҒвҲ’mвӮӮ)vвӮҒбөў/(mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ) = (6вҲ’2)(4)/(6+2) = 16/8 = 2 m/s (same direction)
vвӮӮf = 2mвӮҒvвӮҒбөў/(mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ) = 2(6)(4)/8 = 48/8 = 6 m/s (same direction)
Check p: 6(4) = 6(2)+2(6) = 12+12=24 вң“

Ex 4.11 вҖ” Bullet-Block

Q: 0.02 kg bullet at 300 m/s embeds in 1 kg block on frictionless table. Find v_f and % KE lost. 
v_f = (0.02Г—300)/(0.02+1) = 6/1.02 = 5.88 m/s
KE_i = ВҪ(0.02)(90000) = 900 J
KE_f = ВҪ(1.02)(5.88ВІ) = ВҪ(1.02)(34.6) = 17.6 J
% lost = (900вҲ’17.6)/900 Г— 100 = 98.0%

Ex 4.12 вҖ” Recoil

Q: Astronaut (80 kg) in space throws 2 kg wrench at 6 m/s. Astronaut recoil speed? 
m_A v_A + m_w v_w = 0
80v_A = вҲ’2(6) = вҲ’12
v_A = вҲ’0.15 m/s (opposite to wrench)

Ex 4.13 вҖ” Airbag Example

Q: Driver (75 kg) at 15 m/s stops. Without airbag: 0.05 s. With airbag: 0.3 s. Compare forces. 
О”p = 75(15) = 1125 NВ·s (same both cases)
Without: F = 1125/0.05 = 22,500 N
With: F = 1125/0.3 = 3,750 N
Airbag reduces force by factor of 6!

Ex 4.14 вҖ” Multi-Particle CM Velocity

Q: 3 kg moving +5 m/s, 2 kg moving вҲ’3 m/s. System CM velocity? 
v_cm = (mвӮҒvвӮҒ+mвӮӮvвӮӮ)/(mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ) = (3Г—5 + 2Г—(вҲ’3))/5 = (15вҲ’6)/5 = 9/5 = 1.8 m/s

Ex 4.15 вҖ” Momentum vs KE

Q: Same KE for 4 kg (vвӮҒ) and 9 kg (vвӮӮ). Ratio pвӮҒ/pвӮӮ? 
ВҪmвӮҒvвӮҒВІ = ВҪmвӮӮvвӮӮВІ вҶ’ vвӮҒ/vвӮӮ = вҲҡ(mвӮӮ/mвӮҒ) = вҲҡ(9/4) = 3/2
pвӮҒ/pвӮӮ = mвӮҒvвӮҒ/(mвӮӮvвӮӮ) = 4(3/2)/(9Г—1) Г— (vвӮӮ/vвӮӮ) = 6/9 = 2/3

Ex 4.16 вҖ” Impulse from Variable Force (AP-C)

Q: F(t) = (6tВІ) N acts on 1 kg from t=0 to t=3 s. Find О”v. 
J = вҲ«вӮҖВі 6tВІ dt = [2tВі]вӮҖВі = 2(27) = 54 NВ·s
О”v = J/m = 54/1 = 54 m/s

Ex 4.17 вҖ” Partially Elastic

Q: 3 kg at 8 m/s hits 5 kg at rest. After: 3 kg at 1 m/s. Find 5 kg speed and verify momentum. 
p_initial = 3(8) = 24 kgВ·m/s
p_final: 3(1) + 5vвӮӮ = 24 вҶ’ vвӮӮ = 21/5 = 4.2 m/s
KE_i = ВҪ(3)(64) = 96 J
KE_f = ВҪ(3)(1) + ВҪ(5)(17.64) = 1.5 + 44.1 = 45.6 J
KE lost = 50.4 J (inelastic)

Ex 4.18 вҖ” 2D Elastic Collision

Q: Billiard ball A (1 kg, 3 m/s right) hits B (1 kg, at rest). A deflects 30В° from original. B's direction? 
Equal masses elastic: A and B velocities perpendicular after collision.
A goes 30В° from x-axis вҶ’ B goes 90В°вҲ’30В°=60В° from x-axis (below x-axis).
Using conservation to find speeds:
v_AВІ + v_BВІ = vвӮҖВІ = 9 (equal mass elastic: speed relationship)
p_x: v_A cos30В° + v_B cos(вҲ’60В°) = 3
p_y: v_A sin30В° вҲ’ v_B sin60В° = 0 вҶ’ v_A = v_B Г— вҲҡ3

Solving: v_B = 3/2 = 1.5 m/s, v_A = 1.5вҲҡ3 = 2.60 m/s

Ex 4.19 вҖ” System Approach

Q: Two masses connected by compressed spring (total p=0). Spring releases: 4 kg gets 3 m/s. Find 6 kg velocity and system KE. 
0 = 4(3) + 6v вҶ’ v = вҲ’2 m/s
KE = ВҪ(4)(9) + ВҪ(6)(4) = 18 + 12 = 30 J (from spring PE)

Ex 4.20 вҖ” AP FRQ: Ballistic Pendulum

A 0.03 kg bullet at vвӮҖ embeds in 1 kg pendulum bob. Bob rises height h=0.12 m. (a) Find vвӮҖ. (b) KE before and after. (c) % KE lost. (d) Why not elastic? 
(a) v_f = вҲҡ(2gh) = вҲҡ(2Г—9.8Г—0.12) = 1.53 m/s
    Momentum: 0.03Г—vвӮҖ = (0.03+1)(1.53)
    vвӮҖ = 1.03Г—1.53/0.03 = 52.6 m/s

(b) KE_i = ВҪ(0.03)(52.6ВІ) = ВҪ(0.03)(2767) = 41.5 J
    KE_f = ВҪ(1.03)(1.53ВІ) = ВҪ(1.03)(2.34) = 1.21 J

(c) % lost = (41.5вҲ’1.21)/41.5 = 97.1%

(d) Bullet deforms, generates heat вҶ’ can't be elastic

PART D: 50-QUESTION TEST BANK & FRQ

MCQ (1-50)

  1. p = mv units: kgВ·m/s
  2. Impulse = FО”t = О”p
  3. Conservation of momentum requires: No external net force
  4. Perfectly inelastic: Objects stick together
  5. Elastic collision conserves: Both p and KE
  6. 2 kg at 5 m/s, p = 10 kgВ·m/s
  7. Explosion: total p before = 0, after: Still 0
  8. Ball bounces off wall with same speed: О”p = 2mv (magnitude)
  9. Larger О”t for same О”p means: Smaller force
  10. CM of equal masses at x=0 and x=4: x=2 m
  11. 4 kg at 3 m/s + 2 kg at вҲ’6 m/s total p: 0
  12. Bullet embeds in block. This is: Perfectly inelastic
  13. For elastic equal-mass head-on: Velocities exchange
  14. Impulse-momentum theorem: F_avg = О”p/О”t
  15. KE lost in perfectly inelastic (equal masses, one at rest): 50% of original KE
  16. p conserved in: All collision types
  17. Recoil demonstrates: Newton's 3rd law + conservation of momentum
  18. F-t graph area = Impulse
  19. 0.5 kg at 10 m/s. KE = 25 J; p = 5 kgВ·m/s
  20. 3 kg at 4 m/s collides with 3 kg at вҲ’2 m/s, stick. v_f = (12вҲ’6)/6 = 1 m/s

Unit 05: Torque and Rotational Dynamics

AP Physics 1 | Georgia Standards of Excellence

PART A: CONCEPTS

5.1 Rotational Kinematics

Angular displacement:    Оё           [radians]
Angular velocity:        Пү = dОё/dt   [rad/s]
Angular acceleration:    Оұ = dПү/dt   [rad/sВІ]

Linear-Angular Links:
  s = rОё        (arc length)
  v = rПү        (tangential speed)
  aвӮң = rОұ       (tangential acceleration)
  aвӮ’ = ПүВІr = vВІ/r  (centripetal acceleration)

Rotational Kinematic Equations (constant Оұ):
  Пү = ПүвӮҖ + Оұt
  Оё = ПүвӮҖt + ВҪОұtВІ
  ПүВІ = ПүвӮҖВІ + 2ОұОё
  Оё = ВҪ(ПүвӮҖ + Пү)t

5.2 Torque

П„ = rF sinОё = rвҠҘ F = r FвҠҘ     [NВ·m]

where:
  r = distance from pivot to force application [m]
  F = force magnitude [N]
  Оё = angle between r and F
  rвҠҘ = lever arm (perpendicular distance from pivot to line of action)

Net torque: ОЈП„ = IОұ    (Rotational Newton's 2nd Law)

Torque direction: Use right-hand rule
  CCW = positive (+)
  CW = negative (вҲ’)

5.3 Moment of Inertia

Point mass:     I = mrВІ                    [kgВ·mВІ]
System:         I = ОЈmбөўrбөўВІ

Common shapes (uniform):
  Solid disk/cylinder:   I = ВҪMRВІ
  Hollow cylinder:       I = MRВІ
  Solid sphere:          I = 2/5 MRВІ
  Hollow sphere:         I = 2/3 MRВІ
  Thin rod (center):     I = 1/12 MLВІ
  Thin rod (end):        I = 1/3 MLВІ

Parallel Axis Theorem:
  I = I_cm + MdВІ
  (d = distance from CM to new rotation axis)

5.4 Rotational Dynamics

ОЈП„_net = IОұ       (rotational F=ma)

Rotational KE:    KE_rot = ВҪIПүВІ

Combined rolling:
  KE_total = ВҪmvВІ + ВҪIПүВІ  (= ВҪmvВІ(1 + I/mrВІ) for rolling)

5.5 Static Equilibrium

For complete static equilibrium:
  ОЈFвӮ“ = 0  (translational x)
  ОЈFбө§ = 0  (translational y)
  ОЈП„ = 0   (rotational, about ANY point)

Choosing pivot at unknown force вҶ’ eliminates it from equation!

PART B: DIAGRAMS

Torque Diagram

          F
          вҶ‘  (applied force)
          в”Ӯ
         Оёв”Ӯ
          в”ӮвҶҗ r вҶ’
     в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв—Ҹв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ pivot axis
          
П„ = rF sinОё = rвҠҘF
rвҠҘ = r sinОё (lever arm = perpendicular distance)

Larger lever arm = greater torque for same F
Pushing at 90В° gives maximum torque

Free Body: Beam in Static Equilibrium

     вҶ‘ NвӮҒ        вҶ‘ NвӮӮ
     в”Ӯ            в”Ӯ
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв—Ҹв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв—Ҹв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
              вҶ“
              W = mg
              (at center for uniform beam)

Equilibrium:
ОЈFбө§: NвӮҒ + NвӮӮ = mg
ОЈП„ (about left end): NвӮӮ Г— L = mg Г— L/2 вҶ’ NвӮӮ = mg/2

Mermaid: Rotational vs Linear Analogy

graph LR L[LINEAR] --> R[ROTATIONAL] subgraph L x[x: displacement] v[v: velocity] a[a: acceleration] m[m: mass/inertia] F[F: force] p[p=mv: momentum] KE1[KE=ВҪmvВІ] end subgraph R Оё[Оё: angular displacement] Пү[Пү: angular velocity] Оұ[Оұ: angular acceleration] I[I=ОЈmrВІ: rotational inertia] П„[П„=rF sinОё: torque] L[L=IПү: angular momentum] KE2[KE=ВҪIПүВІ] end

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20)

Ex 5.1 вҖ” Torque

Q: 40 N force perpendicular at 0.8 m from pivot. Torque? 
П„ = rF sinОё = 0.8 Г— 40 Г— sin90В° = 32 NВ·m

Ex 5.2 вҖ” Net Torque

Q: 30 N at 0.5 m (CCW) and 20 N at 0.6 m (CW). Net torque? 
ОЈП„ = +30(0.5) вҲ’ 20(0.6) = 15 вҲ’ 12 = +3 NВ·m (CCW)

Ex 5.3 вҖ” Angular Acceleration

Q: Disk (I=0.4 kgВ·mВІ) has net torque 8 NВ·m. Angular acceleration? 
Оұ = ОЈП„/I = 8/0.4 = 20 rad/sВІ

Ex 5.4 вҖ” Moment of Inertia

Q: Two 3 kg masses at ends of 2 m massless rod rotating about center. I? 
I = ОЈmrВІ = 3(1)ВІ + 3(1)ВІ = 6 kgВ·mВІ

Ex 5.5 вҖ” Wheel Rotation from Rest

Q: Wheel (I=2 kgВ·mВІ) net torque 10 NВ·m. Angle covered in 4 s from rest? 
Оұ = П„/I = 5 rad/sВІ
Оё = ВҪОұtВІ = ВҪ(5)(16) = 40 rad

Ex 5.6 вҖ” Rotational KE

Q: Solid disk (M=4 kg, R=0.3 m) spinning at 10 rad/s. Rotational KE? 
I = ВҪMRВІ = ВҪ(4)(0.09) = 0.18 kgВ·mВІ
KE = ВҪIПүВІ = ВҪ(0.18)(100) = 9 J

Ex 5.7 вҖ” Rolling Object

Q: Solid sphere (I=2/5 MRВІ) rolls at v=5 m/s, M=2 kg. Total KE? 
KE_trans = ВҪmvВІ = ВҪ(2)(25) = 25 J
Пү = v/R; KE_rot = ВҪIПүВІ = ВҪ(2/5 mRВІ)(v/R)ВІ = ВҪ(2/5)mvВІ = 1/5(2)(25) = 10 J
KE_total = 25 + 10 = 35 J

Ex 5.8 вҖ” Static Equilibrium: Seesaw

Q: 60 kg person sits 2 m left of pivot. 40 kg person where on right for balance? 
ОЈП„ = 0: 60(9.8)(2) = 40(9.8)(d) вҶ’ d = 120/40 = 3 m from pivot

Ex 5.9 вҖ” Beam Supported at Ends

Q: 4 m beam (20 kg) with 50 kg load at 1 m from left. Find support forces. 
W_beam = 20(9.8) = 196 N at center (2 m)
W_load = 50(9.8) = 490 N at 1 m

ОЈП„ about left end = 0:
RвӮӮ(4) = 196(2) + 490(1) = 392 + 490 = 882
RвӮӮ = 220.5 N

ОЈFбө§: RвӮҒ + RвӮӮ = 686 вҶ’ RвӮҒ = 465.5 N

Ex 5.10 вҖ” Torque from Gravity on Rod

Q: Uniform rod (mass 5 kg, length 3 m) hinged at one end, horizontal. What torque does gravity exert? 
Gravity acts at CM = 1.5 m from hinge
П„ = mg Г— 1.5 = 5(9.8)(1.5) = 73.5 NВ·m (clockwise)

Ex 5.11 вҖ” Parallel Axis Theorem

Q: Solid disk I_cm = ВҪMRВІ = 0.5 kgВ·mВІ. Find I about edge. 
d = R вҶ’ I = I_cm + MRВІ = 0.5 + MRВІ
If I_cm = ВҪMRВІ = 0.5, then MRВІ = 1.0
I_edge = 0.5 + 1.0 = 1.5 kgВ·mВІ

Ex 5.12 вҖ” Newton's 2nd (Rotation)

Q: 3 kg disk (R=0.4 m) has tangential force 6 N at rim. Оұ? 
П„ = FR = 6(0.4) = 2.4 NВ·m
I = ВҪmrВІ = ВҪ(3)(0.16) = 0.24 kgВ·mВІ
Оұ = П„/I = 2.4/0.24 = 10 rad/sВІ

Ex 5.13 вҖ” Rolling Down Incline

Q: Solid cylinder (I=ВҪMRВІ) rolls down h=2 m incline from rest. Find v at bottom. 
Energy: Mgh = ВҪMvВІ + ВҪIПүВІ = ВҪMvВІ(1 + I/MRВІ) = ВҪMvВІ(1 + ВҪ) = ВҫMvВІ
vВІ = 4gh/3 = 4(9.8)(2)/3 = 26.1
v = 5.11 m/s
(Compare: frictionless slide v=вҲҡ(2gh) = 6.26 m/s вҖ” rolling is slower!)

Ex 5.14 вҖ” Torque at Angle

Q: 50 N force at 60В° to 0.6 m lever arm. Torque? 
П„ = rF sinОё = 0.6(50)(sin60В°) = 0.6(50)(0.866) = 25.98 NВ·m

Ex 5.15 вҖ” Angular Velocity from KE

Q: I=3 kgВ·mВІ, KE_rot=24 J. Angular velocity? 
ВҪIПүВІ = 24 вҶ’ ПүВІ = 48/3 = 16 вҶ’ Пү = 4 rad/s

Ex 5.16 вҖ” Ladder Equilibrium

Q: 5 m uniform ladder (30 kg) leans at 60В° against frictionless wall. Person (70 kg) at 4 m up. Find floor reactions. 
NбөҘбөҘвӮҗвӮ—вӮ— acts horizontally at top.
ОЈFвӮ“: N_wall вҲ’ f_floor = 0 вҶ’ f_floor = N_wall
ОЈFбө§: N_floor вҲ’ 30g вҲ’ 70g = 0 вҶ’ N_floor = 980 N

ОЈП„ (about base):
N_wall Г— 5sin60В° = 30g Г— 2.5cos60В° + 70g Г— 4cos60В°
N_wall Г— 4.33 = 30(9.8)(1.25) + 70(9.8)(2.0)
N_wall Г— 4.33 = 367.5 + 1372 = 1739.5
N_wall = 401.7 N = f_floor

Ex 5.17 вҖ” Calculus: Angular Acceleration (AP-C)

Q: П„(t) = 6tВІ NВ·m on I=3 kgВ·mВІ, ПүвӮҖ=2 rad/s. Find Пү(t). 
Оұ(t) = П„/I = 2tВІ
Пү(t) = ПүвӮҖ + вҲ«вӮҖбө— 2tВІ dt = 2 + 2tВі/3
Пү(3) = 2 + 2(27)/3 = 2 + 18 = 20 rad/s

Ex 5.18 вҖ” Wrench Problem

Q: Two wrenches: 0.3 m vs 0.5 m applying same torque. Force ratio FвӮҒ/FвӮӮ? 
П„ = rвӮҒFвӮҒ = rвӮӮFвӮӮ
FвӮҒ/FвӮӮ = rвӮӮ/rвӮҒ = 0.5/0.3 = 5/3
Longer wrench needs less force!

Ex 5.19 вҖ” Rotational Kinematic

Q: Disk starts at rest, Оұ=8 rad/sВІ. How many revolutions in 5 s? 
Оё = ВҪОұtВІ = ВҪ(8)(25) = 100 rad
Revolutions = 100/(2ПҖ) = 15.9 rev

Ex 5.20 вҖ” AP FRQ: Rotating Rod

Uniform rod (M=2 kg, L=1 m) pivoted at one end, released from horizontal. (a) Initial angular acceleration. (b) Speed of free end when vertical. (c) Torque when 60В° from vertical. 
(a) П„ = Mg(L/2) = 2(9.8)(0.5) = 9.8 NВ·m
    I = MLВІ/3 = 2(1)/3 = 0.667 kgВ·mВІ
    Оұ = П„/I = 9.8/0.667 = 14.7 rad/sВІ

(b) Energy: Mg(L/2) = ВҪIПүВІ [CM falls L/2]
    9.8 = ВҪ(0.667)ПүВІ вҶ’ Пү = 5.42 rad/s
    v_end = ПүL = 5.42 m/s

(c) П„ = Mg(L/2)cos60В° = 2(9.8)(0.5)(0.5) = 4.9 NВ·m

Rolling: v_cm = RПү
KE_roll = ВҪmvВІ(1 + I/mRВІ)
Static equilibrium: ОЈF=0, ОЈП„=0
