FULL FRQ SET (Units 05 вҖ” 10 Questions)

FRQ 05-1 вҖ” Beam Balance Design

A 6 m uniform beam (mass=20 kg) is supported by cables at 1 m from each end. A 50 kg object hangs at 1.5 m from the left cable. (a) Draw a free body diagram of the beam. (b) Find the tension in each cable using torque equilibrium. (c) Verify your answer using force equilibrium. (d) If the right cable is cut, find initial angular acceleration using the left cable as pivot. Answer: 
Setup: Left cable at x=1m; right cable at x=5m; beam CM at x=3m; 50kg load at x=2.5m.

(a) FBD: T_L up at x=1m, T_R up at x=5m, beam weight (196N) down at x=3m, load (490N) down at x=2.5m.

(b) ОЈП„ about left cable (x=1m):
T_RГ—(5вҲ’1) = 196Г—(3вҲ’1) + 490Г—(2.5вҲ’1)
4T_R = 196Г—2 + 490Г—1.5 = 392 + 735 = 1127
T_R = 281.75 N

(c) ОЈFбө§=0: T_L + T_R = 196 + 490 = 686 N
T_L = 686 вҲ’ 281.75 = 404.25 N

(d) Right cable cut вҶ’ only T_L acts at x=1m.
Torques about left end of beam (x=0):
Gravity torques:
П„_gravity = 196Г—3 + 490Г—2.5 = 588+1225=1813 NВ·m (CW, downward)
П„_T_L = 404.25Г—1 = 404.25 NВ·m (CCW) [if T_L still holds]
But T_L is now the only support. The beam now rotates.

Net torque about x=0 (end of beam) = T_L(1) вҲ’ 196(3) вҲ’ 490(2.5)
= 404.25 вҲ’ 1813 = вҲ’1408.75 NВ·m (clockwise)

I about end = I_cm + MdВІ = (1/12)(20)(36) + 20(3ВІ) = 60+180=240 kgВ·mВІ (beam)
+ load: 50(2.5ВІ)=312.5 kgВ·mВІ
I_total = 552.5 kgВ·mВІ
Оұ = П„/I = 1408.75/552.5 = 2.55 rad/sВІ (clockwise)

FRQ 05-2 вҖ” Rotating Disk System

A motor applies a constant torque of 24 NВ·m to a solid disk (M=4 kg, R=0.5 m) that starts from rest. (a) Calculate the moment of inertia of the disk. (b) Calculate angular acceleration. (c) Find angular velocity after 6 s. (d) Find the rotational KE at t=6 s. (e) Find total angle rotated and number of revolutions. Answer: 
(a) I = ВҪMRВІ = ВҪ(4)(0.25) = 0.5 kgВ·mВІ

(b) Оұ = П„/I = 24/0.5 = 48 rad/sВІ

(c) Пү = ПүвӮҖ + Оұt = 0 + 48(6) = 288 rad/s

(d) KE = ВҪIПүВІ = ВҪ(0.5)(288ВІ) = 0.25(82944) = 20,736 J
    Check with work: W = П„Г—Оё

(e) Оё = ВҪОұtВІ = ВҪ(48)(36) = 864 rad
    Revolutions = 864/(2ПҖ) = 137.5 rev
    Check: W = П„Оё = 24Г—864 = 20,736 J вң“

FRQ 05-3 вҖ” Ladder Problem (Classic Statics)

A 4 m uniform ladder (mass=15 kg) leans against a frictionless wall at angle 60В° from floor. A 70 kg person stands 3 m up the ladder. The floor has friction. (a) Draw complete FBD for the ladder. (b) Find normal force from wall. (c) Find normal force from floor. (d) Find minimum static friction coefficient to prevent slipping. Answer: 
(a) FBD: N_wall horizontal at top; N_floor vertical at base; f_floor horizontal at base; W_ladder at center; W_person at 3m up.

(b) ОЈП„ about base (x=0):
N_wall Г— 4sin60В° = W_ladder Г— 2cos60В° + W_person Г— 3cos60В°
N_wall Г— 3.464 = 15(9.8)(1.0) + 70(9.8)(1.5)
N_wall Г— 3.464 = 147 + 1029 = 1176
N_wall = 339.6 N

(c) N_floor = W_ladder + W_person = 15(9.8)+70(9.8) = 147+686 = 833 N

(d) ОЈFвӮ“ = 0: f_floor = N_wall = 339.6 N
Ој_min = f/N_floor = 339.6/833 = 0.408

FRQs 05-4 through 05-10 Key Answers:

FRQ 05-4: Rolling sphere down ramp вҖ” use energy conservation with rotational KE
  v = вҲҡ(10gh/7); solid sphere reaches bottom faster than hollow cylinder

FRQ 05-5: Atwood machine with pulley (Iвү 0) вҖ” tension different on each side
  a = (mвӮҒ-mвӮӮ)g/(mвӮҒ+mвӮӮ+I/RВІ); TвӮҒвү TвӮӮ now

FRQ 05-6: Torque from multiple forces on irregular shape вҖ” vector approach
  Sum all П„_i = r_i Г— F_i; use CCW positive convention

FRQ 05-7: Finding center of mass experimentally вҖ” hanging method
  CM is always below pivot when hanging; two pivot positions give intersection

FRQ 05-8: Angular kinematics вҖ” car wheel acceleration
  Пү=v/R; Оұ=a/R; all rotational kinematics equations apply

FRQ 05-9: Stability analysis вҖ” tipping condition
  Object tips when CM moves beyond support point; П„_gravity CW > 0

FRQ 05-10: Synthesis вҖ” rotating system with multiple objects
  I_total = ОЈm_iR_iВІ; apply ОЈП„=IОұ; include all contributing masses
рҹ”„
Unit 06  В·  AP1/C
Rotating Systems
Angular Momentum В· Rolling Motion
L = IПүIвӮҒПүвӮҒ = IвӮӮПүвӮӮKE_roll = ВҪmvВІ(1+I/mRВІ)v_cm = RПү

Unit 06: Energy and Momentum of Rotating Systems

AP Physics 1 & C | Georgia Standards

PART A: CONCEPTS

6.1 Angular Momentum

Angular momentum of particle:  L = mvr sinОё = IПү    [kgВ·mВІ/s]
For point mass:                L = mrВІПү
For rigid body:                L = IПү

Conservation of Angular Momentum:
  If ОЈП„_ext = 0:  L_i = L_f вҶ’ IвӮҒПүвӮҒ = IвӮӮПүвӮӮ

Applications:
  - Figure skater pulls arms in: I decreases, Пү increases
  - Planets orbit faster when closer to sun
  - Gyroscopes

6.2 Rotational Work and Energy

Work by torque:       W = П„ Г— Оё           [J]
Power by torque:      P = П„Пү              [W]
Rotational KE:        KE = ВҪIПүВІ          [J]
Work-Energy (rot):    W_net = О”KE_rot = ВҪIПүВІ вҲ’ ВҪIПүвӮҖВІ

6.3 Rolling Without Slipping

Condition: v_cm = RПү  (contact point has zero velocity)

Total KE = ВҪmvВІ + ВҪIПүВІ

For common shapes rolling down height h (from rest):
  Solid sphere (I=2/5 mrВІ):    v = вҲҡ(10gh/7)
  Solid cylinder (I=ВҪmrВІ):     v = вҲҡ(4gh/3)
  Hollow cylinder (I=mrВІ):     v = вҲҡ(gh)  [slowest]
  
  Rank (fastest to slowest): sphere > cylinder > hollow cylinder

6.4 Angular Impulse

Angular Impulse:  L_impulse = П„ Г— О”t = О”L = I(Пү_f вҲ’ Пү_i)

PART B: DIAGRAMS

Angular Momentum Conservation: Figure Skater

ARMS OUT                    ARMS IN
I_large вҶ’ Пү_small          I_small вҶ’ Пү_large

L = IвӮҒПүвӮҒ = IвӮӮПүвӮӮ
KE increases! (extra from muscle work done pulling arms in)

      в¬Ҷ                         в¬Ҷ
    в”Ңв”Җв”јв”Җв”җ  вҶҗ arms out         в”Ңв”Җв”јв”Җв”җ  вҶҗ arms in
    в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ                      в”Ӯ в”Ӯ в”Ӯ
    в””в”Җв”ҙв”Җв”ҳ  Пү small            в””в”Җв”ҙв”Җв”ҳ  Пү large

      вҶ‘

v_top = 2v_cm (fastest point)
v_center = v_cm
v_bottom = 0 (instantaneous rest)

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20)

Ex 6.1 вҖ” L = IПү

Q: I=2 kgВ·mВІ, Пү=5 rad/s. L? 
L = IПү = 10 kgВ·mВІ/s

Ex 6.2 вҖ” Conservation of L

Q: Skater: IвӮҒ=3 kgВ·mВІ, ПүвӮҒ=2 rev/s. Pulls to IвӮӮ=1.5 kgВ·mВІ. ПүвӮӮ? 
LвӮҒ=LвӮӮ: 3(2) = 1.5ПүвӮӮ вҶ’ ПүвӮӮ = 4 rev/s
KEвӮҒ=ВҪ(3)(4ПҖВІ)Г—4=236 J; KEвӮӮ=ВҪ(1.5)(16ПҖВІ)=118... 
Actually: KEвӮӮ/KEвӮҒ = IвӮҒ/IвӮӮ Г— (ПүвӮӮ/ПүвӮҒ)ВІ = 2 (KE increases)

Ex 6.3 вҖ” Rolling KE

Q: 2 kg solid disk (R=0.2 m) rolls at 4 m/s. Total KE? 
I=ВҪmrВІ=0.04; Пү=v/R=20 rad/s
KE = ВҪ(2)(16) + ВҪ(0.04)(400) = 16 + 8 = 24 J
Or: KE = ВҪmvВІ(1 + ВҪ) = ВҫmvВІ = Вҫ(2)(16) = 24 J вң“

Ex 6.4 вҖ” Rolling Down Incline

Q: Solid sphere rolls from rest, h=3.5 m. Final v? 
v = вҲҡ(10gh/7) = вҲҡ(10Г—9.8Г—3.5/7) = вҲҡ49 = 7 m/s

Ex 6.5 вҖ” Rotational Work

Q: Torque 15 NВ·m rotates object through 8 rad. Work done? 
W = П„Оё = 15(8) = 120 J

Ex 6.6 вҖ” L of Planet

Q: Earth (m=6Г—10ВІвҒҙ kg) orbits at r=1.5Г—10В№В№ m, v=3Г—10вҒҙ m/s. L? 
L = mvr = 6Г—10ВІвҒҙ Г— 3Г—10вҒҙ Г— 1.5Г—10В№В№ = 2.7Г—10вҒҙвҒ° kgВ·mВІ/s

Ex 6.7 вҖ” Conservation: Star Collapse

Q: Star (IвӮҒ=5Г—10вҒҙвҒ° kgВ·mВІ) at T=30 days collapses to IвӮӮ=2Г—10ВівҒ° kgВ·mВІ. New period? 
L conserved: IвӮҒПүвӮҒ = IвӮӮПүвӮӮ
ПүвӮҒ = 2ПҖ/TвӮҒ ; ПүвӮӮ = IвӮҒПүвӮҒ/IвӮӮ
TвӮӮ = TвӮҒ Г— IвӮӮ/IвӮҒ = 30 Г— 2Г—10ВівҒ°/(5Г—10вҒҙвҒ°) = 1.2Г—10вҒ»вҒё days

Ex 6.8 вҖ” Which Rolls Fastest?

Q: Sphere, disk, and ring of same mass/radius released on same incline. Rank by speed. 
Speed вҲқ вҲҡ(2gh/(1 + I/mRВІ))
Sphere: 1/(1+2/5) = 5/7 вҶ’ fastest
Disk: 1/(1+1/2) = 2/3
Ring: 1/(1+1) = 1/2 вҶ’ slowest

Ex 6.9 вҖ” Power at Angular Speed

Q: Engine torque 200 NВ·m at 3000 rpm. Power? 
Пү = 3000Г—2ПҖ/60 = 314 rad/s
P = П„Пү = 200(314) = 62,800 W = 62.8 kW

Ex 6.10 вҖ” Point Mass L

Q: 0.5 kg ball on 1.2 m string swings at 3 m/s. L? 
L = mvr = 0.5(3)(1.2) = 1.8 kgВ·mВІ/s

Ex 6.11 вҖ” Angular Impulse

Q: Torque 6 NВ·m acts for 3 s on disk at rest with I=0.9 kgВ·mВІ. Final Пү? 
П„О”t = IО”Пү вҶ’ 6(3) = 0.9Пү вҶ’ Пү = 20 rad/s

Ex 6.12 вҖ” Merry-Go-Round + Person

Q: I_mgr=200 kgВ·mВІ, Пү=2 rad/s. Person (60 kg) at r=2 m jumps on. New Пү? 
L_i = 200(2) = 400 kgВ·mВІ/s
I_person = mrВІ = 60(4) = 240 kgВ·mВІ
L_f = (200+240)Пү_f = 440Пү_f = 400
Пү_f = 0.91 rad/s

Ex 6.13 вҖ” KE Change in Conservation

Q: Above problem. Initial KE? Final KE? 
KE_i = ВҪ(200)(4) = 400 J
KE_f = ВҪ(440)(0.91ВІ) = ВҪ(440)(0.828) = 182 J
KE lost = 218 J (to friction/heat as person lands)

Ex 6.14 вҖ” Rolling Without Slipping Condition

Q: Cylinder (R=0.1 m) rolls without slipping. v_cm=2 m/s. Пү? 
Пү = v_cm/R = 2/0.1 = 20 rad/s
v_top = 2v_cm = 4 m/s
v_bottom = 0

Ex 6.15 вҖ” Torque Produces L Change

Q: Object (I=0.5 kgВ·mВІ) has 10 NВ·m torque applied 3 s. О”L? 
О”L = П„О”t = 10(3) = 30 kgВ·mВІ/s

Ex 6.16 вҖ” Hollow vs Solid Cylinder Race

Q: Hollow (I=mrВІ) and solid (I=ВҪmrВІ) cylinders race down 1 m incline. Speed difference? 
v_solid = вҲҡ(4gh/3) = вҲҡ(4Г—9.8/3) = вҲҡ13.1 = 3.61 m/s
v_hollow = вҲҡ(gh) = вҲҡ9.8 = 3.13 m/s
О”v = 0.48 m/s (solid wins)

Ex 6.17 вҖ” Rotation with Friction

Q: Disk (I=0.3 kgВ·mВІ) at 20 rad/s. Friction torque 1.5 NВ·m. Time to stop? 
Оұ = вҲ’П„/I = вҲ’1.5/0.3 = вҲ’5 rad/sВІ
t = вҲ’ПүвӮҖ/Оұ = вҲ’20/(вҲ’5) = 4 s

Ex 6.18 вҖ” Flywheel Energy Storage

Q: Flywheel (I=50 kgВ·mВІ, Пү=300 rad/s). Stored energy? 
KE = ВҪIПүВІ = ВҪ(50)(90000) = 2,250,000 J = 2.25 MJ

Ex 6.19 вҖ” Precession Concept (AP-C)

Q: Gyroscope (L=10 kgВ·mВІ/s) with gravity torque 5 NВ·m. Precession rate? 
Precession: О© = П„/L = 5/10 = 0.5 rad/s

Ex 6.20 вҖ” AP FRQ: Rotating Rod System

Rod (M=1 kg, L=2 m) horizontal, pivoted at end. Ball (m=0.5 kg) dropped on far end. (a) Initial L of ball just before impact: v=3 m/s downward. (b) After ball sticks, find Пү_f. (c) Find KE before and after. 
(a) L_ball = mГ—vГ—r = 0.5Г—3Г—2 = 3 kgВ·mВІ/s (about pivot)

(b) I_rod = MLВІ/3 = 1(4)/3 = 1.33 kgВ·mВІ
    I_ball = mrВІ = 0.5(4) = 2 kgВ·mВІ
    I_total = 3.33 kgВ·mВІ
    
    L conserved: 3 = 3.33Пү_f вҶ’ Пү_f = 0.90 rad/s

(c) KE_ball_i = ВҪ(0.5)(9) = 2.25 J
    KE_f = ВҪ(3.33)(0.81) = 1.35 J
    KE_lost = 0.90 J

FULL FRQ SET (Unit 06 вҖ” 10 Questions)

FRQ 06-1 вҖ” Figure Skater Angular Momentum

A figure skater (I_extended = 4.8 kgВ·mВІ, Пү_i = 1.5 rev/s) pulls arms to I_tucked = 1.2 kgВ·mВІ. (a) Find final angular velocity. (b) Find initial and final rotational KE. (c) Where does the extra KE come from? (d) Repeat if she extends arms back вҖ” does she return to exactly 1.5 rev/s? Why? Answer: 
(a) L conserved: IвӮҒПүвӮҒ = IвӮӮПүвӮӮ
    4.8(1.5) = 1.2ПүвӮӮ вҶ’ ПүвӮӮ = 6.0 rev/s

(b) KEвӮҒ = ВҪIвӮҒПүвӮҒВІ = ВҪ(4.8)(9ПҖВІ) = 212.1 J  [using Пү=1.5Г—2ПҖ=9.42 rad/s]
    More precisely: ПүвӮҒ=1.5Г—2ПҖ=9.42 rad/s; KEвӮҒ=ВҪ(4.8)(88.8)=213 J
    ПүвӮӮ=6Г—2ПҖ=37.7 rad/s; KEвӮӮ=ВҪ(1.2)(1421)=852 J

(c) The skater's muscles do work in pulling arms inward against centrifugal effect.
    Extra KE = 852вҲ’213 = 639 J (comes from internal muscular energy)

(d) Yes вҖ” if muscles extend arms back to exact same I, Пү returns to 1.5 rev/s.
    But in practice: friction at ice, air resistance вҶ’ slight decrease.

FRQ 06-2 вҖ” Rolling Object Energy

A solid sphere (M=2 kg, R=0.1 m) rolls from rest down a ramp (height h=0.7 m) onto flat floor. (a) Find speed at bottom of ramp. (b) Find translational and rotational KE at bottom. (c) On flat floor (Ој_k=0.05), how far does it roll before stopping? Answer: 
(a) v = вҲҡ(10gh/7) = вҲҡ(10Г—9.8Г—0.7/7) = вҲҡ9.8 = 3.13 m/s

(b) KE_trans = ВҪmvВІ = ВҪ(2)(9.8) = 9.8 J
    KE_rot = 2/7 Г— mgh = 2/7 Г— 2Г—9.8Г—0.7 = 3.92 J
    Total = 9.8+3.92 = 13.72 J = mgh = 2Г—9.8Г—0.7 вң“

(c) For rolling deceleration: friction decelerates both translation and rotation.
    Net friction torque: П„=fR=ОјmgR
    Deceleration: a = Ојg(1+I/mRВІ)вҒ»В№ вҶ’ for sphere: a=5Ојg/7=5(0.05)(9.8)/7=0.35 m/sВІ
    Distance: vВІ=2ad вҶ’ d=vВІ/(2a)=9.8/(2Г—0.35)=14 m

06-5: Gyroscope precession вҖ” О©=П„/L; slower spin вҶ’ faster precession
06-6: Angular impulse-momentum вҖ” П„О”t=О”L; find final Пү
06-7: Comparison of rolling shapes вҖ” rank by speed using v=вҲҡ(2gh/(1+k))
06-8: Planet Kepler's 2nd law вҖ” equal areas equal times from angular momentum conservation
06-9: Rotating rod catches ball вҖ” use conservation of L; rod+ball system
06-10: Nuclear fission angular momentum вҖ” initial L=0; fragments must have opposite L

Unit 07  В·  AP1
Oscillations & SHM
Springs В· Pendulums В· Resonance

Unit 07: Oscillations вҖ” SHM, Springs, Pendulums

AP Physics 1 | Georgia Standards

PART A: CONCEPTS

7.1 Simple Harmonic Motion (SHM)

Definition: Restoring force вҲқ вҲ’displacement
  F = вҲ’kx   (Hooke's Law)

Position:    x(t) = A cos(Пүt + ПҶ)    [m]
Velocity:    v(t) = вҲ’AПү sin(Пүt + ПҶ) [m/s]
Acceleration: a(t) = вҲ’AПүВІ cos(Пүt)   [m/sВІ]

Key relationships:
  Пү = 2ПҖf = 2ПҖ/T      [rad/s]
  v_max = AПү           [m/s] (at x=0)
  a_max = AПүВІ          [m/sВІ] (at x=ВұA)
  
  v = ПүвҲҡ(AВІ вҲ’ xВІ)     (velocity at position x)

7.2 Mass-Spring System

Spring constant: F = kx    [N/m]
Period:   T = 2ПҖвҲҡ(m/k)    [s]
Frequency: f = 1/(2ПҖ) Г— вҲҡ(k/m)  [Hz]
Пү = вҲҡ(k/m)               [rad/s]

Note: Period is INDEPENDENT of amplitude (for ideal spring)
Note: Period depends on mass but NOT on g

7.3 Simple Pendulum

For small angles (Оё < 15В°):
Period:    T = 2ПҖвҲҡ(L/g)   [s]
Frequency: f = 1/(2ПҖ)вҲҡ(g/L)  [Hz]

Note: Period independent of mass and amplitude (small angles)
Note: Period DEPENDS on g (unlike spring)

7.4 Energy in SHM

PE_spring = ВҪkxВІ
KE = ВҪmvВІ
E_total = ВҪkAВІ = constant (no friction)

At x = 0 (equilibrium): KE = max, PE = 0
At x = ВұA (amplitude): KE = 0, PE = max

At any position: E = ВҪkxВІ + ВҪmvВІ = ВҪkAВІ

7.5 Damping and Resonance

Damped: Amplitude decreases over time due to friction
Resonance: Maximum amplitude when driving frequency = natural frequency
  f_drive = f_natural = 1/(2ПҖ)вҲҡ(k/m)

PART B: DIAGRAMS

SHM Position-Velocity-Acceleration

x(t):    в”Җв”Җв”Җв—Ҹв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ t
            в•І      в•ұв•І      в•ұ
             в•Ів”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв•ұ  в•Ів”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв•ұ   вҶҗ cosine wave

v(t):    в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв—Ҹв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ t
           в•ұв•І      в•ұв•І      в•ұ
          в•ұ  в•Ів”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв•ұ  в•Ів”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв•ұ     вҶҗ вҲ’sine wave (90В° behind x)

a(t):    в”Җв”Җв”Җв—Ҹв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ t  
            в•І      в•ұв•І      в•ұ
             в•Ів”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв•ұ  в•Ів”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв•ұ   вҶҗ вҲ’cosine = opposite to x

Key: a always points TOWARD equilibrium

Energy in SHM

Energy
в”Ӯ                         в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ E_total (constant)
в”Ӯ                    в•ұв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв•І

в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ x
  вҲ’A         0         +A

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20)

Ex 7.1 вҖ” Spring Period

Q: m=0.5 kg, k=200 N/m. Period and frequency? 
T = 2ПҖвҲҡ(m/k) = 2ПҖвҲҡ(0.0025) = 2ПҖ(0.05) = 0.314 s
f = 1/T = 3.18 Hz

Ex 7.2 вҖ” Finding k from Period

Q: T=0.4 s, m=0.16 kg. Find k. 
TВІ = 4ПҖВІm/k вҶ’ k = 4ПҖВІm/TВІ = 4ПҖВІ(0.16)/(0.16) = 4ПҖВІ = 39.5 N/m

Ex 7.3 вҖ” Pendulum Period

Q: L=1.5 m pendulum on Earth (g=9.8). Period? 
T = 2ПҖвҲҡ(L/g) = 2ПҖвҲҡ(1.5/9.8) = 2ПҖ(0.391) = 2.46 s

Ex 7.4 вҖ” Max Speed in SHM

Q: A=0.08 m, k=100 N/m, m=0.5 kg. Max speed? 
Пү = вҲҡ(k/m) = вҲҡ200 = 14.14 rad/s
v_max = AПү = 0.08(14.14) = 1.13 m/s

Ex 7.5 вҖ” Energy in SHM

Q: k=400 N/m, A=0.1 m. Total energy and max speed if m=0.8 kg. 
E = ВҪkAВІ = ВҪ(400)(0.01) = 2 J
ВҪmvВІ = 2 вҶ’ v = вҲҡ(4/0.8) = вҲҡ5 = 2.24 m/s

Ex 7.6 вҖ” Speed at Position

Q: A=0.12 m, Пү=5 rad/s. Speed at x=0.08 m? 
v = ПүвҲҡ(AВІвҲ’xВІ) = 5вҲҡ(0.0144вҲ’0.0064) = 5вҲҡ0.008 = 5(0.0894) = 0.447 m/s... 
Actually: v=5вҲҡ(0.12ВІвҲ’0.08ВІ) = 5вҲҡ(0.0144вҲ’0.0064) = 5вҲҡ0.008 = 0.447 m/s

Ex 7.7 вҖ” Pendulum on Different Planet

Q: Pendulum T=2 s on Earth. T on Moon (g_moon=1.6 m/sВІ)? 
T = 2ПҖвҲҡ(L/g) вҶ’ L = TВІg/(4ПҖВІ) = 4(9.8)/4ПҖВІ = 0.994 m
T_moon = 2ПҖвҲҡ(0.994/1.6) = 2ПҖвҲҡ0.621 = 4.96 s

Ex 7.8 вҖ” Maximum Acceleration

Q: A=0.05 m, T=0.8 s. Max acceleration? 
Пү = 2ПҖ/T = 7.854 rad/s
a_max = AПүВІ = 0.05(61.7) = 3.08 m/sВІ

Ex 7.9 вҖ” Energy Split

Q: At x=A/2, what fraction of total energy is KE? 
PE = ВҪk(A/2)ВІ = Вј Г— ВҪkAВІ = ВјE_total
KE = E вҲ’ PE = ВҫE_total
вҶ’ 75% of total energy is kinetic at x=A/2

Ex 7.10 вҖ” Frequency from Acceleration

Q: a = вҲ’16x. What is the angular frequency? 
a = вҲ’ПүВІx вҶ’ ПүВІ = 16 вҶ’ Пү = 4 rad/s, f = 2/ПҖ Hz

Exs 7.11вҖ“7.20 Key Results:

7.11: Two springs in series: k_eff = kвӮҒkвӮӮ/(kвӮҒ+kвӮӮ)
7.12: Two springs in parallel: k_eff = kвӮҒ+kвӮӮ
7.13: x(t) = 0.1cos(4t+ПҖ/4); write v(t) and a(t)
7.14: Clock pendulum length for T=2 s: L=g/ПҖВІвүҲ0.994 m
7.15: Spring mass on incline: T unchanged (g component cancels)
7.16: Resonance frequency = natural frequency
7.17: Damped oscillation: amplitude decays as e^(-bt/2m)
7.18: Phase difference: position leads by ПҖ/2 over velocity
7.19: Mass hung from spring stretches xвӮҖ=mg/k; xвӮҖ becomes new equilibrium
7.20 FRQ: Full spring system analysis with energy, speed, time

FULL FRQ SET (Unit 07 вҖ” 10 Questions)

FRQ 07-1 вҖ” Spring-Mass System Analysis

A 0.5 kg block attached to spring (k=200 N/m) oscillates on frictionless surface. Released from rest at x=0.15 m from equilibrium. (a) Period and frequency. (b) Maximum speed and where it occurs. (c) Maximum acceleration and where it occurs. (d) Total energy. (e) Speed at x=0.10 m. (f) Position at t=T/4 (one quarter period) if released from +A at t=0. Answer: 
(a) T=2ПҖвҲҡ(m/k)=2ПҖвҲҡ(0.5/200)=2ПҖвҲҡ(0.0025)=2ПҖГ—0.05=0.314 s
    f=1/T=3.18 Hz

(b) v_max=AПү=0.15Г—вҲҡ(400)=0.15Г—20=3.0 m/s; occurs at x=0 (equilibrium)

(c) a_max=AПүВІ=0.15Г—400=60 m/sВІ; occurs at x=ВұA=Вұ0.15 m

(d) E=ВҪkAВІ=ВҪ(200)(0.0225)=2.25 J

(e) v=ПүвҲҡ(AВІ-xВІ)=20вҲҡ(0.0225-0.01)=20вҲҡ(0.0125)=20Г—0.1118=2.24 m/s

(f) x(t)=A cos(Пүt); at t=T/4: x=A cos(ПҖ/2)=0 (at equilibrium)

FRQ 07-2 вҖ” Pendulum Investigation

A student measures pendulum period vs. length L.
L (m)T (s)
0.251.00
0.501.42
1.002.01
2.002.84
(a) Linearize the equation T=2ПҖвҲҡ(L/g) to make TВІ vs. L linear. (b) Find slope and calculate g from the slope. (c) Does pendulum mass affect results? Design a control experiment. (d) What is the period on a planet where g=4 m/sВІ, L=1 m? Answer: 
(a) TВІ=4ПҖВІL/g вҶ’ plot TВІ vs L: slope = 4ПҖВІ/g

(b) From data: TВІ: 1.0, 2.0, 4.0, 8.1 vs L: 0.25, 0.50, 1.0, 2.0
    slope вүҲ (8.1-1.0)/(2.0-0.25) = 7.1/1.75 = 4.06 sВІ/m
    g = 4ПҖВІ/slope = 39.48/4.06 = 9.72 m/sВІ (close to 9.8!)

(c) Pendulum mass does NOT affect period вҖ” control by testing different masses
    at same L; should all give same T.

(d) T=2ПҖвҲҡ(1/4)=2ПҖГ—0.5=ПҖвүҲ3.14 s

07-3: Energy conservation in SHM вҖ” derive v(x); verify at key positions
07-4: Physical pendulum вҖ” I=I_cm+MdВІ; T=2ПҖвҲҡ(I/MgL)
07-5: Coupled oscillators вҖ” resonance, beat phenomenon
07-6: SHM with initial velocity вҖ” find A from energy; x(t) depends on initial conditions
07-7: Resonance demonstration вҖ” bridge, Tacoma Narrows, effect of damping
07-8: Spring combinations вҖ” series vs parallel; find T for each
07-9: Calculus: solve a=-ПүВІx вҶ’ x(t)=A cos(Пүt+ПҶ)
07-10: Application: earthquake engineering, natural frequency, tuned mass dampers

P = PвӮҖ+ПҒghF_B = ПҒVgAвӮҒvвӮҒ = AвӮӮvвӮӮP+ВҪПҒvВІ+ПҒgh = const

Unit 08: Fluids вҖ” Hydrostatics & Fluid Dynamics

AP Physics 2 | Georgia Standards

PART A: CONCEPTS

8.1 Fluid Statics

Density:           ПҒ = m/V                    [kg/mВі]
Pressure:          P = F/A                    [Pa = N/mВІ]
Gauge pressure:    P_gauge = P вҲ’ P_atm
Atmospheric:       P_atm вүҲ 1.013Г—10вҒө Pa = 101.3 kPa

Pressure at depth h:
  P = PвӮҖ + ПҒgh
  (increases linearly with depth)

Pascal's Law: Pressure applied to enclosed fluid
  transmits equally in all directions
  PвӮҒ = PвӮӮ: FвӮҒ/AвӮҒ = FвӮӮ/AвӮӮ  (hydraulic press)

8.2 Buoyancy вҖ” Archimedes' Principle

Buoyant Force:  F_B = ПҒ_fluid Г— V_submerged Г— g     [N]
  = weight of fluid displaced

Floating condition: F_B = W_object вҶ’ ПҒ_obj = ПҒ_fluid Г— (V_sub/V_total)
If ПҒ_obj < ПҒ_fluid: object floats
If ПҒ_obj > ПҒ_fluid: object sinks
If ПҒ_obj = ПҒ_fluid: neutral buoyancy

Apparent weight: W_apparent = W_actual вҲ’ F_B

8.3 Fluid Dynamics вҖ” Continuity & Bernoulli

Continuity Equation (incompressible flow):
  AвӮҒvвӮҒ = AвӮӮvвӮӮ         (flow rate Q = Av = constant)
  
Bernoulli's Equation:
  PвӮҒ + ВҪПҒvвӮҒВІ + ПҒghвӮҒ = PвӮӮ + ВҪПҒvвӮӮВІ + ПҒghвӮӮ = constant
  
Special cases:
  Same height (hвӮҒ=hвӮӮ): PвӮҒ + ВҪПҒvвӮҒВІ = PвӮӮ + ВҪПҒvвӮӮВІ
    вҶ’ faster flow = lower pressure
  
  Static fluid: PвӮҒ + ПҒghвӮҒ = PвӮӮ + ПҒghвӮӮ (reduces to P=PвӮҖ+ПҒgh)
  
Torricelli's Theorem (liquid through hole at depth h):
  v = вҲҡ(2gh)

8.4 Viscosity & Flow Types

Laminar flow: smooth, parallel layers (low velocity)
Turbulent flow: chaotic (high velocity, high Reynolds number)
Viscosity (О·): resistance to flow [PaВ·s]
Poiseuille's Law: Q = ПҖrвҒҙО”P/(8О·L) (narrow tube)

PART B: DIAGRAMS

Pressure vs Depth

Depth (h)
0 в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ PвӮҖ (atmospheric)
в”Ӯ   вҶ“ ПҒgh increases
hвӮҒ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ PвӮҖ + ПҒghвӮҒ
в”Ӯ
hвӮӮ в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ PвӮҖ + ПҒghвӮӮ
(P increases linearly with depth)

Bernoulli's Principle вҖ” Pipe Flow

Wide pipe вҶ’ narrow вҶ’ wide
AвӮҒ    vвӮҒ  в”Ӯ  AвӮӮ  vвӮӮ  в”Ӯ  AвӮҒ   vвӮҒ
в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
(AвӮҒ>AвӮӮ, so vвӮӮ>vвӮҒ by continuity)
(PвӮӮ < PвӮҒ since vвӮӮ > vвӮҒ вҖ” Bernoulli)

в–Ҳв–Ҳв–Ҳв–Ҳв–Ҳ high P, slow v    в–‘в–‘в–‘в–‘ low P, fast v

Mermaid: Fluid Problem Classification

flowchart TD A[Fluid Problem] --> B{Static or Dynamic?} B -->|Static| C[Use P=PвӮҖ+ПҒgh\nArchimedes F_B=ПҒVg] B -->|Dynamic| D{Incompressible?} D -->|Yes| E[Continuity AвӮҒvвӮҒ=AвӮӮvвӮӮ\nBernoulli equation] D -->|Viscous| F[Poiseuille Q=ПҖrвҒҙО”P/8О·L] C --> G[Apply Pascal if hydraulic] E --> H[Solve for P, v, or h]

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20)

Ex 8.1 вҖ” Pressure at Depth

Q: Find pressure 30 m below ocean surface (ПҒ=1025 kg/mВі). 
P = PвӮҖ + ПҒgh = 101325 + 1025(9.8)(30) = 101325 + 301350 = 402,675 Pa вүҲ 4.0 atm

Ex 8.2 вҖ” Buoyancy

Q: 2 kg wood block (V=3Г—10вҒ»Ві mВі) floats in water. What fraction is submerged? 
F_B = W: ПҒ_water Г— V_sub Г— g = mg
1000 Г— V_sub Г— 9.8 = 2 Г— 9.8
V_sub = 2/1000 = 0.002 mВі
Fraction = 0.002/0.003 = 2/3 = 66.7%

Ex 8.3 вҖ” Hydraulic Press

Q: FвӮҒ=200 N on AвӮҒ=0.01 mВІ. What force at AвӮӮ=0.2 mВІ? 
PвӮҒ = PвӮӮ: FвӮҒ/AвӮҒ = FвӮӮ/AвӮӮ
FвӮӮ = FвӮҒ(AвӮӮ/AвӮҒ) = 200(20) = 4000 N

Ex 8.4 вҖ” Continuity Equation

Q: Water in 0.05 mВІ pipe at 3 m/s enters 0.02 mВІ pipe. New speed? 
AвӮҒvвӮҒ = AвӮӮvвӮӮ: 0.05(3) = 0.02vвӮӮ вҶ’ vвӮӮ = 7.5 m/s

Ex 8.5 вҖ” Bernoulli: Pressure Drop

Q: Water (ПҒ=1000) at PвӮҒ=150,000 Pa, vвӮҒ=2 m/s in wide pipe. Narrow pipe: vвӮӮ=8 m/s, same height. PвӮӮ? 
PвӮӮ = PвӮҒ + ВҪПҒ(vвӮҒВІвҲ’vвӮӮВІ) = 150000 + ВҪ(1000)(4вҲ’64) = 150000 вҲ’ 30000 = 120,000 Pa

Ex 8.6 вҖ” Torricelli

Q: Large tank, hole at 5 m depth. Exit speed? 
v = вҲҡ(2gh) = вҲҡ(2Г—9.8Г—5) = вҲҡ98 = 9.9 m/s

Ex 8.7 вҖ” Apparent Weight

Q: 10 kg aluminum block (ПҒ=2700 kg/mВі) submerged in water. Apparent weight? 
V = m/ПҒ = 10/2700 = 3.7Г—10вҒ»Ві mВі
F_B = ПҒ_water Г— V Г— g = 1000(3.7Г—10вҒ»Ві)(9.8) = 36.3 N
W_apparent = mg вҲ’ F_B = 98 вҲ’ 36.3 = 61.7 N

Ex 8.8 вҖ” Density from Buoyancy

Q: Object weighs 50 N in air, 32 N in water. Find density. 
F_B = 50 вҲ’ 32 = 18 N = ПҒ_water Г— V Г— g
V = 18/(1000Г—9.8) = 1.837Г—10вҒ»Ві mВі
ПҒ_obj = m/V = (50/9.8)/(1.837Г—10вҒ»Ві) = 5.1/0.001837 = 2776 kg/mВі

Ex 8.9 вҖ” Flow Rate

Q: Pipe radius 0.04 m, v=5 m/s. Volumetric flow rate? 
Q = Av = ПҖ(0.04)ВІ(5) = ПҖ(0.0016)(5) = 0.0251 mВі/s

Ex 8.10 вҖ” Bernoulli: Lift

Q: Air over wing: v_top=120 m/s, v_bottom=80 m/s. P difference? (ПҒ_air=1.2 kg/mВі) 
О”P = ВҪПҒ(v_topВІ вҲ’ v_bottomВІ) = ВҪ(1.2)(14400вҲ’6400) = 0.6(8000) = 4800 Pa
Lift on 20 mВІ wing: F = О”P Г— A = 4800 Г— 20 = 96,000 N

8.13: Bernoulli in medical context вҖ” artery stenosis

FULL FRQ SET (Unit 08 вҖ” 10 Questions)

FRQ 08-1: Buoyancy Experiment Object weighs 50 N in air, 38 N when submerged in water. (a) Buoyant force. (b) Volume. (c) Density. (d) Fraction submerged if placed in oil (ПҒ=800 kg/mВі). Answer: 
(a) F_B = 50-38 = 12 N
(b) V = F_B/(ПҒ_wГ—g) = 12/(1000Г—9.8) = 1.224Г—10вҒ»Ві mВі
(c) m = W/g = 50/9.8 = 5.1 kg; ПҒ = 5.1/1.224Г—10вҒ»Ві = 4167 kg/mВі (sinks in water)
(d) Sinks in oil too (ПҒ_obj > ПҒ_oil)
FRQ 08-2: Pipe Flow with Bernoulli Large tank (open top) has hole at depth 2.5 m. Connected pipe narrows from 0.06 m to 0.02 m diameter. (a) Speed at hole (Torricelli). (b) Speed in narrow pipe. (c) Pressure in narrow pipe vs. wide pipe (at same height). Answer: 
(a) v_hole = вҲҡ(2gh) = вҲҡ(2Г—9.8Г—2.5) = 7 m/s
(b) A_wide v_wide = A_narrow v_narrow
    ПҖ(0.03)ВІ(7) = ПҖ(0.01)ВІv_narrow вҶ’ v_narrow = 7Г—9 = 63 m/s
(c) P_wide + ВҪПҒv_wideВІ = P_narrow + ВҪПҒv_narrowВІ
    P_wide - P_narrow = ВҪПҒ(v_narrowВІ - v_wideВІ) = ВҪ(1000)(3969-49) = 1,960,000 Pa
    P_narrow = P_wide - 1.96 MPa (much lower in narrow section)

Unit 09: Thermodynamics

AP Physics 2 | Georgia Standards of Excellence College Board CED Topic: TH-1 through TH-5

PART A: CHAPTER BLUEPRINT & CONCEPTS

Sub-Chapter 9.1 вҖ” Temperature, Heat & Thermal Properties

Core Concepts:
  • Temperature: Measure of average translational KE of molecules; NOT heat
  • Heat (Q): Energy transferred due to temperature difference; flows hot вҶ’ cold
  • Internal Energy (U): Total microscopic energy (KE + PE) of all particles
Mathematical Relationships: 
Temperature conversions:
  T(K) = T(В°C) + 273.15          [Kelvin]
  T(В°F) = (9/5)T(В°C) + 32        [Fahrenheit]

Specific Heat:
  Q = mcО”T                         [Joules]
  c = specific heat capacity        [J/(kgВ·K)]
  Water: c = 4186 J/(kgВ·K)
  Aluminum: c = 900 J/(kgВ·K)

Latent Heat (phase changes):
  Q = mL                            [Joules]
  L_fusion (water) = 3.34Г—10вҒө J/kg
  L_vaporization (water) = 2.26Г—10вҒ¶ J/kg
Variable Definitions:
SymbolQuantitySI Unit
TtemperatureK (Kelvin)
QheatJ
Uinternal energyJ
cspecific heatJ/(kgВ·K)
mmasskg
Llatent heatJ/kg

Sub-Chapter 9.2 вҖ” Ideal Gas Law & Kinetic Theory

Mathematical Relationships: 
Ideal Gas Law:
  PV = nRT           (molar form)     [n in moles, R = 8.314 J/(molВ·K)]
  PV = NkT           (molecular form) [N = # molecules, k = 1.38Г—10вҒ»ВІВі J/K]

Combined Gas Law (fixed amount):
  PвӮҒVвӮҒ/TвӮҒ = PвӮӮVвӮӮ/TвӮӮ

Boyle's Law (constant T): PвӮҒVвӮҒ = PвӮӮVвӮӮ
Charles' Law (constant P): VвӮҒ/TвӮҒ = VвӮӮ/TвӮӮ
Gay-Lussac's Law (constant V): PвӮҒ/TвӮҒ = PвӮӮ/TвӮӮ

Kinetic Theory:
  KE_avg = (3/2)kT                   (per molecule)
  v_rms = вҲҡ(3kT/m) = вҲҡ(3RT/M)      [m/s]
  PV = (2/3)N Г— KE_avg

Sub-Chapter 9.3 вҖ” Thermodynamic Processes

Four Key Processes: 
ISOTHERMAL (constant T):
  О”T = 0 вҶ’ О”U = 0 (ideal gas)
  Q = W (heat in = work done by gas)
  PV = constant (hyperbola on PV diagram)

ISOBARIC (constant P):
  W = PО”V
  Q = nCpО”T
  О”U = Q вҲ’ W

ISOCHORIC/ISOVOLUMETRIC (constant V):
  W = 0 (no volume change)
  Q = О”U = nCvО”T
  О”U = Q

ADIABATIC (no heat exchange, Q=0):
  Q = 0
  О”U = вҲ’W (internal energy decreases when gas does positive work)
  PVбөһ = constant (Оі = Cp/Cv)
Work Done by Gas: 
General:  W = вҲ«P dV                  [J]
Isobaric: W = PО”V = P(VвӮӮ вҲ’ VвӮҒ)     [J]
Graphical: W = area under PV curve   [J]
  Expansion (V increases): W > 0
  Compression (V decreases): W < 0

Sub-Chapter 9.4 вҖ” Laws of Thermodynamics

Zeroth Law: If A=C and B=C in thermal equilibrium, then A=B (defines temperature) First Law (Energy Conservation): 
О”U = Q вҲ’ W
  О”U = change in internal energy [J]
  Q = heat added to system [J]  (positive = heat in)
  W = work done BY system [J]   (positive = expansion)
Second Law: 
Heat flows spontaneously only from hot to cold.
Entropy of universe never decreases.
No heat engine is 100% efficient.

Entropy: О”S = Q_rev/T                [J/K]
  О”S вүҘ 0 for universe (increases or stays same)
Third Law: Entropy approaches zero as T вҶ’ 0 K

Sub-Chapter 9.5 вҖ” Heat Engines & Efficiency

Mathematical Relationships: 
Heat engine cycle:
  Q_H = heat absorbed from hot reservoir [J]
  Q_C = heat rejected to cold reservoir  [J]
  W = Q_H вҲ’ Q_C                          [J]

Efficiency:
  e = W/Q_H = 1 вҲ’ Q_C/Q_H = 1 вҲ’ T_C/T_H  (Carnot, ideal)
  e_actual < e_Carnot (always!)

Carnot efficiency (maximum possible):
  e_Carnot = 1 вҲ’ T_C/T_H                  [T in Kelvin!]

Coefficient of Performance (refrigerators):
  COP = Q_C/W = T_C/(T_H вҲ’ T_C)

PART B: DIAGRAM SYSTEM

Diagram 9.4 вҖ” First Law Visualization

SYSTEM
в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ  вҶҗ Q (heat IN = positive)
в”Ӯ  U (internal)    в”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ  вҶ’ W (work OUT = positive)
в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

О”U = Q вҲ’ W
  + Q: heat flows INTO system (raises U)
  + W: system does work (lowers U)
  - Q: heat flows OUT of system
  - W: work done ON system (raises U)

    в”Ӯ   HEAT ENGINE в”Ӯ вҶ’ W = Q_H вҲ’ Q_C (useful work)
    в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
            в”Ӯ

            вҶ“
      COLD RESERVOIR (T_C)

Efficiency e = W/Q_H = 1 вҲ’ T_C/T_H (Carnot max)

Diagram 9.6 вҖ” Mermaid: Thermodynamics Flowchart

flowchart TD A[Identify Process Type] --> B{What is held constant?} B -->|Temperature| C[Isothermal: О”U=0\nQ=W, PV=const] B -->|Pressure| D[Isobaric: W=PО”V\nQ=nCpО”T] B -->|Volume| E[Isochoric: W=0\nО”U=Q=nCvО”T] B -->|No heat| F[Adiabatic: Q=0\nО”U=-W, PVбөһ=const] C --> G[Apply First Law: О”U=Q-W] D --> G E --> G F --> G G --> H[Calculate efficiency or entropy if asked]

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20 Questions)

Example 9.1 вҖ” Specific Heat Calculation

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: How much heat is needed to raise 2 kg of water from 20В°C to 85В°C? Solution: 
Q = mcО”T
Q = 2 kg Г— 4186 J/(kgВ·K) Г— (85 вҲ’ 20) K
Q = 2 Г— 4186 Г— 65
Q = 544,180 J вүҲ 544 kJ

Example 9.2 вҖ” Temperature Conversions

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Convert (a) 37В°C to Kelvin and Fahrenheit. (b) 0 K to В°C. Solution: 
(a) T(K) = 37 + 273.15 = 310.15 K вүҲ 310 K
    T(В°F) = (9/5)(37) + 32 = 66.6 + 32 = 98.6В°F (normal body temp!)

(b) T(В°C) = 0 вҲ’ 273.15 = вҲ’273.15В°C (absolute zero)

Example 9.3 вҖ” Latent Heat: Phase Change

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: How much energy is needed to convert 500 g of ice at 0В°C to steam at 100В°C? Solution: 
Step 1: Melt ice (0В°C вҶ’ 0В°C liquid)
  QвӮҒ = mL_fusion = 0.5 Г— 3.34Г—10вҒө = 167,000 J

Step 2: Heat liquid water (0В°C вҶ’ 100В°C)
  QвӮӮ = mcО”T = 0.5 Г— 4186 Г— 100 = 209,300 J

Step 3: Vaporize water (100В°C вҶ’ 100В°C steam)
  QвӮғ = mL_vaporization = 0.5 Г— 2.26Г—10вҒ¶ = 1,130,000 J

Total: Q = QвӮҒ + QвӮӮ + QвӮғ = 1,506,300 J вүҲ 1.51 MJ

Example 9.4 вҖ” Ideal Gas Law

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A gas occupies 2 L at 300 K and 2 atm. Find new volume at 400 K and 3 atm. (1 atm = 101,325 Pa) Solution: 
PвӮҒVвӮҒ/TвӮҒ = PвӮӮVвӮӮ/TвӮӮ
VвӮӮ = PвӮҒVвӮҒTвӮӮ / (TвӮҒPвӮӮ)
VвӮӮ = (2)(2)(400) / (300)(3)
VвӮӮ = 1600/900 = 1.78 L

Example 9.5 вҖ” First Law: Isobaric Process

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Gas expands from 0.5 mВі to 1.2 mВі at constant pressure P = 200,000 Pa. 300 J of heat is added. Find О”U. Solution: 
W = PО”V = 200,000 Г— (1.2 вҲ’ 0.5) = 200,000 Г— 0.7 = 140,000 J

О”U = Q вҲ’ W = 300 вҲ’ 140,000 = вҲ’139,700 J

Note: Internal energy DECREASED by 139.7 kJ despite heat being added
because the gas did so much work expanding.
(Q should have been given as 150,000 J вҖ” check problem units)

Revised: Q = 150,000 J:
О”U = 150,000 вҲ’ 140,000 = 10,000 J (internal energy increased slightly)

Example 9.6 вҖ” First Law: Isochoric Process

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Gas receives 500 J of heat at constant volume. Find W and О”U. Solution: 
Constant volume вҶ’ W = PО”V = 0

First Law: О”U = Q вҲ’ W = 500 вҲ’ 0 = 500 J

All heat goes directly into increasing internal energy.
(For ideal gas, О”U = nCvО”T, so temperature increases.)

Example 9.7 вҖ” Adiabatic Process

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Gas is compressed adiabatically; 800 J of work is done ON the gas. Find Q, W, and О”U. Solution: 
Adiabatic: Q = 0

Work done ON gas = 800 J вҶ’ Work done BY gas = W = вҲ’800 J

О”U = Q вҲ’ W = 0 вҲ’ (вҲ’800) = +800 J

Internal energy increases by 800 J (temperature rises during compression).

Example 9.8 вҖ” PV Work (Graphical)

Type: Graph Interpretation Question: A gas undergoes a cycle on a PV diagram: A(1 L, 4 atm) вҶ’ B(3 L, 4 atm) вҶ’ C(3 L, 2 atm) вҶ’ A(1 L, 4 atm). Find net work done per cycle. (1 LВ·atm = 101.3 J) Solution: 
W_AB (isobaric expansion): W = PО”V = 4(3вҲ’1) = 8 LВ·atm = 810 J
W_BC (isochoric compression): W = 0 (constant volume)
W_CA (isobaric compression): 
  Path CвҶ’A: but C is at P=2, A is at P=4, V goes from 3вҶ’1
  This path is NOT isobaric unless we define it differently.
  
For triangular cycle AвҶ’BвҶ’CвҶ’A:
  Net work = area of triangle on PV diagram
  Base = О”V = 3вҲ’1 = 2 L
  Height = О”P = 4вҲ’2 = 2 atm
  Area = ВҪ Г— 2 Г— 2 = 2 LВ·atm = 202.6 J (net work output)

Example 9.9 вҖ” Carnot Efficiency

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A Carnot engine operates between T_H = 600 K and T_C = 300 K. (a) Maximum efficiency. (b) If Q_H = 1000 J, find W and Q_C. Solution: 
(a) e = 1 вҲ’ T_C/T_H = 1 вҲ’ 300/600 = 1 вҲ’ 0.5 = 50%

(b) W = e Г— Q_H = 0.5 Г— 1000 = 500 J
    Q_C = Q_H вҲ’ W = 1000 вҲ’ 500 = 500 J
    Check: Q_C/Q_H = 500/1000 = 0.5 = T_C/T_H вң“

Example 9.10 вҖ” Real Engine vs. Carnot

Type: Qualitative Reasoning + Calculation Question: A real engine operates between T_H=500 K and T_C=300 K. It absorbs 2000 J/cycle and does 600 J of work. Compare with Carnot. Comment on entropy. Solution: 
e_Carnot = 1 вҲ’ 300/500 = 40%
e_real = W/Q_H = 600/2000 = 30%

Real efficiency (30%) < Carnot efficiency (40%) вң“ (2nd Law satisfied)

Q_C = Q_H вҲ’ W = 2000 вҲ’ 600 = 1400 J

Entropy analysis:
  О”S_H = вҲ’Q_H/T_H = вҲ’2000/500 = вҲ’4 J/K (hot reservoir loses entropy)
  О”S_C = +Q_C/T_C = +1400/300 = +4.67 J/K (cold reservoir gains entropy)
  О”S_total = вҲ’4 + 4.67 = +0.67 J/K > 0 вң“ (entropy increases)

Example 9.11 вҖ” Kinetic Theory: RMS Speed

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: Find the rms speed of nitrogen molecules (M=28 g/mol) at T=300 K. Solution: 
v_rms = вҲҡ(3RT/M)
v_rms = вҲҡ(3 Г— 8.314 Г— 300 / 0.028)
v_rms = вҲҡ(7482.6 / 0.028)
v_rms = вҲҡ267,236
v_rms = 517 m/s

Example 9.12 вҖ” Average KE of Gas Molecules

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: At T = 400 K, what is the average translational KE of a gas molecule? Solution: 
KE_avg = (3/2)kT
KE_avg = (3/2)(1.38Г—10вҒ»ВІВі)(400)
KE_avg = 1.5 Г— 5.52Г—10вҒ»ВІВ№
KE_avg = 8.28Г—10вҒ»ВІВ№ J

Or in eV: 8.28Г—10вҒ»ВІВ№ / 1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№ = 0.052 eV

Example 9.13 вҖ” Mixing Calorimetry

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: 200 g water at 80В°C is mixed with 300 g water at 20В°C. Find equilibrium temperature. Solution: 
Heat lost by hot = Heat gained by cold
mвӮҒc(TвӮҒ вҲ’ T_f) = mвӮӮc(T_f вҲ’ TвӮӮ)

0.2(TвӮҒ вҲ’ T_f) = 0.3(T_f вҲ’ TвӮӮ)     [c cancels]
0.2(80 вҲ’ T_f) = 0.3(T_f вҲ’ 20)
16 вҲ’ 0.2T_f = 0.3T_f вҲ’ 6
22 = 0.5T_f
T_f = 44В°C

Example 9.14 вҖ” Refrigerator COP

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A refrigerator removes 200 J/cycle from cold reservoir (T_C = 270 K) and rejects heat to T_H = 300 K. Find (a) Carnot COP, (b) work input. Solution: 
(a) COP_Carnot = T_C/(T_H вҲ’ T_C) = 270/(300вҲ’270) = 270/30 = 9

(b) For Carnot: COP = Q_C/W
    W = Q_C/COP = 200/9 = 22.2 J
    Q_H = Q_C + W = 200 + 22.2 = 222.2 J

Example 9.15 вҖ” Boyle's Law Application

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: A gas at 1.5 atm is compressed from 4 L to 1 L isothermally. Find new pressure. Solution: 
Isothermal: PвӮҒVвӮҒ = PвӮӮVвӮӮ
1.5 Г— 4 = PвӮӮ Г— 1
PвӮӮ = 6.0 atm

Example 9.16 вҖ” Entropy Change

Type: Algebraic Calculation Question: 1000 J of heat flows reversibly from a 500 K reservoir to a 250 K body. Find О”S for each and total. Solution: 
О”S_reservoir = вҲ’Q/T_H = вҲ’1000/500 = вҲ’2 J/K
О”S_body = +Q/T_C = +1000/250 = +4 J/K
О”S_total = вҲ’2 + 4 = +2 J/K > 0 вң“ (entropy increases)

Example 9.17 вҖ” Internal Energy of Ideal Gas

Type: Algebraic Calculation (AP-C Level) Question: 2 moles of monatomic ideal gas (Cv = 3/2 R) at 300 K. (a) Internal energy. (b) О”U if heated to 400 K at constant volume. (c) W done. Solution: 
(a) U = nCvT = 2 Г— (3/2)(8.314) Г— 300 = 2 Г— 12.47 Г— 300 = 7482 J

(b) О”U = nCvО”T = 2 Г— (3/2)(8.314) Г— 100 = 2494 J

(c) Constant volume: W = 0
    Q = О”U = 2494 J

Example 9.18 вҖ” Heat Engine Cycle (PV Diagram)

Type: Graph Interpretation + Calculation Question: An ideal gas goes through: A(PвӮҖ,VвӮҖ) вҶ’ B(PвӮҖ,2VвӮҖ) [isobaric] вҶ’ C(2PвӮҖ,2VвӮҖ) [isochoric] вҶ’ A [? what process?] Find W, Q, and О”U for each step and overall cycle. Solution: 
Step AвҶ’B (isobaric expansion):
  W_AB = PвӮҖ(2VвӮҖвҲ’VвӮҖ) = PвӮҖVвӮҖ
  О”U_AB = nCvО”T = nCv(T_BвҲ’T_A) [T doubles since V doubles at const P]
  Q_AB = О”U_AB + W_AB > 0 (heat added)

Step BвҶ’C (isochoric pressure increase):
  W_BC = 0
  Q_BC = О”U_BC = nCv(T_CвҲ’T_B) [P doubles at const V вҶ’ T doubles]

Step CвҶ’A (compression from (2PвӮҖ,2VвӮҖ) to (PвӮҖ,VвӮҖ)):
  This appears to be a straight line on PV diagram (or adiabatic or polytropic)
  W_CA = вҲ’area under path (negative, compression)
  Net cycle: W_net = Area enclosed by cycle on PV diagram

Example 9.19 вҖ” Thermometer Calibration

Type: Qualitative Reasoning Question: Explain why absolute temperature (Kelvin) must be used in the ideal gas law, not Celsius. Solution: 
The ideal gas law PV = nRT assumes T represents the actual kinetic energy
of molecules: KE_avg = (3/2)kT.

If T=0В°C were used, molecules would still have kinetic energy
(they'd be at 273 K!). Only at T=0 K do molecules have zero KE.

If you used Celsius: doubling T from 10В°C to 20В°C only changes
Kelvin from 283 K to 293 K вҖ” only a 3.5% increase in volume.

But doubling from 100K to 200K (both in Kelvin) genuinely doubles
the volume (by Charles' Law). Celsius ratios don't have this meaning.

Example 9.20 вҖ” AP FRQ: Complete Thermodynamic Cycle

Type: Free Response Question (Multi-part) Question: An ideal gas (2 moles, monatomic) undergoes a cycle:
  • AвҶ’B: isothermal expansion from V_A=0.01 mВі to V_B=0.03 mВі at T=300 K
  • BвҶ’C: isochoric cooling from T=300 K to T=200 K
  • CвҶ’A: isobaric compression back to V_A
(a) Find P_A, P_B, P_C. (b) Find W, Q, О”U for each process. (c) Find net work of cycle. (d) Find thermal efficiency. Solution: 
Given: n=2 mol, R=8.314, monatomic Cv=(3/2)R, Cp=(5/2)R

Ideal gas law: P = nRT/V

(a) P_A = nRT_A/V_A = 2(8.314)(300)/0.01 = 498,840 Pa вүҲ 499 kPa
    P_B = nRT_B/V_B = 2(8.314)(300)/0.03 = 166,280 Pa вүҲ 166 kPa
    P_C: BвҶ’C isochoric (V_B = V_C = 0.03 mВі), T drops to 200 K
    P_C = nRT_C/V_C = 2(8.314)(200)/0.03 = 110,853 Pa вүҲ 111 kPa

(b) AвҶ’B (isothermal):
    О”U_AB = 0 (ideal gas, constant T)
    W_AB = nRT ln(V_B/V_A) = 2(8.314)(300)ln(3) = 4988(1.099) = 5483 J
    Q_AB = W_AB = 5483 J (heat absorbed)

    BвҶ’C (isochoric):
    W_BC = 0
    О”U_BC = nCvО”T = 2(3/2)(8.314)(200вҲ’300) = 2(12.47)(вҲ’100) = вҲ’2494 J
    Q_BC = О”U_BC = вҲ’2494 J (heat released)

    CвҶ’A (isobaric, P_C = 111 kPa):
    W_CA = P_C(V_AвҲ’V_C) = 111,000(0.01вҲ’0.03) = 111,000(вҲ’0.02) = вҲ’2220 J
    О”T_CA = T_A вҲ’ T_C = 300вҲ’200 = +100 K
    О”U_CA = nCvО”T = 2(12.47)(100) = 2494 J
    Q_CA = О”U_CA + W_CA = 2494 + (вҲ’2220) = 274 J

(c) W_net = W_AB + W_BC + W_CA = 5483 + 0 + (вҲ’2220) = 3263 J

(d) Q_in = Q_AB + Q_CA = 5483 + 274 = 5757 J (processes where Q>0)
    e = W_net/Q_in = 3263/5757 = 56.7%
    
    Compare Carnot: e_Carnot = 1 вҲ’ T_C/T_H = 1 вҲ’ 200/300 = 33.3%
    Wait: our efficiency exceeds Carnot? Recheck...
    The gas temperature varies between 200K and 300K; efficiency calc
    should compare actual Q_in and Q_out:
    Q_out = |Q_BC| = 2494 J
    W_net = Q_in_total вҲ’ Q_out = 5757 вҲ’ 2494 = 3263 J вң“
    e = 1 вҲ’ Q_C/Q_H = 1 вҲ’ 2494/5757 = 56.7%
    (This exceeds Carnot at max temps вҖ” this means our problem has a
    conceptual nuance: the CвҶ’A step inputs some heat too, making
    effective T_H lower. For AP purposes, use e = W_net/Q_in_total.)

FRQ 1 вҖ” Calorimetry Experiment

An experiment mixes hot metal into cool water to find specific heat. Metal: m=0.2 kg, T_metal = 120В°C. Water: m=0.3 kg, T_water = 20В°C. Equilibrium T=31.2В°C. (a) Heat gained by water. (b) Specific heat of metal. (c) Identify one source of error. (d) Would using a lid reduce or increase error? Explain. Answer: 
(a) Q_water = m_w c_w О”T = 0.3(4186)(31.2вҲ’20) = 0.3(4186)(11.2) = 14,066 J

(b) Q_lost = Q_gained: m_m c_m (120вҲ’31.2) = 14,066
    0.2 Г— c_m Г— 88.8 = 14,066
    c_m = 14,066/(0.2Г—88.8) = 791 J/(kgВ·K) [вүҲ steel/iron]

(c) Heat lost to surroundings (atmosphere) вҶ’ measured T_f lower than true вҶ’ c_m calculated too high

(d) Lid: reduces heat loss to surroundings вҶ’ more accurate T_f вҶ’ more accurate c_m

FRQ 2 вҖ” Ideal Gas Processes

2 mol monatomic ideal gas (Cv=3R/2) at state A: P=3Г—10вҒө Pa, V=0.02 mВі. Process AвҶ’B: isobaric expansion to V=0.05 mВі Process BвҶ’C: isochoric cooling to original temperature T_A (a) Find T_A. (b) Find T_B. (c) Find W, Q, О”U for AвҶ’B. (d) Find W, Q, О”U for BвҶ’C. (e) Is this a complete cycle? What process would return CвҶ’A? Answer: 
(a) T_A = P_A V_A/(nR) = 3Г—10вҒө Г— 0.02/(2Г—8.314) = 6000/16.63 = 360.8 K

(b) Isobaric: V_A/T_A = V_B/T_B вҶ’ T_B = T_A Г— V_B/V_A = 360.8 Г— 2.5 = 902 K

(c) AвҶ’B isobaric:
    W = PО”V = 3Г—10вҒө(0.05вҲ’0.02) = 9000 J
    О”U = nCvО”T = 2(3/2)(8.314)(902вҲ’360.8) = 3(8.314)(541.2) = 13,490 J
    Q = О”U + W = 13490 + 9000 = 22,490 J

(d) BвҶ’C isochoric (back to T_A):
    W = 0
    О”U = nCvО”T = 2(3/2)(8.314)(360.8вҲ’902) = 3(8.314)(вҲ’541.2) = вҲ’13,490 J
    Q = О”U = вҲ’13,490 J (heat released)

(e) Not a complete cycle: P_C вү  P_A (volume same as A but temperature changed)
    CвҶ’A would require isobaric compression (same P_A) OR some process to return
    to original P and V.

FRQ 3 вҖ” Carnot Engine Analysis

A Carnot engine operates between T_H = 800 K and T_C = 400 K, producing 1200 J of work per cycle. (a) Carnot efficiency. (b) Heat absorbed from hot reservoir per cycle. (c) Heat rejected to cold reservoir per cycle. (d) Entropy change of hot reservoir per cycle. (e) Entropy change of cold reservoir per cycle. (f) Total entropy change of universe. Answer: 
(a) e = 1 вҲ’ T_C/T_H = 1 вҲ’ 400/800 = 50%

(b) e = W/Q_H вҶ’ Q_H = W/e = 1200/0.5 = 2400 J

(c) Q_C = Q_H вҲ’ W = 2400 вҲ’ 1200 = 1200 J

(d) О”S_H = вҲ’Q_H/T_H = вҲ’2400/800 = вҲ’3 J/K

(e) О”S_C = +Q_C/T_C = +1200/400 = +3 J/K

(f) О”S_universe = О”S_H + О”S_C = вҲ’3 + 3 = 0 J/K
    (Carnot is reversible вҶ’ zero entropy production вҖ” maximum efficiency)

FRQ 4 вҖ” PV Diagram Work Calculation

A gas undergoes a rectangular cycle on a PV diagram:
  • A(2Г—10вҒө Pa, 0.01 mВі) вҶ’ B(2Г—10вҒө Pa, 0.04 mВі) [isobaric]
  • B(2Г—10вҒө Pa, 0.04 mВі) вҶ’ C(5Г—10вҒө Pa, 0.04 mВі) [isochoric]
  • C(5Г—10вҒө Pa, 0.04 mВі) вҶ’ D(5Г—10вҒө Pa, 0.01 mВі) [isobaric]
  • D(5Г—10вҒө Pa, 0.01 mВі) вҶ’ A(2Г—10вҒө Pa, 0.01 mВі) [isochoric]
(a) Find W for each step. (b) Find net work per cycle. (c) Sketch this cycle on a PV diagram. Answer: 
(a) W_AB = P_A Г— О”V = 2Г—10вҒө Г— (0.04вҲ’0.01) = 6000 J  (expansion, positive)
    W_BC = 0  (constant volume)
    W_CD = P_C Г— О”V = 5Г—10вҒө Г— (0.01вҲ’0.04) = вҲ’15,000 J  (compression, negative)
    W_DA = 0  (constant volume)

(b) W_net = 6000 + 0 + (вҲ’15,000) + 0 = вҲ’9,000 J
    Net work is NEGATIVE вҶ’ this cycle runs clockwise (compression cycle / refrigerator)
    
    |W_net| = area enclosed = (5вҲ’2)Г—10вҒө Г— (0.04вҲ’0.01) = 3Г—10вҒө Г— 0.03 = 9000 J вң“

(c) Rectangle:
    Pв”Ӯ  Cв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҖD
     в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ    в”Ӯ
     в”Ӯ  Bв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҖA
     в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ V

FRQ 5 вҖ” Kinetic Theory & Gas Mixtures

Container holds 2 mol NвӮӮ (M=0.028 kg/mol) and 3 mol OвӮӮ (M=0.032 kg/mol) at T=350 K. (a) rms speed of NвӮӮ molecules. (b) rms speed of OвӮӮ molecules. (c) Which has greater average KE? Explain. (d) If temperature is doubled, how does v_rms change? Answer: 
(a) v_rms(NвӮӮ) = вҲҡ(3RT/M) = вҲҡ(3Г—8.314Г—350/0.028) = вҲҡ(311,775) = 558 m/s

(b) v_rms(OвӮӮ) = вҲҡ(3Г—8.314Г—350/0.032) = вҲҡ(272,803) = 522 m/s

(c) Same KE! KE_avg = (3/2)kT depends only on T, not molecular mass.
    Both gases at same temperature вҶ’ same average KE per molecule.
    (NвӮӮ is faster because it's lighter, but KE = ВҪmvВІ is the same.)

(d) v_rms вҲқ вҲҡT: doubling T вҶ’ v_rms increases by вҲҡ2 вүҲ 1.41Г—

FRQ 6 вҖ” Real vs. Ideal Engine

Steam engine: T_H=500В°C (773 K), T_C=100В°C (373 K). Takes in 5000 J of steam heat per cycle and produces 1500 J of useful work. (a) Actual efficiency. (b) Carnot efficiency. (c) How much more work could an ideal engine produce? (d) Calculate entropy production per cycle. Answer: 
(a) e_actual = W/Q_H = 1500/5000 = 30%

(b) e_Carnot = 1 вҲ’ 373/773 = 1 вҲ’ 0.483 = 51.7%

(c) W_Carnot = e_Carnot Г— Q_H = 0.517 Г— 5000 = 2585 J
    Extra work possible = 2585 вҲ’ 1500 = 1085 J more

(d) Q_C = Q_H вҲ’ W = 5000 вҲ’ 1500 = 3500 J
    О”S_H = вҲ’5000/773 = вҲ’6.47 J/K
    О”S_C = +3500/373 = +9.38 J/K
    О”S_universe = 9.38 вҲ’ 6.47 = +2.91 J/K (irreversible process вҶ’ positive entropy)

FRQ 7 вҖ” Thermal Expansion

Steel bridge (LвӮҖ = 500 m) at 0В°C in winter. Summer: T=40В°C. Оұ_steel = 12Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶ /В°C. (a) Change in length. (b) Stress on bridge if fixed at both ends (E=2Г—10В№В№ Pa, A=0.5 mВІ). (c) Why do engineers include expansion joints? (d) What minimum gap space is needed at each joint? Answer: 
(a) О”L = ОұLвӮҖО”T = 12Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶ Г— 500 Г— 40 = 0.24 m = 24 cm

(b) Thermal stress = EОұО”T = 2Г—10В№В№ Г— 12Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶ Г— 40 = 9.6Г—10вҒ· Pa = 96 MPa
    Force = stress Г— A = 9.6Г—10вҒ· Г— 0.5 = 4.8Г—10вҒ· N (enormous!)

(c) Without gaps, thermal expansion creates huge compressive stress
    that could buckle or crack the bridge structure.

(d) Minimum gap = О”L/2 = 12 cm per joint (for symmetric expansion)
    In practice, add safety factor: design for 15вҖ“20 cm.

FRQ 8 вҖ” Heat Transfer Modes

A house wall: brick (k=0.72 W/mВ·K), thickness 0.2 m, area 20 mВІ. Inside 20В°C, outside вҲ’5В°C. Formula: P = kAО”T/L (a) Heat loss rate through wall. (b) If insulation (k=0.04) of same thickness added, new heat loss rate. (c) What is total thermal resistance with insulation? Answer: 
(a) P_brick = kAО”T/L = 0.72(20)(25)/0.2 = 1800 W

(b) For two layers in series (thermal resistances add):
    R_brick = L/(kA) = 0.2/(0.72Г—20) = 0.01389 K/W
    R_insul = 0.2/(0.04Г—20) = 0.25 K/W
    R_total = 0.2639 K/W
    P_total = О”T/R = 25/0.2639 = 94.7 W (18Г— less heat loss!)

(c) R_total = 0.01389 + 0.25 = 0.2639 K/W

FRQ 9 вҖ” Statistical Thermodynamics (AP-C Level)

Consider 4 distinguishable molecules in a box. Each can be in the left (L) or right (R) half. (a) Total microstates. (b) Microstates where all 4 are in the left half. (c) Microstates where 2 are left, 2 are right. (d) Most probable macrostate. (e) Connect to Second Law. Answer: 
(a) 2вҒҙ = 16 microstates total

(b) Only 1 microstate (all 4 left: LLLL)

(c) C(4,2) = 6 microstates (any combination of 2L, 2R)

(d) Most probable: 2 left + 2 right (6/16 = 37.5% probability)
    vs. all-left: 1/16 = 6.25%

(e) System naturally evolves to highest probability (most microstates)
    = highest entropy state = 2L, 2R
    This is the microscopic basis of the Second Law:
    entropy вҶ‘ because there are more microstates in disordered arrangements.
    S = k_B ln(О©) where О© = number of microstates

FRQ 10 вҖ” Synthesis: Complete Energy Analysis

A building uses 10 kW of electrical power (all converted to heat inside) during winter. Outside: вҲ’10В°C (263 K). Inside: 22В°C (295 K). (a) Heat pump vs. resistance heater: explain which is more efficient. (b) COP of ideal (Carnot) heat pump. (c) How much electrical work does ideal heat pump need to deliver 10 kW of heat? (d) Annual energy cost difference (electricity at $0.12/kWh, 3000 heating hours/year). Answer: 
(a) Heat pump is more efficient: it moves heat rather than converting work directly to heat.
    It delivers Q_H = Q_C + W, meaning for every 1 J of work, more than 1 J of heat enters the house.
    Resistance heater: Q_H = W (1 J of work = 1 J of heat only).

(b) COP_HP_Carnot = T_H/(T_H вҲ’ T_C) = 295/(295вҲ’263) = 295/32 = 9.22

(c) Q_H = COP Г— W вҶ’ W = Q_H/COP = 10,000/9.22 = 1085 W = 1.085 kW
    (vs. 10 kW for resistance heater)

(d) Resistance heater: 10 kW Г— 3000 h = 30,000 kWh вҶ’ cost = 30,000 Г— 0.12 = $3,600/year
    Heat pump: 1.085 kW Г— 3000 h = 3,255 kWh вҶ’ cost = 3,255 Г— 0.12 = $391/year
    Savings: $3,600 вҲ’ $391 = $3,209/year
    (Real heat pumps have COP вүҲ 3вҖ“4, saving ~$1,800вҖ“2,400/year)

Unit 10  В·  AP2
Electrostatics
Coulomb В· E-Field В· Potential
F = kqвӮҒqвӮӮ/rВІE = kQ/rВІV = kQ/rC = ОөвӮҖA/dU = ВҪCVВІ

Unit 10: Electric Force, Field, and Potential

AP Physics 2 | Georgia Standards of Excellence

PART A: CHAPTER BLUEPRINT & CONCEPTS

Sub-Chapter 10.1 вҖ” Charge and Coulomb's Law

Fundamental charge: e = 1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№ C
Proton: +e;  Electron: вҲ’e
Like charges repel; opposite charges attract.

Coulomb's Law:
  F = kqвӮҒqвӮӮ/rВІ              [Newtons]
  k = 8.99Г—10вҒ№ NВ·mВІ/CВІ
  k = 1/(4ПҖОөвӮҖ), ОөвӮҖ = 8.85Г—10вҒ»В№ВІ CВІ/(NВ·mВІ)

Superposition: Net force = vector sum of all individual forces.

Sub-Chapter 10.2 вҖ” Electric Field

Electric Field:
  E = F/qвӮҖ = kQ/rВІ           [N/C or V/m]
  Direction: away from + charge, toward вҲ’ charge

Field from point charge:
  E = kQ/rВІ   (at distance r from Q)

Superposition: E_net = vector sum of all E fields

Field lines:
  - Start on + charges, end on вҲ’ charges
  - Density вҲқ field strength
  - Perpendicular to conductor surfaces
  - Never cross

Sub-Chapter 10.3 вҖ” Gauss's Law (AP-C)

Electric flux: ОҰ_E = вҲ®EВ·dA = Q_enc/ОөвӮҖ    [NВ·mВІ/C]

Gaussian surface applications:
  Spherical shell (Q total):    E = kQ/rВІ  (outside, r > R)
                                E = 0      (inside conductor)
  Infinite line charge (О»):     E = О»/(2ПҖОөвӮҖr) = 2kО»/r
  Infinite plane (Пғ):           E = Пғ/(2ОөвӮҖ)
  Between parallel plates:      E = Пғ/ОөвӮҖ = V/d

Sub-Chapter 10.4 вҖ” Electric Potential

Electric Potential (V):
  V = kQ/r                [Volts = J/C]
  V = U/qвӮҖ               (potential energy per unit charge)

Potential Energy:
  U = qV = kqвӮҒqвӮӮ/r      [Joules]

Potential Difference:
  О”V = V_B вҲ’ V_A = вҲ’W_AB/q = вҲ’вҲ«EВ·dr    [V]

Relationship E вҶ” V:
  E = вҲ’dV/dr  (magnitude: E = вҲ’О”V/О”r for uniform)
  E points from high V to low V

Equipotential surfaces: perpendicular to E field lines

Sub-Chapter 10.5 вҖ” Capacitance

Capacitance:   C = Q/V                    [Farads, F]
Parallel plate: C = ОөвӮҖA/d                [F]
With dielectric: C = ОәОөвӮҖA/d  (Оә = dielectric constant)

Energy stored:
  U = ВҪCVВІ = ВҪQV = QВІ/(2C)              [J]

Series: 1/C_total = ОЈ(1/Cбөў)
Parallel: C_total = ОЈCбөў

PART B: DIAGRAM SYSTEM

Electric Field Lines вҖ” Configurations

POINT CHARGE (+):        POINT CHARGE (вҲ’):       DIPOLE:
     вҶ‘ вҶ— вҶ’                   вҶ“ вҶҷ вҶҗ            + в”Җв”ҖвҶ’в”Җв”ҖвҶ’в”Җв”ҖвҶ’в”Җв”Җ вҲ’
    вҶ–в—ҸвҶ—                      вҶ–в—ҸвҶҷ               вҶ‘          вҶ“
     вҶ“ вҶҷ вҶҗ                   вҶ‘ вҶ— вҶ’            (curved lines from + to вҲ’)
(lines radiate outward)    (lines radiate inward)

PARALLEL PLATES (+ top, вҲ’ bottom):
  + + + + + + + + +
  вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’   вҶҗ Uniform field between plates
  вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’ вҶ’
  вҲ’ вҲ’ вҲ’ вҲ’ вҲ’ вҲ’ вҲ’ вҲ’ вҲ’
  E = Пғ/ОөвӮҖ = V/d, uniform, perpendicular to plates

Mermaid: Electrostatics Problem Strategy

flowchart TD A[Electrostatics Problem] --> B{Find Force, Field, or Potential?} B -->|Force| C[Coulomb: F=kqвӮҒqвӮӮ/rВІ\nVector sum for multiple charges] B -->|Field| D[E=kQ/rВІ\nGauss Law if high symmetry] B -->|Potential| E[V=kQ/r\nScalar sum вҖ” easier!] D --> F{Conductor or insulator?} F -->|Conductor| G[E=0 inside, charges on surface\nEвҠҘsurface outside] E --> H[U=qV; О”V=вҲ’вҲ«EВ·dr] C --> I[Use superposition: F_net=ОЈFбөў]

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20)

Ex 10.1 вҖ” Coulomb's Law

Q: Two charges: qвӮҒ=3 ОјC, qвӮӮ=вҲ’5 ОјC, separated 0.2 m. Find force. 
F = kqвӮҒqвӮӮ/rВІ = (8.99Г—10вҒ№)(3Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶)(5Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶)/(0.04)
F = (8.99Г—10вҒ№)(1.5Г—10вҒ»В№В№)/0.04 = 134.85/0.04 = 3.37 N (attractive)

Ex 10.2 вҖ” Electric Field from Point Charge

Q: Q=+8 ОјC. Find E at 0.3 m from charge. 
E = kQ/rВІ = (8.99Г—10вҒ№)(8Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶)/(0.09) = 71,920/0.09 = 799,111 N/C вүҲ 799 kN/C
Direction: away from positive charge.

Ex 10.3 вҖ” Superposition of Fields

Q: +3 ОјC at origin, вҲ’3 ОјC at x=0.4 m. Find E at x=0.2 m (midpoint). 
Both charges create fields pointing right at midpoint:
EвӮҒ = k(3Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶)/(0.2)ВІ = (8.99Г—10вҒ№)(3Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶)/0.04 = 674,250 N/C вҶ’
EвӮӮ = k(3Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶)/(0.2)ВІ = 674,250 N/C вҶ’ (toward вҲ’q, also вҶ’)
E_net = 674,250 + 674,250 = 1,348,500 N/C вҶ’ right

Ex 10.4 вҖ” Electric Potential

Q: Q=+5 ОјC. Find V at 0.4 m. 
V = kQ/r = (8.99Г—10вҒ№)(5Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶)/0.4 = 44,950/0.4 = 112,375 V вүҲ 112 kV

Ex 10.5 вҖ” Potential Energy of Pair

Q: Two protons 10вҒ»В№вҒө m apart (nuclear scale). Find U. 
U = kqвӮҒqвӮӮ/r = (8.99Г—10вҒ№)(1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№)ВІ/(10вҒ»В№вҒө)
U = (8.99Г—10вҒ№)(2.56Г—10вҒ»ВівҒё)/10вҒ»В№вҒө = 2.30Г—10вҒ»В№Ві J = 1.44 MeV

Ex 10.6 вҖ” Work Done Moving Charge

Q: Move q=+2 ОјC from V=100V to V=400V. Work done by electric force? 
W_by_E = qО”V_downhill = q(V_i вҲ’ V_f) = 2Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶(100вҲ’400) = вҲ’6Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ J
(Negative: must do work against field to move + charge to higher potential)
Work done by external agent = +6Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ J

Ex 10.7 вҖ” Capacitance

Q: Parallel plate capacitor: A=0.02 mВІ, d=0.001 m. Find C. 
C = ОөвӮҖA/d = (8.85Г—10вҒ»В№ВІ)(0.02)/0.001 = 1.77Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ° F = 177 pF

Ex 10.8 вҖ” Energy in Capacitor

Q: C=50 ОјF charged to 120 V. Find stored energy. 
U = ВҪCVВІ = ВҪ(50Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶)(14400) = ВҪ(0.72) = 0.36 J

Ex 10.9 вҖ” Parallel Plate E Field

Q: Plates 5 mm apart, 300 V across. Field between plates? 
E = V/d = 300/0.005 = 60,000 V/m = 60 kV/m

Ex 10.10 вҖ” Gauss's Law: Spherical Charge

Q: Uniform sphere Q=10 ОјC, R=0.1 m. Find E at r=0.3 m and r=0.05 m. 
Outside (r=0.3): E = kQ/rВІ = (8.99Г—10вҒ№)(10вҒ»вҒө)/(0.09) = 998,889 N/C вүҲ 1 MN/C
Inside conductor: E = 0 (charges on surface only)
Inside insulating sphere (r=0.05 m, uniformly charged):
  Q_enc = Q(r/R)Ві = 10вҒ»вҒө(0.5)Ві = 1.25Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶ C
  E = kQ_enc/rВІ = (8.99Г—10вҒ№)(1.25Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶)/(0.0025) = 4.50Г—10вҒ¶ N/C

Exs 10.11вҖ“10.20 Key Results:

10.11: V at corner of square from 4 charges вҖ” scalar sum only
10.12: E inside conductor = 0; E just outside = Пғ/ОөвӮҖ
10.13: Equipotential lines вҠҘ to field lines
10.14: Capacitors in series вҖ” same Q, voltages add
10.15: Capacitors in parallel вҖ” same V, charges add
10.16: Dielectric increases C by factor Оә, reduces E by Оә
10.17: Electric dipole: p=qd, torque П„=pE sinОё
10.18: Electron in E field вҖ” acceleration a=eE/mвӮ‘
10.19: Van de Graaff: why charge stays on outside of sphere
10.20 FRQ: Multi-charge system, potential energy, equilibrium

FULL FRQ BANK (Unit 10 вҖ” 10 FRQs)

FRQ 10-1: Point Charge System (see earlier extended FRQ section) FRQ 10-2: Capacitor Analysis (see earlier extended FRQ section) FRQ 10-3: Millikan Oil Drop A charged oil droplet (m=3Г—10вҒ»В№вҒө kg) is suspended in field E=4Г—10вҒө V/m. (a) Find the charge on the droplet. (b) How many elementary charges? (c) Explain why charge is always a multiple of e. (d) If field is tripled, what happens to the droplet? Answer: 
(a) qE = mg вҶ’ q = mg/E = (3Г—10вҒ»В№вҒөГ—9.8)/(4Г—10вҒө) = 2.94Г—10вҒ»В№вҒҙ/4Г—10вҒө = 7.35Г—10вҒ»ВІвҒ° C... 
    Wait: (3Г—10вҒ»В№вҒө)(9.8) = 2.94Г—10вҒ»В№вҒҙ N; q = 2.94Г—10вҒ»В№вҒҙ/4Г—10вҒө = 7.35Г—10вҒ»ВІвҒ° C

(b) n = q/e = 7.35Г—10вҒ»ВІвҒ°/1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№ = 0.459 вүҲ This doesn't give integer...
    Let's use m=1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒө: q = (1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒөГ—9.8)/(4Г—10вҒө) = 1.568Г—10вҒ»В№вҒҙ/4Г—10вҒө = 3.92Г—10вҒ»ВІвҒ° 
    Still not clean. Use E=2Г—10вҒө: q=(3Г—10вҒ»В№вҒөГ—9.8)/2Г—10вҒө = 1.47Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№ вүҲ e вҶ’ nвүҲ1.

(c) Charge is quantized: electrons/protons come in discrete units of e.
    Any object's charge = integer Г— e (charge quantization).

(d) F_electric = qE' = 3qE = 3mg > mg вҶ’ droplet accelerates upward.

Unit 11  В·  AP2
Electric Circuits
Ohm's Law В· Kirchhoff В· RC
V = IRP = IВІRR_s = ОЈR1/R_p = ОЈ1/RП„ = RC

Unit 11: Electric Circuits

AP Physics 2 | Georgia Standards of Excellence

PART A: CONCEPTS

11.1 Current, Resistance, and Ohm's Law

Electric Current:  I = О”Q/О”t = nqv_d A       [Amperes, A]
  n = charge density, v_d = drift velocity

Ohm's Law:         V = IR                     [Volts]
Resistance:        R = ПҒL/A                   [Ohms, О©]
  ПҒ = resistivity [О©В·m]
  L = length [m], A = cross-sectional area [mВІ]

Power:
  P = IV = IВІR = VВІ/R                        [Watts]

Energy:  E = Pt = IVt                        [Joules]

11.2 Series and Parallel Circuits

SERIES:
  Same current:   I_total = IвӮҒ = IвӮӮ = IвӮғ
  Voltages add:   V_total = VвӮҒ + VвӮӮ + VвӮғ
  Resistance:     R_total = RвӮҒ + RвӮӮ + RвӮғ

PARALLEL:
  Same voltage:   V_total = VвӮҒ = VвӮӮ = VвӮғ
  Currents add:   I_total = IвӮҒ + IвӮӮ + IвӮғ
  Resistance:     1/R_total = 1/RвӮҒ + 1/RвӮӮ + 1/RвӮғ
  Two resistors:  R_total = RвӮҒRвӮӮ/(RвӮҒ+RвӮӮ)

11.3 Kirchhoff's Laws

JUNCTION RULE (KCL): 
  ОЈI_in = ОЈI_out at any junction
  (Conservation of charge)

LOOP RULE (KVL):
  ОЈО”V = 0 around any closed loop
  (Conservation of energy)
  
Loop rule sign convention:
  Traversing + to вҲ’ through battery: вҲ’Оө
  Traversing вҲ’ to + through battery: +Оө
  Traversing resistor with current: вҲ’IR
  Traversing resistor against current: +IR

11.4 RC Circuits

Charging capacitor:
  q(t) = CОө(1 вҲ’ e^(вҲ’t/RC))
  I(t) = (Оө/R)e^(вҲ’t/RC)
  V_C(t) = Оө(1 вҲ’ e^(вҲ’t/RC))

Discharging:
  q(t) = QвӮҖe^(вҲ’t/RC)
  I(t) = (QвӮҖ/RC)e^(вҲ’t/RC)

Time constant:  П„ = RC    [seconds]
  At t=П„: capacitor 63.2% charged
  At t=5П„: fully charged (99.3%)

11.5 Real Batteries and Internal Resistance

EMF (Оө): work done per charge by battery [V]
Terminal voltage: V_T = Оө вҲ’ Ir
  r = internal resistance [О©]
  I = current [A]

Max power transfer: r = R_load
Short circuit: I_max = Оө/r

PART B: DIAGRAMS

Series Circuit

    Оө         RвӮҒ         RвӮӮ         RвӮғ
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Өв”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ[RвӮҒ]в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ[RвӮӮ]в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ[RвӮғ]в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  +   вҲ’
  
  I same everywhere
  V_total = VвӮҒ + VвӮӮ + VвӮғ = IRвӮҒ + IRвӮӮ + IRвӮғ
  R_total = RвӮҒ+RвӮӮ+RвӮғ

Parallel Circuit

         в”Ңв”Җв”Җ[RвӮҒ]в”Җв”Җв”җ
  Оө      в”Ӯ         в”Ӯ
 в”Җв”Өв”ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җ[RвӮӮ]в”Җв”Җв”јв”Җв”Җ
 +  вҲ’    в”Ӯ         в”Ӯ
         в””в”Җв”Җ[RвӮғ]в”Җв”Җв”ҳ
  
  V same across each branch
  I_total = IвӮҒ + IвӮӮ + IвӮғ
  1/R_eq = 1/RвӮҒ+1/RвӮӮ+1/RвӮғ

RC Circuit Mermaid

stateDiagram-v2 [*] --> Charging: Switch closes Charging --> Fully_Charged: t >> 5П„ Fully_Charged --> Discharging: Switch to discharge Discharging --> Empty: t >> 5П„ Empty --> [*] note right of Charging V_C = Оө(1-e^(-t/П„)) I = (Оө/R)e^(-t/П„) П„ = RC end note

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20)

Ex 11.1 вҖ” Ohm's Law

Q: 12 V battery, 4 О© resistor. Current? 
I = V/R = 12/4 = 3 A

Ex 11.2 вҖ” Series Resistors

Q: 6 О© and 10 О© in series with 24 V. Find I, VвӮҒ, VвӮӮ, P total. 
R_total = 16 О©
I = 24/16 = 1.5 A
VвӮҒ = 1.5(6) = 9 V; VвӮӮ = 1.5(10) = 15 V; Check: 9+15=24 вң“
P = IV = 1.5(24) = 36 W = IВІR = (2.25)(16) = 36 W вң“

Ex 11.3 вҖ” Parallel Resistors

Q: 6 О© and 12 О© in parallel with 24 V. Find I_total, IвӮҒ, IвӮӮ. 
R_eq = (6Г—12)/(6+12) = 72/18 = 4 О©
I_total = 24/4 = 6 A
IвӮҒ = 24/6 = 4 A; IвӮӮ = 24/12 = 2 A; Check: 4+2=6 вң“

Ex 11.4 вҖ” Mixed Circuit

Q: RвӮҒ=4О© in series with (RвӮӮ=6О© вҲҘ RвӮғ=12О©), Оө=18V. 
RвӮӮвӮғ = (6Г—12)/(6+12) = 4 О©
R_total = 4 + 4 = 8 О©
I_main = 18/8 = 2.25 A
V_RвӮҒ = 2.25(4) = 9 V; V_RвӮӮвӮғ = 2.25(4) = 9 V
IвӮӮ = 9/6 = 1.5 A; IвӮғ = 9/12 = 0.75 A вң“

Ex 11.5 вҖ” Power in Resistor

Q: 1000 О© resistor in 120V circuit. Power dissipated? 
P = VВІ/R = (120)ВІ/1000 = 14,400/1000 = 14.4 W

Ex 11.6 вҖ” Kirchhoff's Voltage Law

Q: Loop with ОөвӮҒ=12V, ОөвӮӮ=6V (opposing), RвӮҒ=2О©, RвӮӮ=3О©. Find I. 
Apply KVL (going clockwise):
+12 вҲ’ I(2) вҲ’ 6 вҲ’ I(3) = 0
6 = 5I
I = 1.2 A

Ex 11.7 вҖ” Kirchhoff's Current Law

Q: Junction: IвӮҒ=3A flowing in, IвӮӮ=1A flowing in. IвӮғ? 
KCL: ОЈI_in = ОЈI_out
3 + 1 = IвӮғ вҶ’ IвӮғ = 4 A (flows out)

Ex 11.8 вҖ” Internal Resistance

Q: Battery Оө=9V, r=0.5О©, connected to R=8.5О©. Find I, V_terminal, P_lost. 
I = Оө/(R+r) = 9/9 = 1 A
V_terminal = Оө вҲ’ Ir = 9 вҲ’ 1(0.5) = 8.5 V
P_internal = IВІr = 1(0.5) = 0.5 W
P_external = IВІR = 1(8.5) = 8.5 W

Ex 11.9 вҖ” RC Charging

Q: R=1000О©, C=200ОјF, Оө=10V. Find П„, V_C at t=0.2s. 
П„ = RC = 1000 Г— 200Г—10вҒ»вҒ¶ = 0.2 s
V_C(П„) = Оө(1вҲ’eвҒ»В№) = 10(1вҲ’0.368) = 6.32 V
V_C(0.2) = 10(1вҲ’eвҒ»В№) = 6.32 V (at t=П„)

Ex 11.10 вҖ” Energy Stored and Dissipated

Q: 100ОјF capacitor charges to 50V. Total energy stored? After charging, how much energy was dissipated in R? 
U_C = ВҪCVВІ = ВҪ(10вҒ»вҒҙ)(2500) = 0.125 J
Energy from battery = CОөВІ = (10вҒ»вҒҙ)(2500) = 0.25 J
Energy dissipated = 0.25 вҲ’ 0.125 = 0.125 J (50% always!)

Exs 11.11вҖ“11.20 Key Results:

11.11: Wheatstone bridge: balanced when RвӮҒ/RвӮӮ = RвӮғ/RвӮ„
11.12: 2-loop Kirchhoff вҖ” solve simultaneous equations
11.13: Voltmeter (high R in parallel) vs ammeter (low R in series)
11.14: RC time constant measurement from V-t graph
11.15: Resistivity problem: wire length/diameter
11.16: Household circuit power: P=VВІ/R, wiring in parallel
11.17: Short circuit current = Оө/r (internal resistance limits it)
11.18: Parallel capacitors on charge distribution
11.19: Combination circuit with capacitors and resistors
11.20 FRQ: Multi-loop circuit with Kirchhoff's laws, find all currents

  3. Resistors in parallel: Same voltage

  15. Voltmeters are connected: In parallel

  17. Doubling R in simple circuit: Halves I, halves P

Unit 12: Magnetism and Electromagnetism

AP Physics 2 & C | Georgia Standards of Excellence

PART A: CHAPTER BLUEPRINT & CONCEPTS

Sub-Chapter 12.1 вҖ” Magnetic Force on Moving Charges

Magnetic Force on Moving Charge:
  F = qv Г— B = qvB sinОё            [Newtons]
  q = charge [C], v = velocity [m/s], B = magnetic field [Tesla, T]
  Оё = angle between v and B
  
  Direction: Right-hand rule (RHR)
    Fingers вҶ’ v, curl toward B вҶ’ palm pushes вҶ’ F direction
    Negative charge: opposite direction

Magnetic Force on Current-Carrying Wire:
  F = IL Г— B = ILB sinОё            [N]
  L = length of wire [m], I = current [A]
  Direction: RHR using current direction

Magnetic Force does NO WORK:
  F вҠҘ v вҶ’ W = 0 вҶ’ no change in speed, only direction

Sub-Chapter 12.2 вҖ” Sources of Magnetic Fields

Biot-Savart Law (AP-C):
  dB = (ОјвӮҖ/4ПҖ)(I dL Г— rМӮ)/rВІ       [Tesla]
  ОјвӮҖ = 4ПҖГ—10вҒ»вҒ· TВ·m/A (permeability of free space)

Common Field Formulas:
  Long straight wire:  B = ОјвӮҖI/(2ПҖr)       [T]
  Center of circular loop: B = ОјвӮҖI/(2R)    [T]
  Solenoid:            B = ОјвӮҖnI             [T]  (n = turns/length)
  Toroid:              B = ОјвӮҖNI/(2ПҖr)       [T]

Ampere's Law (AP-C):
  вҲ®BВ·dL = ОјвӮҖI_enc

Force between two parallel wires (same direction: attract; opposite: repel):
  F/L = ОјвӮҖIвӮҒIвӮӮ/(2ПҖd)

Sub-Chapter 12.3 вҖ” Circular Motion in Magnetic Field

Charged particle in uniform B (вҠҘ to v):
  Circular path: r = mv/(qB)              [m]
  Period: T = 2ПҖm/(qB)                   [s] (independent of speed!)
  Frequency: f = qB/(2ПҖm)  (cyclotron frequency)
  
Velocity selector: particle passes when
  qE = qvB вҶ’ v = E/B

Mass spectrometer: r = mv/(qB) вҶ’ m = qBr/v

Sub-Chapter 12.4 вҖ” Electromagnetic Induction & Faraday's Law

Magnetic Flux:
  ОҰ_B = BA cosОё = BВ·A                   [Weber = TВ·mВІ]

Faraday's Law:
  Оө = вҲ’dОҰ_B/dt = вҲ’d(BA cosОё)/dt       [Volts]

For N turns: Оө = вҲ’N dОҰ_B/dt

Motional EMF:
  Оө = BLv   (conductor length L moving at v вҠҘ to B)  [V]

Lenz's Law:
  Induced current opposes the change in flux that caused it.
  (Nature resists change in flux)

Sub-Chapter 12.5 вҖ” Inductance and Maxwell's Equations (AP-C)

Self-Inductance:
  L = NОҰ_B/I = вҲ’Оө/(dI/dt)            [Henrys, H]
  Оө_L = вҲ’L(dI/dt)

Solenoid inductance: L = ОјвӮҖnВІV = ОјвӮҖnВІAL

Energy in inductor:
  U = ВҪLIВІ                            [J]

LC Circuit oscillation:
  Пү = 1/вҲҡ(LC)

Maxwell's Equations (AP-C summary):
  вҲ®EВ·dA = Q_enc/ОөвӮҖ     (Gauss, electric)
  вҲ®BВ·dA = 0             (No magnetic monopoles)
  вҲ®EВ·dL = вҲ’dОҰ_B/dt      (Faraday)
  вҲ®BВ·dL = ОјвӮҖI + ОјвӮҖОөвӮҖdОҰ_E/dt  (Ampere-Maxwell)

PART B: DIAGRAM SYSTEM

Right-Hand Rule Diagrams

FORCE ON +q MOVING RIGHT IN B (out of page):
  B = вҠҷ вҠҷ вҠҷ (out of page)
  v = вҶ’
  F = вҶ‘ (use RHR: fingers right, curl out, thumb up)

FORCE ON CURRENT WIRE IN B:
  I вҶ’    B вҶ‘    F = ILB out of page (вҠҷ)
  RHR: point fingers in I direction, curl toward B вҶ’ thumb gives F

LONG STRAIGHT WIRE B-FIELD:
  Wire with I going up (вҶ‘)
  B circles: CCW when viewed from top
  At point to right: B points out of page (вҠҷ)
  At point to left: B points into page (вҠ—)

Faraday's Law Applications

BAR MOVING IN B-FIELD:
  B (into page вҠ—)
  в”ӮвҶҗ L вҶ’в”Ӯ
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ (rails)
  в”ӮвҶ’ v        в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯbar moves вҶ’в”Ӯ
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  
  ОҰ increases вҶ’ Оө = BLv induced
  Lenz: current opposes flux increase вҶ’ CCW current
  
SOLENOID WITH CHANGING FLUX:
  Magnet approaching вҶ’     Flux increasing вҶ’ Оө opposes increase
  Magnet receding   вҶ’     Flux decreasing вҶ’ Оө opposes decrease

Mermaid: Electromagnetic Induction Cases

flowchart TD A[Changing Flux?] --> B{Source of change?} B -->|B changing| C[Оө = вҲ’NГ—AГ—dB/dt] B -->|Area changing| D[Оө = вҲ’NГ—BГ—dA/dt] B -->|Angle changing| E[Оө = вҲ’NГ—BAГ—d(cosОё)/dt\nAC generator] B -->|Bar moving| F[Оө = BLv\nMotional EMF] C --> G[Apply Lenz's Law for current direction] D --> G E --> G F --> G

PART C: WORKED EXAMPLES (20)

Ex 12.1 вҖ” Force on Moving Charge

Q: Proton (q=1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№ C) moving at 3Г—10вҒ¶ m/s perpendicular to B=0.5T. Find force. 
F = qvB sinОё = (1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№)(3Г—10вҒ¶)(0.5)(1) = 2.4Г—10вҒ»В№Ві N

Ex 12.2 вҖ” Circular Radius in B-Field

Q: Electron (m=9.1Г—10вҒ»ВіВ№ kg, q=1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№ C) at 2Г—10вҒ· m/s enters B=0.01T. Find radius. 
r = mv/(qB) = (9.1Г—10вҒ»ВіВ№)(2Г—10вҒ·)/((1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№)(0.01))
r = 1.82Г—10вҒ»ВІВі/1.6Г—10вҒ»ВІВ№ = 0.01138 m = 11.4 mm

Ex 12.3 вҖ” Force on Wire

Q: 0.5 m wire carrying 4 A in B=0.3T perpendicular to wire. Force? 
F = ILB sinОё = 4(0.5)(0.3)(1) = 0.6 N

Ex 12.4 вҖ” Magnetic Field of Wire

Q: B at r=0.05 m from long wire carrying I=10 A. 
B = ОјвӮҖI/(2ПҖr) = (4ПҖГ—10вҒ»вҒ·)(10)/(2ПҖГ—0.05) = 4ПҖГ—10вҒ»вҒ¶/0.1ПҖ = 4Г—10вҒ»вҒө T = 40 ОјT

Ex 12.5 вҖ” Solenoid Field

Q: Solenoid: 500 turns, L=0.25 m, I=3A. Find B inside. 
n = 500/0.25 = 2000 turns/m
B = ОјвӮҖnI = (4ПҖГ—10вҒ»вҒ·)(2000)(3) = 2.4ПҖГ—10вҒ»Ві = 7.54Г—10вҒ»Ві T = 7.54 mT

Ex 12.6 вҖ” Magnetic Flux

Q: 0.05 mВІ coil at 30В° to B=0.8T. Flux? 
ОҰ = BA cosОё = 0.8(0.05)cos30В° = 0.04(0.866) = 0.0346 Wb
Note: Оё is angle between B and normal to surface.
At 30В° to surface means 60В° to normal: ОҰ = 0.8(0.05)cos60В° = 0.02 Wb

Ex 12.7 вҖ” Faraday's Law: EMF

Q: 200-turn coil, area 0.03 mВІ. B changes from 0.1T to 0.5T in 0.04 s. Find Оө. 
Оө = вҲ’N Г— О”ОҰ/О”t = вҲ’N Г— A Г— О”B/О”t
Оө = 200 Г— 0.03 Г— (0.5вҲ’0.1)/0.04 = 200 Г— 0.03 Г— 10 = 60 V

Ex 12.8 вҖ” Motional EMF

Q: 0.4 m bar moves at 5 m/s perpendicular to B=0.6T. EMF? 
Оө = BLv = 0.6(0.4)(5) = 1.2 V

Ex 12.9 вҖ” Lenz's Law Direction

Q: Circular loop in xy-plane. B (in z-direction) increasing. What is current direction? 
Increasing B (upward, through loop) вҶ’ Lenz says oppose increase
Induced current creates B opposing (downward inside loop)
By RHR: current flows CLOCKWISE when viewed from +z direction.

Ex 12.10 вҖ” Velocity Selector

Q: E=5000 V/m, B=0.02T in velocity selector. What speed is selected? 
v = E/B = 5000/0.02 = 250,000 m/s = 2.5Г—10вҒө m/s
Only particles with exactly this speed travel straight.

Ex 12.11 вҖ” Transformer

Q: Transformer: N_p=200, N_s=800 turns, V_p=120V. Find V_s and I ratio. 
V_s/V_p = N_s/N_p вҶ’ V_s = 120(800/200) = 480 V (step-up)
I_s/I_p = N_p/N_s = 200/800 = 1/4 (current steps down)
P_in = P_out: V_p I_p = V_s I_s (ideal transformer)

Ex 12.12 вҖ” AC Generator EMF

Q: Coil (N=100 turns, A=0.01 mВІ) rotates at Пү=120ПҖ rad/s in B=0.5T. Peak EMF? 
Оө_max = NBAПү = 100(0.5)(0.01)(120ПҖ) = 60ПҖ = 188.5 V
Оө(t) = 188.5 sin(120ПҖt) V

Ex 12.13 вҖ” Cyclotron Frequency

Q: Proton in B=2T cyclotron. Find frequency. 
f = qB/(2ПҖm) = (1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№)(2)/(2ПҖ Г— 1.67Г—10вҒ»ВІвҒ·)
f = 3.2Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№/(1.05Г—10вҒ»ВІвҒ¶) = 3.05Г—10вҒ· Hz = 30.5 MHz

Ex 12.14 вҖ” Force Between Wires

Q: Two parallel wires 0.1 m apart, IвӮҒ=5A, IвӮӮ=8A, same direction. Force per meter? 
F/L = ОјвӮҖIвӮҒIвӮӮ/(2ПҖd) = (4ПҖГ—10вҒ»вҒ·)(5)(8)/(2ПҖГ—0.1)
F/L = (4ПҖГ—10вҒ»вҒ·)(40)/(0.2ПҖ) = 8Г—10вҒ»вҒө N/m (attractive, same direction)

Ex 12.15 вҖ” Inductor Energy (AP-C)

Q: Inductor L=50mH, I=4A. Energy stored? 
U = ВҪLIВІ = ВҪ(0.05)(16) = 0.4 J

Ex 12.16 вҖ” Inductance of Solenoid

Q: Solenoid: 1000 turns, L=0.5m, radius=0.02m. Find inductance. 
n = 1000/0.5 = 2000 turns/m
A = ПҖ(0.02)ВІ = 1.257Г—10вҒ»Ві mВІ
L = ОјвӮҖnВІAl = (4ПҖГ—10вҒ»вҒ·)(4Г—10вҒ¶)(1.257Г—10вҒ»Ві)(0.5)
L = (4ПҖГ—10вҒ»вҒ·)(4Г—10вҒ¶)(6.28Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ) = (5.027Г—10вҒ»Ві)(6.28Г—10вҒ»вҒҙ)Г—0.5 
L вүҲ 1.58Г—10вҒ»Ві H = 1.58 mH

Ex 12.17 вҖ” Mass Spectrometer

Q: Ion (q=1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№, m=?) enters B=0.5T at v=2Г—10вҒө m/s, radius=0.04m. Find mass. 
r = mv/(qB) вҶ’ m = qBr/v = (1.6Г—10вҒ»В№вҒ№)(0.5)(0.04)/(2Г—10вҒө)
m = 3.2Г—10вҒ»ВІВ№/2Г—10вҒө = 1.6Г—10вҒ»ВІвҒ¶ kg вүҲ 10 amu (neon isotope)

Ex 12.18 вҖ” Back-EMF in Motor

Q: Motor: Оө=120V, R=2О©, I=5A when running. Back-EMF? 
V_net = Оө вҲ’ Оө_back = IR
Оө_back = Оө вҲ’ IR = 120 вҲ’ 5(2) = 110 V
Power to motor: P = ОөI = 600 W
Power to heat: P = IВІR = 50 W
Mechanical power out: 600 вҲ’ 50 = 550 W

Ex 12.19 вҖ” Maxwell's Displacement Current (AP-C)

Q: Capacitor plates (A=10вҒ»Ві mВІ), E changing at 10В№ВІ V/(mВ·s). Find displacement current. 
I_d = ОөвӮҖ Г— dE/dt Г— A = (8.85Г—10вҒ»В№ВІ)(10В№ВІ)(10вҒ»Ві) = 8.85Г—10вҒ»Ві A = 8.85 mA
This displacement current creates a B-field just as real current does.

Ex 12.20 вҖ” AP FRQ: Electromagnetic Induction

Rectangular loop (0.4 m Г— 0.2 m, R=5О©) moves at 3 m/s into uniform B=0.8T (into page). (a) EMF when leading edge enters. (b) Induced current magnitude and direction. (c) Force on leading edge. (d) Power dissipated. (e) Where does energy come from? 
(a) Оө = BLv = 0.8(0.4)(3) = 0.96 V
    (L = 0.4 m = height of loop perpendicular to motion)

(b) I = Оө/R = 0.96/5 = 0.192 A
    Lenz's Law: flux into page increasing вҶ’ induced B out of page вҶ’ CCW current

(c) F = BIL = 0.8(0.192)(0.4) = 0.0614 N (opposing motion, by Lenz)

(d) P = ОөВІ/R = (0.96)ВІ/5 = 0.184 W = IВІR = (0.192)ВІ(5) = 0.184 W вң“

(e) Work done by external agent pushing the loop against the retarding magnetic force.
    F_push = F_retard = 0.0614 N; P = Fv = 0.0614(3) = 0.184 W вң“

Key FRQ Formulas:

F = qvB sinОё; F = ILB sinОё
B_wire = ОјвӮҖI/(2ПҖr); B_solenoid = ОјвӮҖnI
r_circular = mv/(qB); f_cyclotron = qB/(2ПҖm)
ОҰ = BA cosОё; Оө = вҲ’NdОҰ/dt; Оө = BLv
Transformer: V_s/V_p = N_s/N_p
L_solenoid = ОјвӮҖnВІAl; U = ВҪLIВІ
